## DM Guidance Notes

### **Quest 1.1 Design Philosophy**

This quest teaches players the core themes of Blood & Coin:

1. **Clients Lie** - Every single contract has hidden truth
2. **No Clear Morality** - Every choice has pros and cons
3. **Consequences Matter** - Choices establish reputation
4. **Pragmatism vs Idealism** - Both are valid, both have costs
5. **Money Matters** - Gold differences actually mean something

### **Adapting to Player Choices**

The key to running this quest well is **not judging player choices**. The DM should:

âœ… Present situations neutrally  
âœ… Show consequences (not punishments)  
âœ… Let PCs feel the weight of choices  
âœ… Respect different moral frameworks  
âœ… Track reputation changes for later use  

âŒ Don't moralize at the table  
âŒ Don't punish "evil" choices mechanically  
âŒ Don't reward "good" choices artificially  
âŒ Don't railroad toward specific outcome  

### **Pacing Notes**

**Session 1:**
- Character introductions (30 min)
- Arrival at Crossroads (15 min)
- Meeting Finn and Mira (30 min)
- Meeting Varak, choosing contract (45 min)

**Session 2:**
- Complete chosen contract (2-3 hours)
- Return to Varak, get membership
- Brief downtime, meet more NPCs
- Hook for Quest 1.2

### **Difficulty Adjustments**

**If Party Struggles:**
- Reduce rat count to 5-6
- Give Thomas 50gp in goods he can pay with
- Have officers be less competent fighters

**If Party Dominates:**
- Add 2-3 more rats
- Have Vareth demand more aggressive collection
- Add 2 more officers to road stop

### **Branching Consequences**

Track these for later quests:

**Reputation Types:**
- Ruthless (brutal methods)
- Merciful (showed compassion)
- Pragmatic (chose middle path)
- Law-Abiding (sided with authorities)
- Outlaw (opposed law)
- Opportunistic (maximized profit)

**Ally/Enemy Status:**
- Oleg Tharn (ally/enemy)
- Cassia Valen (ally/enemy)
- Thomas Redhill (grateful/dead/unaware)
- Vareth Goldtooth (satisfied/suspicious)
- Thaldros Officers (neutral/hostile)

These will come back in Acts II and III!

---

**Quest 1.1 Complete - Ready for DM Use**

This quest alone is ~8,000 words of fully playable content. PCs will spend 1-2 sessions on it and learn everything they need to know about the campaign's tone.

---

## ðŸŽ¯ Quest 1.2: The PRICE OF LOYALTY

**Level:** 2  
**Duration:** 2-3 sessions  
**Objective:** Choose between competing clients with opposite goals  
**Key NPCs:** Baron Darius Thornhill, Thomas Redwood, Elara Thornhill  
**Rewards:** 150-200gp (varies), permanent enemy made, lasting consequences  
**Theme:** "You can't serve two masters"

### **Quest SETUP**

After 1-2 days of downtime following Quest 1.1, Varak summons the PCs to the guild hall. This time, things are differentâ€”there's tension in the air.

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*You arrive at the guild hall to find it more crowded than usual. Two groups of mercenaries eye each other warily from opposite sides of the room. Hands rest on weapon hilts. The air crackles with potential violence.*
>
{{descriptive
*Varak sits at his desk, jaw clenched, clearly irritated. Two men stand before him, both talking at once:*
>
{{descriptive
*On the left: A nobleman in expensive clothing, mid-40s, imperious bearing, hand on his sword. His voice is commanding, entitled: "I offered first! The contract is MINE!"*
>
{{descriptive
*On the right: A younger man in merchant's clothing, nervous but determined, clutching a heavy coin purse: "I'm offering more gold! That's how this works!"*
>
{{descriptive
*Varak slams his fist on the desk. Silence falls.*
>
{{descriptive
*"Enough. You both want mercenaries for the same target. Same woman. Different reasons. I don't care about your family dramaâ€”this is business. The guild doesn't take sides in personal disputes."*
>
{{descriptive
*He turns to you.*
>
{{descriptive
*"Two clients. Same target. Opposite goals. One wants her brought back. One wants her protected. Choose one contract. The other will hire someone elseâ€”probably to fight you. This is the business we're in. Choose wisely."*

### **The Competing Clients**

Both clients present their case. Let them argue, interrupt each other, appeal to the PCs. This should feel chaotic, uncomfortable, real.

---

### **Client A: Baron Darius Thornhill**

**NPC: Baron Darius Thornhill**

*Medium humanoid (human), lawful neutral (thinks he's lawful good)*

**Appearance:** Mid-40s, graying temples, expensive noble clothing, ornate longsword, military bearing, entitled but not cruel

**Personality:**
- Authoritarian father who "knows what's best"
- Genuinely loves his daughter (in his way)
- Views commoners as beneath his family
- Not evil, just classist and controlling
- Believes he's protecting his daughter

**Stats:** Use **Noble** with combat training (+2 longsword, 30 HP)

**Baron's Pitch:**

{{descriptive
*"My daughter, Elara, has been kidnappedâ€”no, seducedâ€”by a common merchant. A nobody. Thomas Redwood. He's filled her head with romantic nonsense about 'true love' and 'freedom.' She's nineteen, naive, doesn't understand the world.*
>
{{descriptive
*Three weeks ago, she disappeared. Left a note saying she was 'following her heart.' I have it on good authority she's hiding in a cottage five miles north with this... boy. He's probably using her for her family's money and connections.*
>
{{descriptive
*Your job: Retrieve my daughter. Bring her home. Unharmed. I don't care about the boyâ€”kill him, let him go, whatever. Just bring Elara back. She belongs with her family.*
>
{{descriptive
*Payment: 200 gold pieces. Plus, I'll owe you a favorâ€”a noble's favor is worth more than gold in this kingdom."*

**If PCs ask questions:**

**"Why do you think she was kidnapped?":** *"Because she would never leave willingly. She knows her duty to the family. He must have enchanted her somehowâ€”magic or manipulation, doesn't matter."*

**"What if she wants to stay with him?":** *"She's nineteen. She doesn't know what she wants. I'm her father. It's my duty to protect her from her own foolishness. She'll thank me when she's older."*

**"Will you hurt the merchant?":** *"If he resists? Yes. If he's smart enough to walk away? No. I'm not a monster. But if he's harmed my daughter in any way, I'll have him executed. Legally."*

**"What about Elara's wishes?":** *"She's a child. Children don't get to make adult decisions. This isn't about what she wantsâ€”it's about what's right. What's safe. What's proper."*

**Insight DC 14:** The Baron genuinely believes he's protecting his daughter. He loves her, but in a controlling, possessive way. He sees Thomas as a threat, not because he's evil, but because he's "inappropriate."

---

### **Client B: THOMAS REDWOOD**

**NPC: Thomas Redwood** (not the same Thomas from Quest 1.1)

*Medium humanoid (human), neutral good*

**Appearance:** Early 20s, merchant's son, clean-cut, earnest, scared but determined, wearing simple but quality clothing, obviously in love

**Personality:**
- Genuinely loves Elara
- Not fortune hunter (his family is modestly wealthy)
- Idealistic but practical
- Willing to fight for love but prefers peace
- Fears the Baron but won't abandon Elara

**Stats:** Use **Commoner** with +2 Persuasion, +3 Insight (22 HP from determination)

**Thomas's Pitch:**

{{descriptive
*"Please, hear me out. The Baron is lyingâ€”or deluded. Elara wasn't kidnapped. She chose to leave. She chose me. We're in love. We want to marry.*
>
{{descriptive
*But her father won't allow it because I'm a merchant's son, not nobility. As if love cares about bloodlines! We ran away three weeks ago because he threatened to marry her off to some old duke for political alliance.*
>
{{descriptive
*She's not a childâ€”she's nineteen, an adult. This is her choice. But I know the Baron. He'll send mercenaries. He'll send assassins. He'll never stop until he gets her back.*
>
{{descriptive
*I'm offering 150 goldâ€”everything I have savedâ€”to protect us. To protect her. Just for a few weeks until we can reach the free territories where the Baron has no legal authority. Then we can start a new life.*
>
{{descriptive
*Please. Don't let him take her back. She'll be trapped in a gilded cage for the rest of her life."*

**If PCs ask questions:**

**"How do we know she really loves you?":** *"Talk to her yourself. She's at the cottage. She'll tell you. She chose this. She chose me."*

**"Why not just explain this to her father?":** *"We tried. He refused to listen. He called me a gold-digger, said I'd enchanted her. He had his guards beat me and throw me out. That's when we ran."*

**"What if the Baron attacks?":** *"That's why I need you. I can't fight trained soldiers. I'm a merchant, not a warrior. But I won't let her go back. I'd rather die."*

**"What about her family? Won't she miss them?":** *(Pained)* *"Yes. She misses her mother. But her father is a tyrant. He's never let her make her own choices. This is her first real decisionâ€”and it's to choose love over duty."*

**Insight DC 12:** Thomas is telling the truth. He's genuinely in love. He's not after moneyâ€”his own family is comfortable. He's terrified but determined.

---

### **The Decision Moment**

Varak interrupts:

{{descriptive
*"Enough. I've heard both sides. You're both paying customers. The guild doesn't judge moralityâ€”we judge contracts. Both are legitimate.*
>
{{descriptive
*Here's how this works: The mercenaries choose one contract. The other client leaves and finds different mercenaries. Then you'll probably end up fighting each other over this girl. That's the business."*
>
{{descriptive
*He looks at you.*
>
{{descriptive
*"So. Baron offers 200 gold and a noble's favor. Merchant offers 150 gold and gratitude. Baron wants girl brought back. Merchant wants her protected. Choose. Now."*

**Important:** Give players time to discuss. This is a major choice. Let them debate. Some might want the money. Others might care about morality. Some might try to negotiate (won't workâ€”both clients are stubborn).

### **The CHOICE**

**Option 1: Accept Baron's Contract**
- Work for the noble
- Higher pay (200gp + favor)
- Orders: Retrieve Elara, don't harm her, merchant is irrelevant
- Thomas hires rival mercenaries (3 level 2 fighters) to protect them

**Option 2: Accept Thomas's Contract**  
- Work for the lovers
- Lower pay (150gp) but morally clearer
- Orders: Protect Elara and Thomas from Baron's mercenaries
- Baron hires rival mercenaries (4 level 2 fighters) to retrieve Elara

**Option 3: Refuse Both**
- Walk away, no payment
- Both clients hire other mercenaries
- PCs stay out of it
- **Consequence:** Varak respects neutrality but warns you'll make enemies either way by not choosing

**Option 4: Try to Mediate** (Persuasion DC 20, very hard)
- Attempt to broker peace between father and daughter
- If successful: Baron agrees to meet with Elara one time, no guards
- If failed: Both clients think you're wasting their time, both hire other mercenaries
- If mediation works (rare), both pay half (175gp combined), no one fights

### **Investigating The Truth**

Smart players might want to verify claims before choosing.

**Option: Visit the Cottage First**

Both clients agree (reluctantly) to let PCs investigate before deciding.

**the cottage**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*The cottage is small but well-kept, five miles north of Crossroads. Smoke rises from the chimney. Flowers grow in window boxesâ€”someone planted them recently. A young woman tends a small garden out front, humming to herself. She looks up as you approach.*
>
{{descriptive
*She's prettyâ€”dark hair, nobleman's features, but dressed in simple peasant clothing. Her hands are dirty from gardening. She looks... happy. Content. Free.*
>
{{descriptive
*She sees you. Her hand goes to her beltâ€”a small knife. Her expression hardens.*
>
{{descriptive
*"More mercenaries? Did my father send you? Tell him I'm not going back."*

**NPC: Elara Thornhill**

*Medium humanoid (human), neutral good*

**Appearance:** 19 years old, dark hair, nobleman's features, simple clothing, sun-tanned (new for her), calloused hands from work, defiant eyes

**Personality:**
- Strong-willed, not naive
- Knows what she wants
- Loves her mother but resents her father
- Has thought this through carefully
- Not being controlled or enchantedâ€”this is her choice

**Stats:** Use **Commoner** (4 HP), will not fight but will run

**Elara's Truth:**

If PCs talk to her peacefully:

{{descriptive
*"Let me guessâ€”my father told you I was kidnapped? Enchanted? That I'm a silly girl who doesn't know her own mind?*
>
{{descriptive
*I'm nineteen. I'm an adult. I know exactly what I'm doing. I love Thomas. He loves me. We want to build a life together. But my father sees me as propertyâ€”a trading piece for political alliances.*
>
{{descriptive
*He was arranging my marriage to Duke Harmond. The man is forty-five years old. He's buried two wives already. My father didn't ask my opinionâ€”he just told me it was 'decided.'*
>
{{descriptive
*So yes, I left. I chose Thomas. I chose freedom. I chose love over duty. And I'm not going back.*
>
{{descriptive
*If you're here to drag me back... you'll have to tie me up and carry me. I won't go willingly. And I'll hate every mercenary who helps my father cage me again."*

**Insight DC 10:** She's telling the truth. She's not enchanted, not manipulated. This is genuine choice.

**If PCs ask about Thomas:**

*"Thomas is kind. He's gentle. He's the first person who ever asked what I wanted instead of telling me. His family is wealthy enoughâ€”he's not after my father's gold. He wants me. Just me. That's enough."*

**If PCs ask about her mother:**

*"I miss her. Gods, I miss her. But she won't stand up to father. She never has. She told me once, 'Sometimes we sacrifice freedom for security.' I refuse to make that trade."*

**If PCs mention Duke Harmond:**

*"He's not evil. Just... old. Boring. Entitled. He views me as decorationâ€”a young wife to produce heirs. That's my entire value to these men. My father sees a political alliance. Harmond sees a breeding mare. Only Thomas sees Elara."*

### **The Truth Revealed**

After investigating, players should understand:

âœ… Elara was NOT kidnapped  
âœ… She chose to leave willingly  
âœ… Thomas is genuinely in love, not a con artist  
âœ… Baron is controlling but loves his daughter (in his way)  
âœ… This is about freedom vs. family duty  
âœ… No clear villainâ€”just opposing values

**Now players must choose despite having all the facts.**

---

## Branching Paths

### **Path A: Working For The Baron**

If PCs accept Baron's contract:

**Phase 1: The Approach**

Baron provides:
- Map to cottage
- Description of Elara
- 100gp upfront, 100gp on delivery
- Orders: "Bring her back alive. Unharmed. Use force only if necessary."

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*You approach the cottage at dusk. As expected, Thomas Redwood is outside, chopping firewood. He sees you coming. His face falls. He knows why you're here.*
>
{{descriptive
*He drops the axe and sprints inside, shouting: "Elara! They're here! The Baron sent them!"*
>
{{descriptive
*Moments later, Elara appears in the doorway. Behind her, three armed figures emerge from the cottageâ€”mercenaries. Thomas hired protection.*
>
{{descriptive
*One of them, a scarred woman with a crossbow, calls out: "You're trespassing. Leave now or we make you leave."*

**Encounter:** 3 **Rival Mercenaries** (Thomas's hired guards)

- 1 **Fighter** (Female leader, CR 1) - Uses Longsword, shield
- 2 **Thugs** (Male guards, CR 1/2 each) - Use clubs, pack tactics

**Tactics:**
- Mercenaries defend the cottage, don't pursue
- Leader shouts: "We don't want to fight! Just leave them alone!"
- If PCs attack, they defend but try for non-lethal (don't want murder charges)
- If leader drops below 10 HP, she calls retreat
- Thomas and Elara barricade inside cottage during fight

**Non-Combat Options:**

**Option: Negotiation** (Persuasion DC 16)
- Offer rival mercenaries MORE money to walk away (requires 100gp bribe)
- Success: They leave, apologize to Thomas, "business is business"
- Failure: They refuse, see PCs as dishonorable

**Option: Intimidation** (DC 15)
- Threaten rivals with guild backing or superior numbers
- Success: They back down, leave angry
- Failure: They attack out of pride

**Option: Deception** (DC 17)
- Lie about Baron's intentions ("He just wants to talk!")
- Success: Rivals lower guard, can be surprised or convinced to mediate
- Failure: They attack, angry at deception

**Phase 2: Elara's Resistance**

Once rivals are dealt with (fought, bribed, or convinced), face Elara:

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*The cottage door opens. Elara stands there, knife in handâ€”useless against armed mercenaries, but she's not going quietly. Thomas stands behind her, protective but helpless.*
>
{{descriptive
*"So you chose him," Elara says bitterly. "You chose gold over doing the right thing. Typical. My father knew exactly what mercenaries to hire."*
>
{{descriptive
*She raises the knifeâ€”not to attack, but to her own throat.*
>
{{descriptive
*"I won't go back. I'd rather die free than live in a cage. You'll have to bring him my corpse. Tell him I loved him, but I loved freedom more."*

**The Hostage Situation:**

**Option 1: Call Her Bluff** (Insight DC 15 to see if she's serious)
- If she's bluffing: She lowers knife, breaks down crying, gives up
- If she's serious: She cuts herself (1d4 damage), demands you leave
- **DM Note:** She IS serious. This is her last stand.

**Option 2: Disarm Her** (Athletics or Acrobatics DC 14, opposed check)
- Success: Grab the knife, restrain her
- Failure: She cuts herself (1d6 damage), screams for Thomas

**Option 3: Convince Her** (Persuasion DC 18, very hard)
- Argue that Baron loves her, will listen, she can negotiate terms
- Success: She agrees to meet father with YOU as mediators
- Failure: She refuses, threatens self-harm

**Option 4: Knock Her Out** (Non-lethal attack)
- Hit her unconscious, tie her up
- Thomas attacks you (futilely, easily subdued)
- **Consequence:** Most brutal option, but "completes" contract

**Option 5: Walk Away**
- Refuse to force her
- Return to Baron, report she'd rather die
- Baron is furious, refuses payment, hires assassins to target Thomas
- **Consequence:** Contract broken, reputation hit, but conscience clear

**Phase 3: The Return**

If you successfully retrieve Elara (willing or not):

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Baron Thornhill waits at the guild hall. When you bring Elara through the door, his face floods with reliefâ€”then hardens when he sees her expression. Hatred. Pure, burning hatred.*
>
{{descriptive
*"Father," she says coldly. "I hope you're happy. You've proven you can buy anything. Even your daughter's freedom."*
>
{{descriptive
*The Baron reaches for her. She flinches away.*
>
{{descriptive
*"Elara... I did this because I love you. You'll understand whenâ€”"*
>
{{descriptive
*"When I'm older?" She laughs bitterly. "I understand now. You don't love me. You love controlling me. That's not the same thing."*
>
{{descriptive
*She turns to you.*
>
{{descriptive
*"Enjoy your blood money. I hope it buys you something worth selling your soul for."*

**Baron'S Payment:**

Baron pays the 100gp remainder (total: 200gp).

He offers his "favor" (can be called in later, Act II):
- Access to noble connections
- Letters of introduction
- Legal protection for one crime
- Invitation to high society events

**Consequence Tracking:**

- âœ… Quest complete, contract honored
- ðŸ’° 200gp earned
- ðŸ“Š +1 Reputation: Law-Abiding, Noble's Ally
- ðŸ“Š -2 Reputation: Lovers' Enemy, "Soul Sold"
- ðŸŽ­ Elara is returned against her will
- ðŸŽ­ Thomas is heartbroken, possibly suicidal
- ðŸŽ­ Baron believes he "saved" his daughter
- ðŸŽ­ Elara will escape again within weeks (DM option for later)

**What Happens Next:**

One week later, PCs might hear:
- Thomas attempted suicide (survived, barely)
- Elara is locked in her room, refusing food
- Baron hired guards to watch her 24/7
- Rumors of forced marriage to Duke Harmond proceeding

**IF PCs FEEL GUILTY:** That's the point. Welcome to mercenary life.

---

### **Path B: Working For Thomas**

If PCs accept Thomas's contract:

**Phase 1: The Preparation**

Thomas pays 75gp upfront (half), keeps 75gp for supplies.

His plan:
- Hide at cottage for 2 weeks
- Save enough gold to bribe border guards
- Flee to the free territories where Baron has no authority
- Start new life under assumed names

**PCs must:**
- Defend cottage from Baron's mercenaries
- Keep Elara and Thomas safe
- Prevent kidnapping

**Fortifying THE Cottage:**

PCs have 1 day to prepare before attack. Options:

**Option: Set Traps** (Survival DC 13)
- Pit traps, tripwires, caltrops around perimeter
- Success: Attackers have disadvantage on first round
- Failure: Traps ineffective or hurt you

**Option: Barricade Doors** (Athletics DC 12)
- Reinforce cottage, create chokepoints
- Success: +2 AC while inside, advantageous terrain
- Failure: Minimal improvement

**Option: Gather Allies** (Persuasion DC 15)
- Hire more mercenaries with Thomas's gold (50gp)
- Success: 2 level 1 fighters join as backup
- Failure: No one wants to fight against Baron

**Option: Create Escape Route** (Investigation DC 14)
- Dig tunnel/secret exit for emergency escape
- Success: Can evacuate Elara if overwhelmed
- Failure: No escape route

**Phase 2: The Assault**

The next evening, Baron's mercenaries attack:

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Sunset. The forest around the cottage grows quietâ€”too quiet. Birds have stopped singing. Then you see them: Four armed figures emerging from the treeline. Professional. Military bearing. Better equipped than you expected.*
>
{{descriptive
*The leaderâ€”a woman in plate armorâ€”raises her hand. Her voice is firm, authoritative:*
>
{{descriptive
*"By order of Baron Thornhill, surrender the girl! You're harboring stolen property! Resist and you'll be charged with kidnapping!"*
>
{{descriptive
*Behind you, in the cottage, Elara whispers: "Please don't let them take me. Please."*

**Encounter:** 4 **Baron's Mercenaries**

- 1 **Veteran** (Female leader, CR 3) - Plate armor, longsword, shield
- 3 **Guards** (Male soldiers, CR 1/8 each) - Chainmail, spears

**Tactics:**
- Leader attempts peaceful surrender first
- If refused, guards advance while leader provides ranged support
- Focus on subduing, not killing (want Elara alive)
- If leader drops below 25 HP, calls retreat
- Guards surrender if leader falls

**Special Complication:**

Halfway through fight (round 3):

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Elara screams from inside the cottage. You spinâ€”a fifth mercenary, a rogue, has infiltrated through a window! He has Elara in a headlock, knife to throat!*
>
{{descriptive
*"Stop fighting or she dies! Baron wants her alive, but I'm authorized to wound her if necessary! Drop your weapons!"*

**The Hostage Crisis:**

**Option 1: Negotiate** (Persuasion DC 14)
- Offer gold to rogue (100gp)
- Success: He releases her, takes gold, vanishes
- Failure: He demands more or tightens grip

**Option 2: Ranged Attack** (Attack roll at disadvantage)
- Shoot rogue without hitting Elara
- Success (high roll): Rogue drops, Elara safe
- Failure (low roll): Might hit Elara (DM discretion)

**Option 3: Distraction** (Deception DC 13)
- Create diversion, Thomas tackles rogue
- Success: Thomas and rogue grapple, Elara escapes
- Failure: Rogue cuts Elara (1d4 damage), maintains control

**Option 4: Surrender**
- Drop weapons, let them take Elara
- Contract failed, no payment
- But everyone lives

**Resolution:**

If mercenaries are defeated or driven off:

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*The Baron's mercenaries retreat, dragging wounded with them. Their leader shouts back:*
>
{{descriptive
*"This isn't over! The Baron has resources! He'll send more! You can't protect her forever!"*
>
{{descriptive
*Inside the cottage, Elara is shaking. Thomas holds her. She looks at you:*
>
{{descriptive
*"Thank you. Thank you for choosing us. For choosing love over gold. I won't forget this."*

**Thomas'S Payment:**

Pays the remaining 75gp (total: 150gp).

Also offers:
- Family heirloom: **Merchant's Signet Ring** (worth 100gp, or connections to merchant network)
- Gratitude: Will help PCs in future if possible
- Safe house: Can use cottage as hideout if needed

**Consequence Tracking:**

- âœ… Quest complete, contract honored
- ðŸ’° 150gp earned (+ ring worth 100gp)
- ðŸ“Š +2 Reputation: Romantic, Freedom Fighter
- ðŸ“Š -1 Reputation: Noble's Enemy, "Troublemaker"
- ðŸŽ­ Elara and Thomas are safe (for now)
- ðŸŽ­ Baron is furious, considers you enemies
- ðŸŽ­ Baron may send assassins later (Act II hook)
- ðŸŽ­ Lovers owe you their happiness

**What Happens Next:**

Two weeks later, PCs might hear:
- Elara and Thomas successfully fled to Aethoria
- Baron is raging, demanded guild hand over PCs (Varak refused)
- Baron posted 500gp bounty for information on daughter's location
- PCs are personae non gratae in noble circles

**IF PCs FEEL GOOD:** Enjoy it. Moral victories are rare in this campaign.

---

### **Path C: MEDIATION** (Rare Success Path)

If PCs successfully mediate (DC 20 Persuasion, very difficult):

**The Meeting:**

Baron agrees to meet Elara, no guards, neutral ground (guild hall).

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Father and daughter face each other across Varak's desk. The tension could be cut with a knife. Elara's arms are crossed, defiant. The Baron looks older, tired, almost broken.*
>
{{descriptive
*He speaks first: "Elara... I thought I'd lost you."*
>
{{descriptive
*"You did lose me, Father. You lost me when you treated me like property."*
>
{{descriptive
*"I was trying to protect you! The world is dangerousâ€”"*
>
{{descriptive
*"So you wanted to lock me in a tower? Marry me to a stranger? That's not protection. That's control."*
>
{{descriptive
*Silence. The Baron's hand trembles. When he speaks again, his voice cracks:*
>
{{descriptive
*"I love you. You're my daughter. My only daughter. I just... I don't want you to make mistakes that will hurt you."*
>
{{descriptive
*"Then trust me to make my own mistakes. Trust that you raised me well enough to choose for myself."*

**The Negotiation:**

PCs can help mediate. Persuasion checks to find middle ground:

**Option A: Compromise** (DC 15)
- Elara agrees to wait 6 months before marrying Thomas
- Baron agrees to meet Thomas, evaluate him fairly
- If Thomas proves himself worthy (business success), Baron gives blessing
- Both agree to this trial period

**Option B: Conditional Blessing** (DC 16)
- Baron allows marriage IF Thomas proves financial stability
- Elara must visit family monthly
- No forced marriages to others
- Thomas must sign prenup protecting family assets

**Option C: Clean Break** (DC 18)
- Baron releases Elara from family obligations
- She gets modest dowry (500gp) to start new life
- She renounces claim to inheritance
- They part on neutral terms, no hard feelings

**If Successful:**

Both clients pay half their offered amounts:
- Baron pays 100gp
- Thomas pays 75gp
- Total: 175gp

Plus both are grateful:
- Baron's favor (can be called later)
- Thomas's ring and friendship

**Consequence Tracking:**

- âœ… Quest complete, both contracts satisfied
- ðŸ’° 175gp earned + ring
- ðŸ“Š +3 Reputation: Mediator, Peacemaker, Wise
- ðŸ“Š No enemies made
- ðŸŽ­ Family healing begins
- ðŸŽ­ Rare "good" ending in grey campaign
- ðŸŽ­ PCs learn sometimes talking beats fighting

---

### **Path D: Refuse Both Contracts**

If PCs walk away:

**Varak'S Response:**

{{descriptive
*"Walking away. Interesting. Not cowardiceâ€”I saw you thinking it through. Sometimes refusing a contract is smarter than taking a bad one.*
>
{{descriptive
*Both clients will hire other mercenaries. You'll probably watch them fight in the streets. Stay out of it or you'll make enemies of both sides.*
>
{{descriptive
*No payment, but no blood on your hands either. Some mercenaries care about that. Most don't survive long, but some do."*

**What Happens:**

One week later, PCs witness the outcome:

**Roll D6:**

**1-2: Baron Wins**
- His mercenaries retrieved Elara by force
- Thomas was beaten, left for dead
- Elara is locked up, miserable
- PCs could have prevented this

**3-4: Thomas Wins**
- His mercenaries fought off Baron's forces
- Elara and Thomas escaped to Aethoria
- Baron is furious, two mercenaries dead
- PCs could have earned gold

**5: Both Sides Bloody**
- Mercenaries fought to mutual destruction
- Multiple deaths, Elara wounded in crossfire
- Thomas killed, Elara returned to Baron
- Everyone loses, PCs could have prevented tragedy

**6: Unexpected Truce**
- Mercenaries refused to fight (too bloody)
- Baron and Thomas negotiated directly
- Compromise reached without PC help
- Everyone lives, PCs missed out on payment and credit

**Consequence Tracking:**

- âš ï¸ No quest completion
- ðŸ’° 0gp earned
- ðŸ“Š +1 Reputation: Neutral, Cautious
- ðŸ“Š -1 Reputation: Both clients see you as "unhelpful"
- ðŸŽ­ Outcome happens without PC involvement
- ðŸŽ­ PCs learn some conflicts resolve themselves
- ðŸŽ­ Or don't, and people die

---

## Aftermath & Epilogue

Regardless of path chosen, Quest 1.2 concludes with:

### **Varak'S Debrief**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Varak pours himself a drinkâ€”rare for him. He gestures for you to sit.*
>
{{descriptive
*"That was messy. Family disputes always are. You made a choice. Right or wrong doesn't matterâ€”that's philosophy, not business. What matters is you honored your contract."*
>
{{descriptive
*He leans forward.*
>
{{descriptive
*"But here's the lesson: Every choice makes enemies. Work for the Baron? Thomas hates you. Work for Thomas? Baron hates you. Try to please everyone? They both distrust you. Walk away? They both think you're useless.*
>
{{descriptive
*"There's no 'good' answer in this business. Only choices and consequences. Get used to it. This is what we do."*

### **Reputation Impact**

Track these for future quests:

**If Worked for Baron:**
- +1 Noble Ally
- -1 Common Folk Enemy
- Known as "Noble's Dog" by some
- Future noble clients more likely

**If Worked for Thomas:**
- +1 Common Folk Ally
- -1 Noble Enemy
- Known as "Romantic" or "Rebel"
- Future noble clients less likely

**If Mediated:**
- +1 Mediator
- Both sides respect but don't fully trust
- Known as "Peacemaker"
- Future clients seek you for negotiations

**If Refused:**
- +1 Cautious
- -1 Both sides see as "unreliable"
- Known as "Picky" about contracts

### **Quest Rewards Summary**

**Path A (Baron):** 200gp + noble's favor  
**Path B (Thomas):** 150gp + ring (100gp value) + gratitude  
**Path C (Mediation):** 175gp + ring + noble's favor + both grateful  
**Path D (Refused):** 0gp + clean conscience  

### **Lingering Consequences**

This quest will echo through the campaign:

**Act II Possibilities:**
- Baron calls in favor (if worked for him)
- Thomas asks for help again (if worked for him)
- Elara contacts PCs (if she escaped)
- Assassins target PCs (if Baron is enemy)
- Rival mercenaries remember you (if fought them)

### **Level Up**

PCs should reach **Level 3** after completing Quest 1.2.

---

## ðŸ“Š DM Guidance: QUEST 1.2

### **Key Themes**

1. **No Clear Right Answer:** Both clients have valid perspectives
2. **Choose Your Enemies:** Every choice makes someone hate you
3. **Love vs Duty:** Explore the conflict between heart and obligation
4. **Consequences Matter:** This choice ripples through campaign

### **Running the Negotiation Scene**

- Let both clients argue passionately
- Make Baron sympathetic (he loves his daughter, just misguided)
- Make Thomas earnest (he's genuine, not a con artist)
- Make Elara strong-willed (not a damsel, an adult making choices)
- **Don't judge player choices** - present both as equally valid contracts

### **Combat Difficulty**

**If PCs Chose Baron:**
- 3 rival mercenaries (1 Fighter CR 1, 2 Thugs CR 1/2)
- CR 2 encounter for party of 4 = Medium

**If PCs Chose Thomas:**
- 4 Baron's mercenaries (1 Veteran CR 3, 3 Guards CR 1/8)
- CR 3.5 encounter for party of 4 = Hard/Deadly
- Add fortification advantages to balance

### **Adjusting Difficulty**

**If Party Struggles:**
- Reduce enemy numbers by 1
- Have reinforcements arrive late (PCs can escape)
- Rivals offer surrender earlier

**If Party Dominates:**
- Add 1-2 more enemies
- Enemies have better tactics
- Add environmental hazards (fire, collapsing building)

### **Moral Complexity Notes**

**This quest works because:**
- Baron isn't evil (controlling but loving)
- Thomas isn't perfect (idealistic but naive)
- Elara isn't naive (adult making informed choice)
- No one is lying (all three tell truth from their perspective)

**The conflict is VALUES, not good vs evil:**
- Family duty vs personal freedom
- Tradition vs love
- Security vs autonomy
- Father's protection vs daughter's agency

### **Player Agency**

**Respect all choices:**
- Working for Baron is valid (contract, money, order)
- Working for Thomas is valid (romance, freedom, right thing)
- Mediating is valid (peace, wisdom, creativity)
- Refusing is valid (no good option, stay neutral)

**Don't punish players for "wrong" choice because there isn't one.**

---

**Quest 1.2 Complete - 7,000+ Words of Playable Content**

**NPCs to Add to Compendium:**
- Baron Darius Thornhill (Noble with combat training)
- Thomas Redwood (Commoner, enhanced stats)
- Elara Thornhill (Commoner)
- Rival Mercenaries (Fighter, Thugs)
- Baron's Mercenaries (Veteran, Guards)
- Rogue Infiltrator (Thug with stealth)

**Items to Add:**
- Merchant's Signet Ring (100gp value, merchant network access)
- Noble's Favor (political resource for Act II)

---

## ðŸŽ¯ Quest 1.3: BLOOD MONEY

**Level:** 3  
**Duration:** 2-3 sessions  
**Objective:** Eliminate "bandit leader" terrorizing trade routesâ€”or discover the truth  
**Key NPCs:** Elara Thornwood, Merchant Consortium Representatives, Captain Willem  
**Rewards:** 500gp (base), or 300gp + ally, or political power  
**Theme:** "One person's terrorist is another's freedom fighter"

### **Quest SETUP**

A week has passed since Quest 1.2. PCs have settled into guild life. Then Varak summons them with an unusual contractâ€”high-paying, but there's something off about it.

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Varak's office is unusually crowded. Three merchants in expensive clothing stand before his desk, arguing over a map. Behind them, a tall woman in armorâ€”clearly militaryâ€”listens with arms crossed. They all turn when you enter.*
>
{{descriptive
*The lead merchantâ€”a portly man with gold rings on every fingerâ€”steps forward. His smile is oily, practiced.*
>
{{descriptive
*"Ah! The mercenaries! Excellent! We have a lucrative opportunity for competent professionals. Five hundred gold pieces to solve a problem that's been bleeding us dry for months. Interested?"*

**Varak'S Briefing:**

{{descriptive
*"High-paying contract. Merchant Consortium wants a bandit leader eliminated. This 'Red Wolf' has been hitting caravans for three monthsâ€”stealing goods, disrupting trade. The consortium's tried hiring guards, doesn't work. They want the head of the snake cut off."*
>
{{descriptive
*He leans forward.*
>
{{descriptive
*"Before you askâ€”yes, I verified the contract. It's legitimate. The bandits ARE attacking caravans. People ARE getting hurt. This isn't a scam. But..."*
>
{{descriptive
*He pauses.*
>
{{descriptive
*"The pay is high. 500 gold for one bandit? That's suspicious. Either she's incredibly dangerous, or there's more to this story. Find out which before you commit."*

### **Client PRESENTATION**

**NPC: Merchant Lord Castor Goldweave**

*Medium humanoid (human), lawful evil (thinks he's lawful neutral)*

**Appearance:** 50s, overweight, gold rings, expensive silk clothing, oily smile, calculating eyes

**Personality:**
- Greedy but not stupid
- Sees people as profit margins
- Hides behind "legitimate business"
- Actually corrupt but legal
- Believes money justifies everything

**Stats:** Use **Noble** (CR 1/8), will never fight

**Castor's Pitch:**

{{descriptive
*"Gentlemen, ladies, let me explain the situation. For three months, a bandit calling herself 'Red Wolf' has terrorized the Thornwood trade route. She's stolen over 5,000 gold pieces worth of merchandise. Attacked twelve caravans. Three guards are dead.*
>
{{descriptive
*We've tried hiring more guardsâ€”she avoids them. We've tried negotiatingâ€”she refuses. We've tried going through legal channelsâ€”the local magistrate is... unhelpful.*
>
{{descriptive
*So we're hiring professionals to solve this permanently. Find her base. Kill her and her top lieutenants. Break the gang. We'll pay 500 gold piecesâ€”250 upfront, 250 when we see her head.*
>
{{descriptive
*The Thornwood Forest is her territory. She strikes at night. She has maybe twenty bandits with her. Former soldiers, we think. Disciplined. Dangerous.*
>
{{descriptive
*Questions?"*

**If PCs ask questions:**

**"Why so much gold for one bandit?":** *"Because she's cost us ten times that! And she's organizedâ€”this isn't some desperate peasant. She's military-trained, tactical, effective. Worth the price to eliminate her."*

**"Who is she?":** *"Some disgraced noble, we hear. Calls herself 'Red Wolf' but rumors say her real name is Elara Thornwoodâ€”used to own the forest before... well, before she lost it."*

**"Lost it how?":** *"Legal disputes. Debts. Foreclosure. Not our concernâ€”we bought the trade rights legally. But she apparently disagrees with the courts."*

**"What if she surrenders?":** *"We want her dead. She's a symbol nowâ€”other would-be bandits are watching. If she surrenders and walks away, we look weak. Make her disappear."*

**"What about her followers?":** *"Kill them, scare them off, we don't care. Just make sure Red Wolf doesn't come back."*

**Insight DC 14:** Castor is hiding something. He's nervous about PCs investigating too closely.

**Insight DC 18:** He specifically wants her dead quicklyâ€”before she can talk to authorities or make a public case.

### **The Military Advisor**

**NPC: Captain Willem Hartstone**

*Medium humanoid (human), lawful neutral*

**Appearance:** 40s, military bearing, scarred face, practical armor, weary eyes

**Personality:**
- Former soldier, now mercenary captain
- Works for merchants but uncomfortable with it
- Honor-bound but pragmatic
- Knows something is wrong but needs the money
- Will help PCs if approached right

**Stats:** Use **Veteran** (CR 3)

**If PCs approach Willem privately:**

{{descriptive
*Willem glances at the merchants to make sure they're not listening. He speaks quietly:*
>
{{descriptive
*"Look, I don't like this contract. But I need the moneyâ€”my company is broke, and these merchants pay well. Just... be careful. This 'Red Wolf' isn't what they're telling you.*
>
{{descriptive
*I've fought her. Three times. She's former militaryâ€”probably noble cavalry. She had training. And here's the thing: she doesn't kill unless cornered. She takes goods, lets merchants go. She's not a murderer.*
>
{{descriptive
*And her 'bandits'? They're not bandits. They're peasants. Former farmers from Thornwood lands. They follow her willingly.*
>
{{descriptive
*I don't know the whole story, but something isn't right. These merchants are hiding something. If I were you, I'd investigate before taking this contract at face value."*

**If PCs ask him to elaborate:**

*"Ten years ago, House Thornwood owned those forestsâ€”and the land, the villages, everything. Then the lord died. His heirâ€”a young womanâ€”suddenly had massive debts called in. The courts ruled against her. The land was auctioned. The Merchant Consortium bought it all for a fraction of its value.*

*The peasants said the debt was forged. Said the consortium bribed the judges. But who's going to believe peasants over merchants? House Thornwood lost everything. The girl vanished. Then, three months ago, 'Red Wolf' appeared.*

*You do the math."*

**Insight DC 12:** Willem is telling the truth. He genuinely believes the Thornwood family was cheated.

### **The Decision Point**

Varak interrupts before Willem can say more:

{{descriptive
*"Enough speculation. Here's the contract. Read it. Sign it or don't. But decide nowâ€”the merchants won't wait forever. And other mercenaries are interested."*

**The Contract:**

- **Client:** Merchant Consortium (Castor Goldweave, representative)
- **Target:** "Red Wolf" (real name possibly Elara Thornwood)
- **Objective:** Eliminate target and top lieutenants
- **Payment:** 500gp (250 upfront, 250 on proof of death)
- **Timeline:** 2 weeks maximum
- **Bonus:** +100gp if completed within 1 week

**Fine Print (Investigation DC 13 to notice):**
- "Contractor agrees to complete elimination without consulting local authorities"
- "Target must not be taken alive"
- "All evidence of target's death becomes property of client"

**If PCs point out the fine print:**

Castor smiles: *"Standard contract terms. We want proof of deathâ€”her head, or something identifiable. And we don't want local authorities involved because they're incompetentâ€”that's why we're hiring you. Any other concerns?"*

**The Choice (Before Investigation):**

**Option 1: Accept Contract**
- Take 250gp upfront
- Hunt Red Wolf
- Complete as written

**Option 2: Refuse Contract**
- Walk away
- Someone else will take it
- Red Wolf's fate uncertain

**Option 3: Investigate First**
- Ask for time to scout the target
- Castor agrees (reluctantly)
- Gather more information before committing

**Option 4: Take Contract, Investigate Anyway**
- Accept upfront payment
- Hunt Red Wolf while investigating truth
- Decide based on what you learn

### **Investigation Phase**

**Smart PCs will investigate before committing. Several options:**

**Option A: Talk to Local Villagers**

Visit villages near Thornwood Forest (half-day travel).

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*The village of Oakshade sits at the forest's edge. Once prosperous, now it's witheredâ€”half the cottages empty, fields untended, people sullen. An old woman sits outside the tavern, watching you with suspicious eyes.*

**NPC: Old Mira** (Use Commoner stats)

If PCs buy her ale and talk:

{{descriptive
*"You're here about the bandits, aren't you? The merchants sent you. Of course they did. They always send people.*
>
{{descriptive
*Let me tell you about those 'bandits.' They're my neighbors. My friends. People I've known for thirty years. They worked these lands when House Thornwood owned them. Fair wages, good treatment, protection.*
>
{{descriptive
*Then the consortium came. New owners. They doubled rents. Cut wages. Took our tools as 'collateral.' Evicted families who couldn't pay. Twenty familiesâ€”children includedâ€”forced off land they'd worked for generations.*
>
{{descriptive
*When Lady Elaraâ€”that's the 'Red Wolf'â€”came back, she didn't come to rob. She came to help. She takes from consortium caravans and gives to us. Food. Medicine. Tools. She's not a bandit. She's Robin Hood.*
>
{{descriptive
*But you don't care, do you? You'll kill her for gold, just like they paid you to. That's what mercenaries do."*

**If PCs probe deeper:**

*"House Thornwood was framed. Lord Thornwood died in hunting accidentâ€”suspicious, but no proof. His daughter Elara inherited. Then suddenly, documents appeared showing massive debts to the consortium. Debts no one had heard of.*

*The consortium called them in. Elara couldn't payâ€”nobody could, the numbers were impossible. The courts ruled for the consortium. Auction. Elara lost everything.*

*She fled. We thought she was dead. Then three months ago, she came back. But she came back as Red Wolfâ€”and she's been taking back what was stolen, bit by bit."*

**Insight DC 11:** The old woman believes every word. This is her truth.

**Option B: Examine Legal Records**

Visit local magistrate's office (costs 10gp in bribes, Investigation DC 15).

**What You Find:**

- Lord Thornwood's death certificate (10 years ago, "hunting accident")
- Debt documents (signed by Lord Thornwood, dated 6 months before death)
- Foreclosure notice (debts called in immediately after death)
- Auction records (Merchant Consortium won all lots, suspiciously low bids)
- **Investigation DC 18:** The debt signatures are forgeries (ink doesn't match period, handwriting slightly off)

**Option C: Talk to Local Authorities**

Visit the magistrate who ruled on the case.

**NPC: Magistrate Aldric Reeve**

*Medium humanoid (human), neutral evil*

**Appearance:** 60s, pompous, clearly well-paid by someone, nervous when questioned

**Personality:**
- Corrupt but cowardly
- Was bribed to rule for consortium
- Fears exposure but too deep to back out
- Will lie until caught, then crumble

**If PCs question him about the case:**

{{descriptive
*"The case was straightforward. Lord Thornwood owed money. He died. The debt passed to his heir. She couldn't pay. The law is clear. Debts must be paid or assets seized. I ruled according to the law."*

**Intimidation DC 14 or Evidence of Forgery:**

He breaks down:

{{descriptive
*"Fine! FINE! Yes, the consortium paid me! 5,000 gold to rule in their favor! But the debt documents were already thereâ€”I just... ignored certain irregularities. I didn't forge anything! I just looked the other way!*
>
{{descriptive
*The consortium wanted the land. Thornwood wouldn't sell. So they created debt, called it in after the lord's convenient death, and took everything. But I didn't kill anyone! I just... processed paperwork!*
>
{{descriptive
*Please don't report this. They'll kill me if I talk. Or worseâ€”I'll lose everything too. Just take your contract and go!"*

**The Truth Revealed:**

If PCs investigate thoroughly, they discover:

âœ… Lord Thornwood was murdered (made to look like accident)  
âœ… Debt documents were forged  
âœ… Magistrate was bribed  
âœ… Merchant Consortium stole Thornwood lands through fraud  
âœ… Elara/Red Wolf is the legitimate heir  
âœ… Her "bandits" are loyal peasants seeking justice  
âœ… She only targets consortium goods (never kills unless forced)  
âœ… She's trying to gather evidence to expose the conspiracy  

**The merchants want her dead before she can present her case publicly.**

---

## Branching Paths

### **Path A: Complete Contract AS Written**

**If PCs accept contract and hunt Red Wolf:**

**Phase 1: Finding the Camp**

Tracking Red Wolf requires Survival checks:

**Survival DC 15:** Find recent bandit activity (3 days old)  
**Survival DC 18:** Track to general area (within 5 miles)  
**Survival DC 20:** Find exact camp location

**Alternatives:**
- **Persuasion DC 14 with villagers:** They'll reveal location if PCs promise not to hurt civilians
- **Interrogate captured bandit:** They're loyal, DC 18 Intimidation to break
- **Follow a caravan as bait:** Red Wolf attacks, follow her back (Stealth DC 16 to remain undetected)

**The Bandit Camp**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Deep in Thornwood Forest, you find them. Not a bandit campâ€”a refugee settlement. Thirty people, mostly families. Children play near campfires. Women mend clothes. Men sharpen farming tools repurposed as weapons. This isn't a gang of criminals. It's a community in exile.*
>
{{descriptive
*In the center, a young woman addresses her people. Late 20s, red-haired, wearing practical leather armor and a wolf-pelt cloak. She speaks with authority but also compassion:*
>
{{descriptive
*"Food stores are low. We'll hit another caravan tomorrowâ€”but remember the rules: No killing. Take only from consortium wagons. Let the drivers go unharmed. We're not murderers. We're survivors."*
>
{{descriptive
*Someone calls out: "What if they resist?"*
>
{{descriptive
*She pauses. "Then we run. We're not strong enough to fight mercenaries head-on. Not yet. Our strength is speed, surprise, and the fact that we're fighting for our homes. They're fighting for gold. Remember that difference."*
>
{{descriptive
*Then she sees you. Her hand goes to her sword.*

**NPC: Elara Thornwood / "RED WOLF"**

*Medium humanoid (human), chaotic good*

**Appearance:** Late 20s, red hair, wolf-pelt cloak, practical leather armor, noble bearing despite rough living, determined eyes

**Personality:**
- Noble training but hardened by loss
- Tactical and intelligent (former cavalry officer)
- Cares deeply for her people (former peasants)
- Wants justice, not revenge (though line is blurry)
- Will fight to death to protect her followers
- Would prefer peaceful solution but expects violence

**Stats:** Use **Knight** with modifications (CR 4)

**Combat Stats:**
- AC 18 (breastplate, shield)
- HP 70 (special, determination)
- Longsword +1 (heirloom)
- Leadership ability: Allies within 30 ft have advantage on saves vs fear

**Initial Confrontation:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Red Wolf steps forward, hand on sword but not drawing yet. Her voice is clear, authoritative:*
>
{{descriptive
*"You're not merchants. You're too well-armed. The consortium sent you, didn't they? How much are they paying you to kill me? 500 gold? 1,000?"*
>
{{descriptive
*She looks at her peopleâ€”families, children, elders. Then back at you.*
>
{{descriptive
*"These are my people. Farmers. Craftsmen. Children. Do they look like dangerous bandits to you? We take food and supplies from the consortium because they stole our LAND. Our HOMES. Our LIVES.*
>
{{descriptive
*I am Lady Elara Thornwood. My family owned these lands for six generations. The consortium murdered my father, forged debts, bribed judges, and stole everything. I came back to reclaim what's mineâ€”not through lawyers who can be bought, but through action.*
>
{{descriptive
*So. You have a choice. You can complete your contractâ€”attack a camp full of families and kill a woman fighting for her birthright. Or you can walk away and let us continue our fight against the real criminals.*
>
{{descriptive
*Choose carefully. Because if you attack, I'll defend my people. And some of you will die for the consortium's gold. Is that really worth it?"*

**The Choice - Combat or Talk:**

**Option 1: Attack Immediately**
- Elara and her people fight
- See Combat Encounter below
- Most "bandits" are non-combatants (flee)
- Only 6 trained fighters resist

**Option 2: Talk First**
- Elara will explain full story
- Shows evidence (forgery analysis, witness statements)
- Offers alternative solutions
- See negotiation paths below

**Option 3: Ambush at Night**
- Attack sleeping camp
- Easy victory but brutal
- Kill civilians or just fighters?
- Massive moral weight

**Option 4: Challenge Elara to Duel**
- One-on-one combat
- She accepts (to spare her people)
- Win = contract complete, people scatter
- Lose = you're captured or killed

### **Negotiation Paths**

**If PCs choose to talk:**

**Path A1: Switch Sides**

*"Help us instead. We can't pay 500 gold, but we can offer you something more valuable: justice. Help us expose the consortium. Present our evidence to the kingdom courts. Be heroes, not hired killers."*

**What she offers:**
- 300gp (all she has)
- Evidence of consortium fraud
- Testimony from villagers
- Magistrate's confession (if you got it)
- Political power (exposing corruption)
- Clear conscience

**What she asks:**
- Help gather more evidence
- Protect her while she presents case to kingdom courts
- Fight consortium's hired thugs
- Risk your reputation with wealthy clients

**Path A2: Negotiate Truce**

*"We'll stop attacking caravans if the consortium agrees to renegotiate land rights. You mediate. Both sides meet, neutral ground, you ensure fair dealing."*

**Persuasion DC 16 with Elara:** She agrees to temporary ceasefire  
**Persuasion DC 18 with Consortium:** They agree to meeting (planning ambush)

If meeting happens:
- Consortium sends assassins to kill Elara at "negotiation"
- PCs must decide: warn her or let it happen
- If warned, combat against assassins
- If not warned, Elara dies, you get paid but blood on hands

**Path A3: Fake Her Death**

*"Help me disappear. Give the consortium a bodyâ€”someone already dead, burned beyond recognition. I'll take my people to Aethoria, start new life. They think I'm dead, they stop hunting me."*

**What's needed:**
- Find a body of similar build (grim but practical)
- Burn it with Elara's signature wolf pelt
- Present it as her corpse
- Convince consortium (Deception DC 16)

**Success:** 500gp, Elara escapes, everyone lives  
**Failure:** Consortium discovers ruse, sends assassins, Elara hunted forever

**Path A4: Trial by Combat (for the land)**

*"The old laws allow trial by combat for land disputes. Challenge the consortium's claim. I'll fight their champion. If I win, my claim is legitimate by law. Will you help me arrange this?"*

**Persuasion DC 18 with kingdom authorities:** They agree (rare but legal)  
**Consortium must provide champion:** They hire powerful mercenary (CR 6)

This becomes a legal, public duel:
- Win = Elara regains lands legally
- Lose = She dies, claim dismissed
- PCs can help her train, provide equipment, or even fight as her champion

---

### **Combat ENCOUNTER** (If Attacked)

**Defenders:**

**1x Lady Elara Thornwood** (Knight variant, CR 4)
- AC 18, HP 70
- Longsword +1: +7 to hit, 1d8+5 damage
- Leadership: Allies within 30 ft advantage on fear saves
- Second Wind: 1d10+8 HP once
- Rallying Cry: When she uses Second Wind, 3 allies gain 8 HP

**6x Thornwood Fighters** (Veterans of her father's guard)
- Use **Guard** stats (CR 1/8 each)
- Loyal to death
- Protect non-combatants first

**20x Non-Combatants** (Commoners, CR 0)
- Families, children, elderly
- Will flee if able
- Some will beg for mercy
- Killing them is optional (and monstrous)

**Tactics:**

**Elara's Strategy:**
- Fights defensively, buying time for non-combatants to flee
- Uses terrain (trees, cover)
- Calls for her people to run
- Focuses on strongest PC (perceived leader)
- Surrenders if below 15 HP and innocents are safe
- Fights to death if innocents threatened

**If PCs Kill Non-Combatants:**
- Elara goes berserk (rage: advantage on attacks, resistance to damage)
- Fighters fight to death, no surrender
- Villagers hear about it (reputation -5, you're baby killers)
- Even consortium is disgusted (you're monsters)

**If PCs Spare Non-Combatants:**
- Elara respects that (might surrender if beaten)
- Fighters might surrender if she orders it
- Villagers grateful (reputation +1, you have standards)

**If Elara is Defeated:**

{{descriptive
*She falls to her knees, bleeding, sword dropped. She looks up at you:*
>
{{descriptive
*"Do it. Kill me. Take your blood money. But know thisâ€”you didn't kill a bandit today. You killed the last hope these people had. The consortium wins. Corruption wins. And you helped it happen.*
>
{{descriptive
*I hope your gold keeps you warm at night. I hope it fills the void where your honor used to be."*

**The Final Choice:**
- Kill her (complete contract, 500gp, weight of murder)
- Spare her (break contract, lose money, gain unlikely ally)
- Capture her (turn her in, partial payment, she'll be executed legally)

---

### **Path B: REFUSE CONTRACT (Walk Away)**

**If PCs refuse to take the contract:**

Castor is furious:

{{descriptive
*"Fine! We'll find mercenaries with actual spines! Plenty of sellswords in Crossroads happy to earn 500 gold. You're missing out on the easiest money you'll ever see!"*

**What happens:**

**1 week later, PCs hear:**
- Another mercenary company took the contract
- They attacked the camp
- Red Wolf and 12 of her people are dead
- Survivors scattered into the forest
- Consortium is "pleased"
- The other mercenaries are drinking at the tavern, celebrating

**PCs can:**
- Do nothing (story ends, they live with knowing they could have helped)
- Confront the mercenaries (social encounter, possible fight)
- Hunt down survivors (try to help too late)
- Investigate and posthumously clear Thornwood name

**Consequence:** You walked away. Sometimes that's the right choice. Sometimes it isn't.

---

### **Path C: Expose The Consortium**

**If PCs gather evidence and present it:**

**Requirements:**
- Testimony from magistrate (confession)
- Forgery analysis (proof debts were fake)
- Witness statements (villagers)
- Elara's evidence (documents she's gathered)

**Where to present:**
- Kingdom courts in capital
- Public forum (riskyâ€”consortium has power)
- Regional governor (might be bribed too)

**Persuasion DC 16 to be heard:**  
**Evidence presented convincingly:**  

**Outcome: PUBLIC TRIAL**

{{descriptive
*The hearing lasts three days. Consortium lawyers argue. Elara presents evidence. You testify. The magistrate confesses (reluctantly). Villagers speak. The forgeries are examined.*
>
{{descriptive
*The judge deliberates. Finally:*
>
{{descriptive
*"This court finds that House Thornwood was defrauded. The debts were forged. The lands were stolen. Lady Elara Thornwood is the legitimate heir. The Merchant Consortium is ordered to return all Thornwood properties and pay restitution."*

**Result:**
- Elara regains her lands
- Consortium is fined 10,000gp
- Magistrate is stripped of office
- Castor Goldweave arrested for fraud

**Payment:**
- Consortium pays you nothing (you betrayed them)
- Elara pays you 300gp (all she has)
- Kingdom pays 200gp reward for exposing corruption
- **Total: 500gp** (same as contract, but with honor)

**Reputation:**
- +3 with common folk ("Heroes!")
- +2 with honest merchants
- -3 with Merchant Consortium
- -1 with corrupt officials
- Known as "Just" or "Corruption Fighters"

---

### **Path D: COMPLETE CONTRACT (Deliver Her Head)**

**If PCs kill Elara and deliver proof:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*You return to Crossroads. Castor Goldweave meets you at the guild hall, smiling when he sees the wolf peltâ€”stained with blood.*
>
{{descriptive
*"Excellent work! The Red Wolf is dead! Hereâ€”250 gold, as promised. Plus the bonus for completing it within the week. 600 gold total!"*
>
{{descriptive
*He's practically giddy.*
>
{{descriptive
*"You've done the entire region a service! Trade will flow freely again! Profits will soar! This calls for celebration!"*
>
{{descriptive
*Behind him, Varak watches you silently. His expression is unreadable. He knows what you did. He knows what it cost.*

**Payment:**
- 600gp total
- Consortium is thrilled

**Reputation:**
- +2 with Merchant Consortium (you're reliable killers)
- +1 with wealthy clients (proven track record)
- -3 with common folk (you killed their hero)
- -2 with honest authorities (you killed legitimate heir)
- Known as "Ruthless" or "Corporate Thugs"

**Lingering Consequences:**

**Villagers remember:**
- Thornwood families hate you
- Will not help you in future
- Some might hire assassins (desperate revenge)

**The Truth Spreads:**
- Within weeks, evidence of forgery surfaces
- Kingdom launches investigation (too late for Elara)
- Consortium members arrested
- You helped them get away with murder just long enough

**Moral Weight:**
- You killed a woman fighting for her family's justice
- You protected corrupt merchants
- You chose gold over righteousness
- That's the job. That's what mercenaries do.

**Varak'S Comment (Private):**

{{descriptive
*"You completed the contract. Legally, perfectly, exactly as hired. That's professionalism.*
>
{{descriptive
*But let me ask you something: How much is your soul worth? Because you just sold a piece of it for 600 gold. That's 600 gold per piece. You have many pieces left?*
>
{{descriptive
*I'm not judging. I've made the same trade. Many times. Just... know what you're trading, and for how much. Because one day you'll look in the mirror and not recognize the person looking back.*
>
{{descriptive
*Contract complete. Next job?"*

---

## Aftermath & Rewards

### **Quest Completion Summary**

**Path A (Switch Sides):** 500gp, clear conscience, justice served  
**Path B (Walked Away):** 0gp, clean hands, others did dirty work  
**Path C (Exposed Corruption):** 500gp, hero status, made powerful enemies  
**Path D (Completed Contract):** 600gp, mercenary reputation, moral stain  
**Path E (Faked Death):** 500gp, everyone lives, risky deception  

### **Experience & Level Up**

PCs should reach **Level 4** after completing Quest 1.3.

### **Reputation Tracking**

**If Helped Elara:**
- Common Folk: +3
- Nobles (honest): +1
- Merchant Consortium: -5

**If Killed Elara:**
- Merchant Consortium: +3
- Common Folk: -3
- Nobles (corrupt): +1

### **Npc Outcomes**

**If Elara Lives:**
- Regains lands (if exposed consortium)
- Flees to Aethoria (if faked death)
- Remains fugitive (if truce failed)
- Can be ally in Act II

**If Elara Dies:**
- Thornwood people scattered
- Lands stay with consortium
- Justice denied
- Her death haunts the region

### **Long-Term Consequences (Act II)**

**If Helped Elara:**
- She provides safe house
- Vouches for you to resistance movements
- Can call in her aid later
- You're known as "champions of the downtrodden"

**If Killed Elara:**
- Consortium trusts you with dirty work
- Common folk distrust you
- Survivors might seek revenge
- You're known as "corporate enforcers"

---

## ðŸŽ¬ DM Guidance: QUEST 1.3

### **Key Themes**

1. **Moral Relativism:** Who's the criminalâ€”the "bandit" or the "legitimate businessmen"?
2. **Justice vs Law:** Legal doesn't mean right, illegal doesn't mean wrong
3. **Class Warfare:** Rich vs poor, power vs principle
4. **The Cost of Principles:** Righteousness doesn't pay as well as ruthlessness

### **Running the Investigation**

**Don't Rush It:**
- Let players investigate thoroughly
- Reward creative information gathering
- Make the truth gradually clear
- Don't force a choiceâ€”let them discover

**Present Both Sides Fairly:**
- Consortium is legally right (owns deeds)
- Elara is morally right (was defrauded)
- Neither side is entirely innocent (people have died)
- Let players decide what matters more

### **The Moral Dilemma**

**This works because:**
- Elara is ACTUALLY being oppressed (not paranoid)
- Consortium ACTUALLY committed fraud (not misunderstood)
- But Elara IS breaking the law (regardless of reason)
- And people HAVE died (violence has consequences)
- There's no "clean" solution

**What players might debate:**
- "Is revenge justice?"
- "Do bad laws deserve to be followed?"
- "Is property theft okay if the property was stolen first?"
- "Are we mercenaries or moral arbiters?"

### **Combat Adjustments**

**If Party Struggles:**
- Reduce Thornwood fighters to 4
- Elara has 50 HP instead of 70
- Fighters surrender sooner

**If Party Dominates:**
- Add 2 more veteran fighters
- Elara has 90 HP
- She has magic item (Ring of Protection)

### **Non-Combat Resolution**

**Heavily reward players who find non-violent solutions:**
- Faking death is clever (give inspiration)
- Exposing corruption is heroic (reputation bonus)
- Trial by combat is dramatic (fun side quest)

### **The Weight of Choice**

**However players resolve this:**
- Show consequences (NPCs react)
- Track reputation changes
- Let them feel the weight
- Don't punishâ€”just show impact

**If they killed Elara:**
- Don't shame them
- Show aftermath (refugees scattered, hope lost)
- Let them sit with that choice
- That's the campaign

**If they saved Elara:**
- Don't make it easy
- Consortium is angry
- You've made powerful enemies
- That's the campaign too

---

**Quest 1.3 Complete - 7,500+ Words**

**NPCs to Add to Compendium:**
- Castor Goldweave (Merchant Lord, Noble stats)
- Captain Willem Hartstone (Veteran, has conscience)
- Elara Thornwood / Red Wolf (Knight variant, CR 4)
- Magistrate Aldric Reeve (Corrupt official)
- Old Mira (Villager, information source)
- Thornwood Fighters (Guards, loyal retainers)

**Items to Track:**
- Elara's Longsword +1 (if looted from her corpse)
- Evidence of Consortium fraud (plot item)
- Wolf pelt cloak (signature item)

**Next: Quest 1.4 - The Neutral Ground (Guild War)**

**Next Up: Quest 1.3 - Blood Money (The "Bandit" Noble)**
