## Npc: Elara Corvus

*Medium humanoid (human), chaotic good*

**Appearance:** 20s, resembles Corvus, scholar's clothing, desperate eyes, frightened but determined

**Who She Is:**
- Corvus's daughter
- Former Unbound believer
- Realized father is insane
- Stole journal pages
- Trying to stop him

**Armor Class:** 12 (15 with *mage armor*)  
**Hit Points:** 45 (10d8)  
**Speed:** 30 ft.

**STR** 8 (-1) | **DEX** 14 (+2) | **CON** 10 (+0)  
**INT** 16 (+3) | **WIS** 14 (+2) | **CHA** 13 (+1)

**Skills:** Arcana +6, History +6, Investigation +6, Perception +5  
**Senses:** Passive Perception 15  
**Languages:** Common, Draconic, Elvish  
**Challenge:** 4 (1,100 XP)

#### Spellcasting

**Spellcasting Ability:** Intelligence (spell save DC 14, +6 to hit)

**Cantrips:** *fire bolt, mage hand, minor illusion, prestidigitation*

**Spells Prepared:**
- 1st level (4 slots): *detect magic, mage armor, shield, thunderwave*
- 2nd level (3 slots): *invisibility, misty step, shatter*
- 3rd level (3 slots): *counterspell, fireball, fly*
- 4th level (2 slots): *dimension door, greater invisibility*
- 5th level (1 slot): *cone of cold*

#### Personality

**Motivation:**
- Stop her father from apocalypse
- Loved him but recognizes madness
- Willing to die to prevent catastrophe
- Needs helpâ€”can't stop him alone

**What She Knows:**
- Components are corrupting Corvus
- He'll kill 30-40% of world population
- Final restructuring removes free will
- He has two Components (needs three more)
- Plans to use mercenaries until last moment, then eliminate them

**What She Wants:**
- Destroy the Components
- Stop Corvus (even if it means killing him)
- Save humanity from "salvation"

---

### **Confrontation With Corvus**

**If PCs confront him:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Corvus looks at the journal pages. His expression shiftsâ€”not shame, but annoyance.*
>
{{descriptive
*"Elara. Always too sentimental." He looks at you calmly. "Yes. It's all true. 30-40% casualties. Free will removal. Necessary steps for perfect world.*
>
{{descriptive
*(He's not apologetic. He's EXPLAINING.)*
>
{{descriptive
*"You're mercenaries. You understand hard choices. Sometimes you must kill to save. This is that, scaled up. Kill millions to save billions.*
>
{{descriptive
*The old world is BROKEN. War. Poverty. Oppression. I can FIX it. Make humanity perfect. Isn't that worth the cost?"*

**Insight DC 15:** He's completely serious and genuinely believes this is right

**If PCs call him insane:**

{{descriptive
*"Insane? I'm the ONLY sane one. Look at the world! Thaldros murders refugees. Aethoria betrays its own ideals. Endless cycles of suffering. I'm offering to END that.*
>
{{descriptive
*Yes, the price is high. Yes, you'll lose free will. But you'll also lose suffering. Pain. War. Isn't that worth it?"*

**If PCs threaten to stop him:**

{{descriptive
*(Sadly)*
{{descriptive
*"I hoped you'd understand. But if you oppose me, you're choosing suffering over salvation. I can't allow that.*
>
{{descriptive
*(He raises hand, Components glowing)*
>
{{descriptive
*I'm sorry. You were good mercenaries. But the new world has no place for doubters."*

**Boss Fight Initiated**

---

### **The CHOICE (Unbound Path)**

**PCs must decide:**

#### **Option 1: Fight Corvus Now**

**Actions:**
- Kill Corvus before he completes plan
- Destroy/secure Components
- End Unbound threat

**Boss Fight:**

**Corvus Blackwood (Powered by Two Components)**

**Armor Class:** 18 (enhanced by Components)  
**Hit Points:** 150 (augmented)  
**Challenge:** 11 (7,200 XP)

**New Abilities (Component-Enhanced):**

**Reality Distortion (Recharge 5-6).** 30-ft. radius. All creatures make DC 18 Wis save or take 8d6 psychic damage and stunned until end of Corvus's next turn.

**Phase Shift (3/Day).** As bonus action, become incorporeal until start of next turn. Can move through objects, immune to all damage.

**Summon Unbound Fanatics (1/Day).** 6 Unbound Cultists appear and fight for him.

**If defeated:**
- Corvus dies
- Components can be secured/destroyed
- Unbound collapses without leader
- World saved from restructuring
- You're heroes (to some)

**If you lose:**
- Corvus captures you
- Imprisoned until restructuring
- Bad ending (experience new world firsthand)

**Consequences of victory:**
- No payment (killed employer)
- Reputation: -20 with remaining Unbound
- Reputation: +10 with both kingdoms (removed mutual threat)
- Components in your possession (very dangerous)
- What do you do with them?

---

#### **Option 2: JOIN CORVUS**

**Accept his vision:**

**Rationalization:**
- Maybe he's right about world being broken
- 30% dead vs centuries of war casualties
- Perfect world worth the price
- Free will causes suffering

**Consequences:**
- Continue working for Unbound
- Help collect remaining Components
- Enable apocalypse
- Become architects of "perfect" tyranny
- Quest 2.5 involves completing restructuring
- Act III: You rule the new world (dystopian)

---

#### **Option 3: Flee The Unbound**

**Actions:**
- Abandon Corvus
- Don't fight him but don't help
- Go independent

**Consequences:**
- Unbound hunts you
- Both kingdoms hunt you (you're known Unbound members)
- Wanted by everyone
- Must survive as outlaws
- Can try to warn kingdoms about Corvus

**If you warn kingdoms:**
- They might believe you
- Might ally against Unbound threat
- Quest 2.5 becomes alliance mission

---

#### **Option 4: STEAL COMPONENTS**

**Actions:**
- Betray Corvus
- Steal both Components from him
- Prevent apocalypse but keep power

**Stealth/Deception DC 18 to steal them:**

**If successful:**
- You have 2 of 5 Components
- Corvus hunts you obsessively
- Both kingdoms want them
- Ultimate power in your hands
- What will YOU do with god-tier artifacts?

**Consequences:**
- Corruption (Wisdom saves every long rest)
- Everyone hunts you
- Temptation to use them yourself
- Can you resist Components' influence?

---

#### **Option 5: Sabotage From Within**

**Pretend to stay loyal, sabotage secretly:**

**Deception DC 17 to maintain cover:**

**Plan:**
- Act loyal to Corvus
- Secretly work against him
- Feed intelligence to kingdoms
- Destroy Components when opportunity arises

**If successful:**
- Continue Unbound missions outwardly
- Secretly undermine operations
- Lead to final confrontation in Quest 2.5
- Dramatic betrayal at crucial moment

---

## Universal Elements (All Paths)

### **Regardless of faction, this quest includes:**

**The Betrayal:**
- Every faction was lying
- Trust broken
- Must reassess allegiances

**The Informant:**
- Someone inside helps you
- Risk their life to warn you
- Represents conscience in corrupt system

**The Confrontation:**
- Face your faction leader with evidence
- They don't deny it (refreshingly honest)
- Gives their justification

**The Choice:**
- Stay loyal despite betrayal
- Switch sides
- Go independent
- Expose corruption
- Take violent action

**The Consequences:**
- This decision determines your path through remaining Act II
- No "right" answer
- All choices have costs

---

**Two weeks later (regardless of choice):**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*The world shifted. You learned the truth. You made your choice. Now you live with it.*
>
{{descriptive
*War continues. Factions maneuver. But you're no longer naive. You know what you're fighting forâ€”or against. You know the costs.*
>
{{descriptive

>

*The Royal Vault of Kaer Thandros. Everyone wants in. Everyone's planning heists.*
>

*This is where the truth dies or spreads.*

## Level Up

**PCs reach Level 9** after Quest 2.3.

**New capabilities:**
- 5th level spells (casters)
- More powerful class features
- Higher stakes combat
- Ready for Act II finale buildup

## New Npcs For Compendium

**Add these:**

1. **Captain Sarah Vale** (Thaldros Informant, CR 3)
2. **General Marcus Thorne** (if survived Quest 2.2, now informant)
3. **Julia Redwind** (Aethoria Informant, CR 3)
4. **Elara Corvus** (Corvus's Daughter, Wizard, CR 4)
5. **Corvus Blackwood (Component-Enhanced)** (CR 11 boss form)

---

## DM Guidance

### **Running The Betrayal**

**Make it hurt:**
- PCs trusted their faction
- Faction genuinely betrayed them
- Not "misunderstanding"â€”real treachery
- Forces difficult decision

**But make it understandable:**
- Factions have logical reasons
- Not "evil for evil's sake"
- Pragmatic but wrong
- Grey, not black

### **The Confrontation Scene**

**Let faction leaders defend themselves:**
- They have reasons
- They're not apologizing
- They believe they're right
- Might even respect PCs for discovering truth

**Don't make them cartoonishly evil:**
- Dawnblade follows orders (lawful evil)
- Valen compromised principles (conflicted good)
- Corvus believes own rhetoric (chaotic neutral)

### **Player Agency**

**All choices are valid:**
- Stay loyal = pragmatic
- Switch sides = adaptive
- Go independent = principled
- Expose corruption = heroic
- Violence = emotional

**Don't judge:**
- Present options
- Show consequences
- Let them decide
- Respect their choice

### **Consequences**

**This choice matters ENORMOUSLY:**
- Determines Quest 2.4-2.5 structure
- Affects Act III options
- Creates permanent allegiances/enemies
- Shapes campaign endgame

**Track carefully:**
- Who they joined
- Who they betrayed
- Who they exposed
- Who died

---

>

# Quest 2.4: The Heist
}}

## Blood & Coin Campaign - Act II

**Level:** 9  
**Duration:** 3-4 sessions  
**Objective:** Infiltrate Royal Vault, steal critical intelligence/artifact/gold  
**Key NPCs:** Rival heist teams, Vault Guardian, faction contacts  
**Rewards:** 3,000-10,000gp + vault contents  
**Theme:** "Ocean's Eleven meets political conspiracy"

---

## Quest Setup

**Time:** Two weeks after Quest 2.3

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*The war is reaching critical mass. Both kingdoms marshaling forces. The Unbound growing bolder. Everyone positioning for the final push.*
>
{{descriptive
*Then word spreads through the underworld: someone's planning to hit the Royal Vault of Kaer Thandros. The most secure location in the kingdom. Impossible to crack. Legendary security.*
>
{{descriptive
*And suddenly, everyone wants in.*
>
{{descriptive
*Your employer (whoever that is now) contacts you with an offer you can't refuse: "The vault contains what we need to win the war. Get it for us. Payment: enough gold to retire. Plus, you keep whatever else you find."*
>
{{descriptive
*This is it. The big score. The heist of the century.*
>
{{descriptive
*Question is: who else is planning the same thing?*

---

## The Royal Vault

### **Location**

**Kaer Thandros Capital Cityâ€”Royal District**

**Description:**

The Royal Vault is built beneath the treasury building, five levels underground. It's been accumulating national treasures for 500 years.

**What's Inside:**

1. **Military Intelligence**
   - Complete battle plans (both kingdoms)
   - Troop movements
   - Supply routes
   - Diplomatic secrets

2. **World-Splitter Component #3**
   - Third of five artifacts
   - Both Corvus and kingdoms want it
   - Worth more than gold

3. **Historical Documents**
   - Proof of Marcus Blackwood's innocence (from Quest 1.5)
   - Evidence of various royal crimes
   - Conspiracy records

4. **Critical: The War Conspiracy**
   - Letters between Thaldros and Aethoria high command
   - Proof war is partially manufactured
   - Both sides coordinated conflict for political gain
   - Real casualties, fake justification

5. **Gold and Treasures**
   - 100,000+ gold pieces
   - Crown jewels
   - Magical artifacts
   - Priceless art

---

## The Mission Briefing

**Your employer (varies) gives orders:**

### **If Working For Thaldros:**

**Commander Dawnblade (if still employed):**
{{descriptive
*"Aethoria intelligence suggests they're targeting the vault. We need you to get there first. Recover our military plans before they do. Also, there's a... component we need. Magical artifact. Retrieve it. Payment: 5,000 gold."*

### **If Working For Aethoria:**

**Envoy Valen (if still employed):**
{{descriptive
*"Thaldros keeps evidence of their crimes in the vaultâ€”including proof of manufactured atrocities. We need those documents to turn public opinion. Also, military intelligence. Payment: 3,000 gold plus whatever you find."*

### **If Working For Unbound:**

**Corvus Blackwood (if still employed):**
{{descriptive
*"Component #3 is in the royal vault. I NEED it. Get it for me. I don't care what else you take. Just bring me the Component. Payment: 2,000 gold plus ancient artifacts."*

### **IF INDEPENDENT:**

**Multiple buyers:**
- Thaldros: 5,000gp for Component + intelligence
- Aethoria: 3,000gp for documents + intelligence
- Unbound: 2,000gp for Component only
- Black Market: 10,000gp for everything (no questions)

**You can choose buyer AFTER the heist**

---

## Phase 1: Intelligence Gathering

**One week to prepare. PCs must gather intel:**

### **Research Checks**

**History DC 14 (Vault Background):**
{{descriptive
*Royal Vault built 300 years ago by dwarf architects. Five levels deep. Never successfully robbed. Three attempted heistsâ€”all thieves executed.*

**Investigation DC 16 (Security Systems):**
{{descriptive
*Five layers of security:*
> 1. *Outer perimeter (guards, patrols)*
> 2. *Magical wards (detect intruders)*
> 3. *Mechanical traps (lethal)*
> 4. *Puzzle locks (ancient dwarven)*
> 5. *Guardian (construct, never seen, only legends)*

**Persuasion DC 15 (Insider Information):**

**If PCs find former guard:**
{{descriptive
*"I worked vault security for five years. Shifts change at midnight. East entrance has blind spot. Wards can be temporarily dispelled if you have the right magic. But the Guardian... that's your real problem. No one knows what it is. Some say dragon. Some say demon. I say: don't find out."*

---

### **Casing The Vault**

**PCs can scout the location:**

**Stealth DC 16 to observe without detection:**

**What they see:**
- Royal Treasury building (above ground)
- 20 **Guards** patrolling (CR 1/8 each)
- 4 **Knights** at main entrance (CR 3 each)
- No obvious entrance to vault (underground)
- Magical shimmer around building (wards)

**Arcana DC 15:**
{{descriptive
*The wards are... impressive. Seventh-level magic. Detect intruders, prevent teleportation, sound alarm if bypassed incorrectly. But they pulse on a cycleâ€”every 10 minutes, there's a 30-second window where they're weakest.*

---

### **Gathering Specialists**

**PCs can recruit specialists for the heist:**

**Available for hire:**

1. **"Fingers" McGee** (Master Thief)
   - Cost: 500gp
   - Skills: Thieves' tools +12, Stealth +10
   - Specialty: Locks and traps

2. **Archmage Elise Ravencroft** (Dispel Expert)
   - Cost: 1,000gp
   - Skills: Arcana +10, can cast *dispel magic* at 7th level
   - Specialty: Magical wards

3. **Professor Aldrich Stone** (Puzzle Scholar)
   - Cost: 300gp
   - Skills: History +12, Intelligence +5
   - Specialty: Dwarven puzzles

4. **"Tank" Ironhide** (Muscle)
   - Cost: 400gp
   - Stats: Barbarian, CR 5
   - Specialty: Combat backup

**PCs can hire 0-4 specialists (costs add up)**

---

## The Rival Teams

**Critical: PCs are NOT the only ones planning this heist.**

**Three other teams targeting vault simultaneously:**

### **Team 1: The Shadows (Professional Thieves)**

**Leader:** **Razor** (Master Thief, CR 8)

**Members:**
- Razor (leader, stealth specialist)
- Whisper (mage, ward expert)
- Lockjaw (locksmith)
- Ghost (scout, invisible)

**Their Plan:**
- Hit vault at midnight
- Use magical invisibility
- Bypass guards via east entrance
- Target: Gold and jewels

**Threat Level:** HIGH (very skilled)

---

### **Team 2: The Fanatics (Unbound Cultists)**

**Leader:** **Brother Ash** (Unbound Priest, CR 7)

**Members:**
- Brother Ash (leader, fanatic)
- 6 Unbound Cultists (CR 2 each)

**Their Plan:**
- Hit vault at midnight (same as everyone)
- Suicidal frontal assault
- Don't care about stealth
- Target: Component #3 only

**Threat Level:** MEDIUM (reckless but dangerous)

---

### **Team 3: The Betrayers (Your Former Faction)**

**If PCs switched sides in Quest 2.3, their OLD faction sends team:**

**Leader:** Varies by former faction:
- **Captain Vale** (if betrayed Thaldros, CR 6)
- **Republican Commandos** (if betrayed Aethoria, CR 6 team)
- **Unbound Assassins** (if betrayed Corvus, CR 7 team)

**Their Plan:**
- Hit vault at midnight
- Specifically targeting YOU for revenge
- Want to ruin your heist
- Target: Whatever you're after

**Threat Level:** HIGH (personal vendetta)

---

## Phase 2: The Plan

**PCs must create heist plan:**

### **Three Approaches**

**Approach 1: Stealth**

**Requirements:**
- High Stealth skills
- Dispel magic capability
- Lock-picking expertise

**Plan:**
- Wait for ward cycle (30-second window)
- Sneak past guards
- Pick locks silently
- Reach vault before alarm

**Advantages:** Avoids combat, stealthy  
**Disadvantages:** One mistake = alarm

---

**Approach 2: Social Engineering**

**Requirements:**
- Disguises
- Forgery skills
- High Deception/Persuasion

**Plan:**
- Forge guard orders
- Disguise as treasury officials
- Talk way inside
- Blend until opportunity

**Advantages:** Guards don't suspect  
**Disadvantages:** Requires multiple successful checks

---

**Approach 3: Distraction**

**Requirements:**
- Create major diversion elsewhere
- Fast entry while guards respond

**Plan:**
- Set fire/explosion in noble district
- Guards respond to emergency
- Vault momentarily undermanned
- Rush in during chaos

**Advantages:** Fewer guards to deal with  
**Disadvantages:** High noise, attracts attention, rival teams might use same window

---

**Approach 4: Magical**

**Requirements:**
- High-level spells
- Teleportation or dimension door
- Dispel magic at 7th+ level

**Plan:**
- Bypass wards magically
- Teleport directly into vault
- Grab and go

**Advantages:** Skips most security  
**Disadvantages:** Wards resist (DC 18), might trigger Guardian

---

**PCs choose approach and execute.**

---

## Phase 3: The Infiltration

### **Getting Inside**

**Based on approach, series of skill challenges:**

**Stealth Approach:**

**Challenge 1: Timing the Ward Cycle**
- Arcana DC 16 to identify exact window
- Stealth DC 17 (group check) to approach during window

**Challenge 2: The East Entrance**
- Thieves' tools DC 18 to pick lock
- Stealth DC 16 to avoid patrolling guard

**Challenge 3: Internal Security**
- Perception DC 15 to spot pressure plate trap
- Acrobatics DC 14 to navigate without triggering

---

**Social Approach:**

**Challenge 1: Forged Documents**
- Forgery kit DC 17 to create convincing orders
- Investigation DC 15 to match official format

**Challenge 2: Talking Past Guards**
- Deception DC 16: "Official inspection, by order of Commander [name]"
- Persuasion DC 18 if they're suspicious

**Challenge 3: Maintaining Cover**
- Performance DC 14 to act like you belong
- Insight DC 13 to read guard suspicion

---

**Distraction Approach:**

**Challenge 1: Creating Diversion**
- Choose: Fire (Arson), Explosion (Demolition), or Riot (Social)
- Stealth DC 14 to set up undetected

**Challenge 2: Timing Entry**
- 3-round window when guards redeploy
- Must reach vault in 3 rounds or alarm triggers

**Challenge 3: Speed Entry**
- Thieves' tools DC 16 but you have disadvantage (rushing)
- Strength DC 15 as alternative (break it)

---

**Magical Approach:**

**Challenge 1: Dispelling Wards**
- *Dispel magic* at 7th level vs DC 18
- Arcana DC 17 to target correct ward layer

**Challenge 2: Teleportation**
- Must know exact vault location (Investigation DC 16)
- Risk: Wrong location = appear in solid stone (instant death)

**Challenge 3: Alarm Suppression**
- Wards sound alarm when teleportation detected
- 2 rounds to suppress or guards arrive

---

## Phase 4: The Vault

### **Level 1-4: Descended Levels**

**Each level has:**
- 1 mechanical trap (Perception DC 15-18)
- 1 magical ward (Arcana DC 14-17)
- 1 puzzle lock (Investigation DC 14-18)

**Summarize descent with 3 skill challenges (one per level)**

---

### **Level 5: The Inner Vault**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*You reach the bottom. The Inner Vault.*
>
{{descriptive
*It's cathedral-sized. Shelves of gold. Display cases of artifacts. Document archives. At the far end: a pedestal with crystalline shard glowing with unnatural lightâ€”Component #3.*
>
{{descriptive
*It's beautiful. Overwhelming. This is the kingdom's heart. 500 years of accumulated wealth and power.*
>
{{descriptive
*And you're not alone.*

---

## The Three-Way Encounter

**All three rival teams arrive simultaneously:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*From the east entrance: The Shadows emerge from invisibility. Four professional thieves, eyes on the gold.*
>
{{descriptive
*From the west stairs: The Fanatics storm in. Six Unbound cultists, chanting Corvus's name, eyes on the Component.*
>
{{descriptive
*From the south passage: [Team 3, your former faction's revenge squad], weapons drawn, eyes on YOU.*
>
{{descriptive
*And standing between everyone and the treasure: something moves in the shadows. The GUARDIAN.*
>
{{descriptive
*This just became very complicated.*

---

## Multi-Faction Combat

**Initiative for Five groups:**

1. **PCs**
2. **The Shadows** (Razor + 3 thieves)
3. **The Fanatics** (Brother Ash + 6 cultists)
4. **The Revenge Squad** (varies by PC history)
5. **The Guardian** (CR 10 construct)

---

### **Enemy: The Shadows**

**Razor** (Assassin, CR 8)  
**AC:** 16 | **HP:** 78 | **Speed:** 40 ft.

**Sneak Attack:** +4d6 damage when has advantage

**Assassinate:** Surprise attacks are automatic crits

**Evasion:** No damage on successful Dex save (half on fail)

**Actions:**
- Multiattack (2 shortsword attacks)
- Shortsword +8 to hit, 1d6+5 + 4d6 sneak attack

**3 Shadow Thieves** (Spy stats, CR 1)

**Their Goal:** Steal gold, avoid fighting if possible

---

### **Enemy: The Fanatics**

**Brother Ash** (Priest, CR 7)  
**AC:** 15 | **HP:** 67 | **Speed:** 30 ft.

**Divine Eminence:** +3 damage to all cleric spells

**Spellcasting (Wis, DC 14):**
- Cantrips: *sacred flame, thaumaturgy*
- 1st: *cure wounds, guiding bolt, shield of faith*
- 2nd: *hold person, spiritual weapon*
- 3rd: *dispel magic, spirit guardians*
- 4th: *guardian of faith*

**6 Unbound Cultists** (Cultist stats, CR 1/8)

**Their Goal:** Get Component #3, kill anyone who interferes

---

### **Enemy: The Revenge Squad**

**Composition varies by PC's Quest 2.3 choice:**

**If betrayed Thaldros:**
- **Captain Sarah Vale** (Knight, CR 6) + 4 Thaldros Guards

**If betrayed Aethoria:**
- **4 Republican Commandos** (Veterans, CR 3 each)

**If betrayed Unbound:**
- **3 Unbound Assassins** (Assassins, CR 5 each)

**Their Goal:** Kill PCs, ruin heist

---

### **Enemy: The Vault Guardian**

## Vault Guardian (CR 10)

*Huge construct, unaligned*

**Armor Class:** 19 (natural armor)  
**Hit Points:** 210 (20d12 + 80)  
**Speed:** 30 ft., fly 30 ft. (hover)

**STR** 24 (+7) | **DEX** 10 (+0) | **CON** 18 (+4)  
**INT** 6 (-2) | **WIS** 12 (+1) | **CHA** 1 (-5)

**Damage Immunities:** poison, psychic; bludgeoning, piercing, slashing from nonmagical attacks  
**Condition Immunities:** charmed, exhaustion, frightened, paralyzed, petrified, poisoned  
**Senses:** darkvision 120 ft., tremorsense 60 ft., passive Perception 11  
**Languages:** understands Common but doesn't speak  
**Challenge:** 10 (5,900 XP)

**Immutable Form:** Immune to form-altering effects

**Magic Resistance:** Advantage on saves vs spells

**Magic Weapons:** Attacks are magical

**Antimagic Vulnerability:** Dispel magic (DC 19) shuts it down for 1 minute

#### Actions

**Multiattack:** Two slam attacks OR one slam + force beam

**Slam:** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +11 to hit, reach 10 ft., one target.  
*Hit:* 25 (4d8 + 7) bludgeoning damage

**Force Beam:** *Ranged Weapon Attack:* +11 to hit, range 120 ft., one target.  
*Hit:* 27 (6d8) force damage. Target must succeed DC 17 Str save or be pushed 20 feet.

**Alarm (Recharge 5-6):** Sounds vault-wide alarm. 20 more guards arrive in 5 rounds.

**Vault Lockdown (1/Day):** Seals all exits for 10 minutes. No teleportation in or out.

#### Tactics

- **Priority:** Defend vault contents
- **First action:** Sound alarm (guards incoming)
- **Second action:** Lockdown vault (trap everyone)
- **Then:** Methodically eliminate intruders
- **Ignores:** Rival teams fighting each other (let them thin themselves)

---

## The Heist Chaos

**This is NOT a traditional combat.**

**Multiple factions, multiple goals, multiple opportunities:**

### **Possible Actions**

**Combat:**
- Fight any/all factions
- Guardian attacks everyone indiscriminately

**Negotiation:**
- Ally with Shadows against Fanatics
- Ally with Fanatics against Shadows
- Ally with anyone against Guardian

**Stealth:**
- Let others fight Guardian
- Sneak to targets while distracted
- Grab and run

**Distraction:**
- Set off false alarms
- Trigger traps on others
- Create chaos, escape in confusion

**Speed:**
- Ignore fighting
- Rush to targets
- Grab what you came for
- Flee immediately

---

## The Targets

**What PCs can steal (limited carrying capacity):**

### **Primary Targets**

**Component #3:**
- Size of football
- 10 lb
- Glows, obvious
- Worth millions
- Multiple factions want it

**Military Intelligence:**
- 20 lb of documents
- Rolled scrolls, leather satchels
- Contains battle plans
- Your employer wants this

**Historical Documents:**
- 30 lb of archives
- Includes Blackwood evidence
- Various political scandals
- High value to right buyers

**THE WAR CONSPIRACY:**
- Single folder, 2 lb
- Letters between kingdoms
- Proof war is manufactured
- EXPLOSIVE if revealed

---

### **Secondary Targets**

**Gold:**
- Literally tons
- Can carry ~100 lb = 5,000gp
- Heavy but valuable

**Crown Jewels:**
- Display case, 20 lb total
- Worth 10,000gp
- Symbolic theft

**Magic Items:**
- Various (see list below)
- Can take 2-3 items
- Powerful but limited space

---

### **Magic Items Available**

**In display cases (choose wisely):**

1. **Defender Longsword** (+3 weapon, Very Rare)
2. **Staff of Power** (Very Rare)
3. **Ring of Spell Storing** (Rare)
4. **Cloak of Invisibility** (Legendary)
5. **Amulet of Health** (Rare, Con = 19)
6. **Belt of Giant Strength (Frost)** (Very Rare, Str = 23)

**Can only take 2-3 items due to carrying capacity + everything else**

---

## The Discovery

**If PCs examine documents carefully:**

**Investigation DC 14 (while in vault):**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Among the military intelligence, you find something... unexpected. Letters. Correspondence between Thaldros high command and Aethoria military leadership.*
>
{{descriptive
*You read with growing horror:*
>
{{descriptive
*"Agreed. Naval skirmishes will justify military buildup. Casualties acceptable. Public opinion will demand action."*
>
{{descriptive
*"Confirmed. Assassination attempt staged. Blame enemy. This should suffice for war declaration."*
>
{{descriptive
*"War serves both our interests. Thaldros consolidates power through emergency measures. Aethoria senate suspends elections. We both win."*
>
{{descriptive
*(Date: Three years agoâ€”before war started)*
>
{{descriptive
*The war was manufactured. Coordinated. Both kingdoms working together to create conflict for political gain.*
>
{{descriptive
*The casualties are real. The justification is fake.*

**This is the BIG reveal.**

---

## The Choice

**PCs must decide what to take:**

**Carrying Capacity:**
- Average PC: ~100 lb capacity
- 5-person party: ~500 lb total
- Must prioritize

**What TO Take:**

**Option 1: Component #3** (10 lb)
- Fulfill mission for Corvus
- Or sell to highest bidder
- Or destroy (prevent apocalypse)

**Option 2: Military Intelligence** (20 lb)
- Fulfill mission for kingdom
- Or sell to enemy
- Win the war

**Option 3: War Conspiracy Docs** (2 lb)
- Expose the truth
- Reveal both kingdoms' lies
- End war OR cause chaos

**Option 4: Gold** (100 lb per PC = ~5,000gp each)
- Immediate wealth
- No political consequences
- Pure mercenary choice

**Option 5: Magic Items** (2-3 items)
- Personal power
- Very valuable
- Legendary gear

**Option 6: Everything (Impossible)**
- Can't carry all
- Must choose priorities
- Reveals what you value

**Most parties take: War Conspiracy (2 lb) + Component OR Intelligence (10-20 lb) + some gold (remaining capacity)**

---

## The Escape

**Once targets acquired:**

### **Getting Out**

**Guardian tries to stop everyone:**
- Lockdown activated (exits sealed)
- Must defeat OR bypass Guardian
- 20 guards incoming (ETA: 5 rounds)

**Escape Options:**

**Option 1: Fight Through**
- Defeat Guardian (CR 10, tough)
- Fight guards (20+ CR 1/8)
- Bloody but straightforward

**Option 2: Dispel Lockdown**
- Arcana DC 19 to counter lockdown
- Then flee before guards arrive

**Option 3: Teleportation**
- *Dimension door*, *teleport*, etc.
- Wards are down (breach opened)
- Must know safe exit point

**Option 4: Hostage**
- Grab noble/official
- Use as leverage
- Negotiate safe passage

**Option 5: Blame Someone Else**
- Frame rival team
- Plant evidence
- Escape in confusion

---

## Aftermath

**Once escaped:**

### **The DECISION**

**What do you do with what you stole?**

**The War Conspiracy Documents:**

**Option A: Expose Everything**
- Go public with documents
- Reveal war is manufactured
- Major political scandal

**Consequences:**
- Both kingdoms embarrassed
- War might end (50% chance)
- Or both governments double down (50%)
- You're heroes to common folk
- Hunted by both governments
- Massive political upheaval

---

**Option B: Sell to Highest Bidder**
- Blackmail both kingdoms
- Demand payment for silence
- Keep war going but profit

**Consequences:**
- 20,000gp from BOTH kingdoms (40k total)
- You're complicit in conspiracy
- War continues
- Gold-rich but morally bankrupt

---

**Option C: Destroy Documents**
- Burn evidence
- Maintain status quo
- "Some truths are too dangerous"

**Consequences:**
- War continues as planned
- Nothing changes
- You could have stopped it but didn't
- Guilt or pragmatism (player choice)

---

**Option D: Give to One Kingdom**
- Strengthen one side
- Help them win war
- Keep conspiracy secret

**Consequences:**
- 10,000gp from chosen kingdom
- That kingdom wins war
- Conspiracy stays hidden
- You've picked the winning side

---

**Component #3:**

**Similar choices:**
- Give to Corvus (enable apocalypse)
- Give to kingdom (weaponize it)
- Keep it (corruption risk)
- Destroy it (world safer)

---

## Rewards

**Based on choices:**

**If sold everything to employers:**
- 5,000-10,000gp
- Faction reputation +10
- Mission complete

**If kept loot:**
- 5,000gp in gold
- 2-3 magic items
- War Conspiracy docs (priceless)
- Component #3 (dangerous)

**If exposed conspiracy:**
- 0gp (no buyers)
- Reputation: +20 with common folk
- Reputation: -20 with both governments
- Hunted but heroic

---

## Level Up

**PCs reach Level 10** after Quest 2.4.

**Major milestone:**
- Tier 3 play begins
- Access to 6th level spells
- Extra Attack (third) for fighters
- Powerful class abilities
- Ready for Act II finale

---

# Quest 2.5: The Breaking Point

## Blood & Coin Campaign - Act II Finale

**Level:** 10  
**Duration:** 3-4 sessions  
**Objective:** War beginsâ€”or is prevented (PCs decide outcome)  
**Key NPCs:** All major faction leaders, armies, your allies  
**Rewards:** 2,000-10,000gp + faction rewards + Act III setup  
**Theme:** "Blood or peace?"

---

## Quest Setup

**Time:** Two months after Quest 2.4

**What's Happened:**
- The heist sent shockwaves through both kingdoms
- Your Quest 2.4 choices had consequences
- War preparations accelerated
- Both armies now at the border
- Zero hour: Tomorrow at dawn

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Two months since the heist. Two months of escalation.*
>
{{descriptive
*Every choice you made across Act II led here: The Border of Judgment, where Thaldros and Aethoria armies face each other across one mile of no-man's-land.*
>
{{descriptive
*Thaldros: 10,000 soldiers, siege weapons, royal banner flying. Order through strength.*
>
{{descriptive
*Aethoria: 8,000 soldiers, guerrilla fighters, republican flags waving. Freedom through blood.*
>
{{descriptive
*The Unbound: Hidden cells throughout, waiting for chaos. Salvation through apocalypse.*
>
{{descriptive
*And you: mercenaries who've seen behind the curtain. You know the truth. You know the lies. You know what hangs in the balance.*
>
{{descriptive
*War begins at dawn. Unless you stop it. Or unless you decide one side must win.*
>
{{descriptive
*This is the breaking point. The choice that defines Act III.*
>
{{descriptive
*What will you do?*

---

## The Five Possible Outcomes

**Based on PC actions in this quest:**

1. **thaldros victory** - Monarchy wins, tyranny spreads
2. **aethoria victory** - Republic wins, democracy prevails
3. **unbound apocalypse** - Corvus succeeds, reality reshaped
4. **peace achieved** - War prevented, fragile coexistence
5. **total war** - Stalemate, endless conflict

**PCs' choices THIS QUEST determine which occurs.**

---

# ðŸ° Path 1: Thaldros Victory

**If PCs choose to fight for Thaldros:**

## The Battle

### **Deployment**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Dawn breaks. You stand with Thaldros vanguardâ€”500 elite soldiers. Commander Dawnblade briefs you:*
>
{{descriptive
*"Aethoria's left flank is weak. Volunteers, poor training. Break through there. Collapse their line. Victory is ours. You lead the charge. For the kingdom!"*
>
{{descriptive
*Behind you: 10,000 Thaldros soldiers.*  
{{descriptive
*Across the field: 8,000 Republican defenders.*  
{{descriptive
*Above: Carrion birds, waiting.*

---

### **Phase 1: The CHARGE**

**PCs lead 500 soldiers against Aethoria left flank:**

**Encounter:**
- 300 **Aethoria Militia** (Commoner stats, CR 0, poorly trained)
- 50 **Republican Veterans** (Guard stats, CR 1/8)
- 1 **Republican Commander** (Knight stats, CR 3)

**This is a massacre.**

**PCs can:**
- **Fight honorably:** Kill only soldiers, spare surrendering
- **Fight ruthlessly:** Kill everyone, break morale faster
- **Show mercy:** Try to minimize casualties (harder)

**Combat Summary (not every soldier):**
- Militia breaks after 50% casualties
- Veterans fight to last man
- Commander demands single combat (PC can accept)

**If PCs win:**
- Left flank collapses
- Thaldros floods through breach
- Aethoria line crumbles

---

### **Phase 2: The PURSUIT**

**Aethoria forces retreat:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*They're running. Aethoria soldiers fleeing in disarray. Dawnblade orders: "Pursue! No quarter! End this!"*
>
{{descriptive
*You see them: terrified young soldiers, farmers with spears, people who believed in democracy. Running for their lives.*
>
{{descriptive
*Orders are orders. But...*

**The Choice:**

**Option A: Follow Orders**
- Pursue and kill retreating soldiers
- War crime but effective
- Aethoria routed completely
- Thaldros victory assured

**Option B: Show Mercy**
- Let them retreat
- Disobey orders
- Dawnblade furious but battle won anyway

---

### **Phase 3: The Final Stand**

**Aethoria makes last stand at command tent:**

**Boss Fight:**

**Envoy Valen (if alive) + Republican Champions:**

**Envoy Valen** (CR 6, as previous stats)  
**4 Republican Champions** (Veteran stats, CR 3 each)

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Valen stands defiant, bloody, defeated but not broken:*
>
{{descriptive
*"So. You chose tyranny. I hope it's everything you dreamed. When the king turns on youâ€”and he willâ€”remember this moment. Remember you had a choice."*

**PCs can:**
- **Kill them:** Complete victory, no mercy
- **Capture them:** Take prisoners, war trials later
- **Let them flee:** Final mercy (Dawnblade will be angry)

---

### **Outcome: Thaldros Victory**

**If Thaldros wins:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Aethoria falls. Republic collapses. Democracy dies on this field.*
>
{{descriptive
*Thaldros banners fly over captured territory. Valen executed (if captured). Survivors flee to distant lands.*
>
{{descriptive
*You're heroes of the kingdom. Commander Dawnblade promotes you. King grants titles, lands, gold.*
>
{{descriptive
*But walking through the battlefield afterward, you see: 3,000 dead. Mostly Aethoria militiaâ€”farmers, shopkeepers, people who believed freedom was worth fighting for.*
>
{{descriptive
*You helped create this. You helped tyranny win.*
>
{{descriptive
*Was it worth it?*

**Rewards:**
- 5,000gp
- Lands and titles (become landed nobility)
- Reputation: +20 with Thaldros
- Reputation: -30 with Aethoria survivors
- **ACT III Path A: THALDROS VICTORY**

### **Phase 1: The DEFENSE**

**Thaldros charges:**

**Encounter:**
- 200 **Thaldros Heavy Infantry** (Guard stats, CR 1/8)
- 20 **Thaldros Knights** (Knight stats, CR 3)
- 1 **Commander** (Veteran, CR 5)

**PCs lead defensive position:**

**Tactics:**
- Use terrain (trenches, barriers)
- Focus fire on knights
- Hold the line

**This is desperate defense.**

**If PCs hold 5 rounds:**
- Thaldros assault breaks
- First wave repelled
- Morale boost for Aethoria

---

### **Phase 2: The COUNTER-ATTACK**

**Valen orders guerrilla strike:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*"While they regroup, we strike their supply lines. Their siege weapons. Their command tent. Guerrilla warfare. This is how we winâ€”not by matching their strength, but by attacking their weaknesses."*

**PCs lead strike team:**

**Mission Options (choose 2 of 3):**

1. **Destroy Siege Weapons**
   - Stealth mission to Thaldros rear
   - Sabotage 6 trebuchets
   - Prevents bombardment

2. **Assassinate Commander**
   - Infiltrate command tent
   - Kill/capture Dawnblade
   - Decapitate leadership

3. **Free Prisoners**
   - Liberate captured Republicans
   - Boost morale
   - Gain reinforcements

**Each mission: 2-3 skill challenges + 1 combat encounter**

**If succeed both:**
- Thaldros momentum broken
- Aethoria gains initiative

>
{{descriptive
*(She raises her sword)*
>
{{descriptive

**PCs can:**
- **Kill her:** Symbolic victory, no mercy
- **Force surrender:** Take prisoner, use as leverage
- **Let her retreat:** Honorable combat

# ðŸ”¥ Path 3: Unbound Apocalypse

## The Heist During Battle

### **The Plan**

**Corvus explains:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive

>
{{descriptive
*You infiltrate both sides during battle chaos. Steal both Components. Bring them to me. I'll perform the ritual.*

{{descriptive
*Tomorrow, we remake the world. No more war. No more suffering. Perfection.*
>
{{descriptive
*(His eyes are wild, intense)*
>
{{descriptive
*This is what we've worked for. This is salvation."*

---

### **Phase 1: STEAL COMPONENT #4 (Thaldros King)**

**Infiltrate Thaldros royal command:**

**Challenges:**
- Disguise as Thaldros soldiers (Deception DC 16)
- Reach royal pavilion during battle (Stealth DC 17)
- Bypass King's Honor Guard (6 Knights, CR 3)
- Steal Component from King's person (Sleight of Hand DC 20 or combat)

**Encounter:**

**King Aldric IV** (CR 9, uses Archmage stats with protection spells)

**PCs can:**
- **Stealth steal:** Pickpocket during battle chaos
- **Combat:** Fight King and guards
- **Deception:** Trick him into giving it up

---

### **Phase 2: STEAL COMPONENT #5 (Aethoria General)**

**Infiltrate Aethoria command:**

**Challenges:**
- Navigate battle (Survival DC 15)
- Reach Aethoria command tent (Stealth DC 16)
- Bypass Republican Guards (8 Veterans, CR 3)
- Steal Component from General (Sleight of Hand DC 19 or combat)

**Encounter:**

**General Marcus Vale** (CR 7, uses Champion stats)

**PCs can:**
- **Stealth steal:** While General commands troops
- **Combat:** Assassinate General, take Component
- **Persuasion:** Convince him to give it up (nearly impossible)

---

### **Phase 3: The RITUAL**

**Deliver Components to Corvus:**

{{descriptive

{{descriptive
*"Perfect. PERFECT! Now, the ritual. Reality will bend. The world will change. Humanity will be saved."*
>
{{descriptive
*(He begins arranging Components in circleâ€”intricate pattern, glowing with power)*
>
{{descriptive
*"When I activate this, 30-40% of population will die. Necessary sacrifice. The rest will enter new world order. No free will, but no suffering. Perfect peace. Perfect control."*
>
{{descriptive
*(He looks at you)*
>
{{descriptive
*"Are you with me? Or do you lack the courage to save humanity?"*

---

### **The Final Choice**

**PCs must decide:**

**Option A: LET RITUAL COMPLETE**

**Corvus succeeds:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Corvus chants. Components pulse with power. Reality TEARS.*
>
{{descriptive

>

>

>
{{descriptive
*The old world dies. The new world is born.*

**Outcome: UNBOUND APOCALYPSE**

**Consequences:**
- 35% of world population dies (instant)
- Remaining 65% lose free will
- Corvus rules as Archon
- You're Wardens (governors of regions)
- Perfect order, zero freedom
- **ACT III Path C: UNBOUND APOCALYPSE**

**Rewards:**
- 2,000gp (symbolic, money is meaningless now)
- Position as Warden
- Power over thousands
- Haunted by what you've done

---

**Option B: STOP THE RITUAL**

**Fight Corvus:**

**Final Boss Fight:**

## Corvus Blackwood (Ascended)

*Medium humanoid (human), chaotic neutral - CR 13*

**Armor Class:** 20 (enhanced by all 5 Components)  
**Hit Points:** 180 (augmented)  
**Speed:** 30 ft., fly 60 ft. (Components grant flight)

**STR** 10 (+0) | **DEX** 18 (+4) | **CON** 16 (+3)  
**INT** 22 (+6) | **WIS** 16 (+3) | **CHA** 18 (+4)

**Saving Throws:** Int +11, Wis +8, Cha +9  
**Skills:** Arcana +16, History +16  
**Damage Resistances:** all damage from spells  
**Condition Immunities:** charmed, frightened  
**Senses:** truesight 120 ft., passive Perception 13  
**Languages:** All  
**Challenge:** 13 (10,000 XP)

**Component-Enhanced:** Can cast any spell 7th level or lower without spell slots

**Reality Anchor:** Cannot be moved, banished, or teleported against will

**Legendary Resistance (3/Day):** Can choose to succeed failed save

#### Actions

**Multiattack:** Three *reality beam* attacks

**Reality Beam:** *Ranged Spell Attack:* +11 to hit, range 120 ft., one target.  
*Hit:* 28 (8d6) force damage. Target must succeed DC 19 Wis save or be stunned until end of Corvus's next turn.

**Reshape Reality (Recharge 5-6):** 60-ft. radius. All creatures make DC 19 Charisma save or take 10d10 psychic damage and be transported to harmless demiplane for 1 minute.

**Component Blast (1/Day):** Releases stored energy. 120-ft. cone. DC 19 Dex save, 20d6 force damage (half on success).

#### Legendary Actions

**Corvus takes 3 legendary actions, choosing from options below:**

**Teleport:** Teleports up to 60 feet

**Cast Spell (Costs 2):** Casts spell 5th level or lower

**Reality Warp (Costs 3):** Changes battlefield terrain dramatically

#### Tactics

- **First Round:** *Time stop*, position Components
- **Second Round:** Begin ritual (takes 3 rounds total)
- **While Casting:** Uses legendary actions to defend
- **If Interrupted:** Goes all-out offensive
- **Desperate:** Uses Component Blast (destroys Components but might win)

---

**IF PCs defeat Corvus:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Corvus falls. Components shatter. Reality snaps back like a released bowstring.*
>
{{descriptive
*The ritual fails. The world remains unchanged. Free will intact. Suffering continues.*
>
{{descriptive
*(Corvus, dying)*
>
{{descriptive
*"You... you doomed them. Humanity could have been perfect. Now... now they'll suffer forever. You... chose..."*
>
{{descriptive
*(He dies)*
>
{{descriptive
*Outside, the war continues. Nothing changed. Except you stopped an apocalypse. Maybe that's enough.*

**Outcome: PREVENTED APOCALYPSE**

**Consequences:**
- Corvus dead
- Components destroyed
- Unbound collapses
- War continues (returns to Path 1, 2, or 4)
- World saved from "salvation"
- No payment (killed employer)

**But:** Prevents Unbound ending. Must choose different Act III path.

---

# â˜®ï¸ Path 4: Peace Achieved

**If PCs try to prevent war entirely:**

## The Diplomatic Mission

### **The CHALLENGE**

**Stopping war requires:**

1. Expose war conspiracy (from Quest 2.4 documents)
2. Convince both sides to stand down
3. Broker peace treaty
4. Survive assassination attempts from warmongers

**This is the HARDEST path.**

---

### **Phase 1: Expose The Conspiracy**

**PCs must reveal truth publicly:**

**Options:**

**Option A: Public Speech**
- Speak to both armies simultaneously
- Show war conspiracy documents
- Persuasion DC 20 (difficult)

**Option B: Command Infiltration**
- Give documents to both commanders privately
- Let them see truth
- Persuasion DC 18 per commander

**Option C: Mass Distribution**
- Copy documents, spread everywhere
- Public can't ignore truth
- Printing/distribution 1 day + 500gp

---

### **Phase 2: Negotiation**

**If conspiracy exposed, both sides shocked:**

**Meeting of Leaders:**

**Attendees:**
- Commander Dawnblade (Thaldros)
- Envoy Valen (Aethoria)
- PCs (mediators)
- Witnesses

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Neutral tent. Two enemies sit across from each other. Documents between themâ€”proof of conspiracy.*
>
{{descriptive
*Dawnblade: "This... this is real? High command manufactured this war?"*
>
{{descriptive
*Valen: "Our senate too. We've been played. Both of us."*
>
{{descriptive
*(They look at each otherâ€”first time seeing shared victimhood)*
>
{{descriptive
*Dawnblade: "So what now? Do we fight knowing it's a lie?"*
>
{{descriptive
*You have a chance. Broker peace.*

---

### **Negotiation Rounds**

**Four rounds of Persuasion checks:**

**Round 1: Ceasefire**
- DC 16: Convince both to stop fighting TODAY
- Success: Temporary ceasefire
- Failure: Negotiations collapse, return to war

**Round 2: Terms**
- DC 17: Define peace treaty terms
- Success: Border status quo, trade agreement
- Failure: Can't agree on territory

**Round 3: Justice**
- DC 18: What happens to conspirators?
- Success: Joint tribunal, public trials
- Failure: Each side protects own criminals

**Round 4: Future**
- DC 19: Long-term coexistence plan
- Success: Permanent peace treaty, alliance
- Failure: Temporary truce only

**Required: All 4 rounds successful for lasting peace**

**3 or fewer: Temporary truce (eventually fails)**

---

### **Phase 3: Assassination Attempts**

**Warmongers from both sides try to kill you:**

**Encounters:**

**Attempt 1: Thaldros Hardliners**
- 4 Royal Assassins (Assassin stats, CR 8)
- Want war to continue
- Attack during negotiations

**Attempt 2: Aethoria Radicals**
- 6 Republican Extremists (Veteran stats, CR 3)
- Believe compromise is betrayal
- Attack at treaty signing

**Attempt 3: Unbound Saboteurs**
- Corvus's agents (if he's alive)
- War serves his chaos goals
- Bomb attempt (DC 18 Investigation to find, DC 20 Thieves' tools to disarm)

**Must survive all three to complete peace**

---

### **Outcome: Peace Achieved**

**If all negotiations successful AND survived assassinations:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Two months later. Treaty of Judgment Border signed. War ends. Ceasefire holds.*
>
{{descriptive
*It's fragile. Hardliners on both sides grumble. Tensions remain. But no one's dying today.*
>
{{descriptive
*You brokered peace. Ended a war. Saved thousands of lives.*
>
{{descriptive
*Statues erected in your honor. Songs sung. "The Peacemakers," they call you.*
>
{{descriptive
*But you know the truth: Peace requires constant maintenance. One wrong move and it shatters. You'll spend Act III defending what you built.*
>
{{descriptive
*Was it worth it? Ask the people who didn't die.*

**Outcome: PEACE ACHIEVED**

**Rewards:**
- 3,000gp (from grateful citizens' fund)
- Reputation: +30 with common folk
- Reputation: +10 with moderate leaders
- Reputation: -20 with hardliners (both sides)
- Title: "Peacemaker"
- **ACT III Path D: FRAGILE PEACE**

**This is the "best" endingâ€”but hardest to achieve and maintain.**

---

# âš”ï¸ Path 5: Total War

**If PCs do nothing or fail to tip balance:**

## The Stalemate

**War begins. PCs stay neutral or choose no side:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*War begins at dawn. You watch from hillside as armies clash.*
>
{{descriptive
*Thaldros cavalry charges. Aethoria pikes hold. Siege weapons fire. Magic flares. Thousands die.*
>
{{descriptive
*By sunset: Stalemate. Neither side wins. Both sides bloodied.*
>
{{descriptive
*This repeats. Day after day. Week after week. Month after month.*
>
{{descriptive
*You're mercenaries. You survive. But the war? It never ends.*

---

### **Phase 1-3: Endless Battle**

**PCs can fight for either side as freelancers:**

**Per battle engagement:**
- 1-2 combat encounters
- 500-1,000gp payment
- XP and exhaustion

**But no resolution. No victory. Just grinding attrition.**

---

### **Outcome: Total War**

**If neither side wins:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Six months later. War continues. Casualty count: 15,000+ dead. No end in sight.*
>
{{descriptive
*Both kingdoms bleeding resources. Neither willing to surrender. Pride and sunk costs keep it going.*
>
{{descriptive
*Mercenary work is plentiful. Tragic but profitable. You're wealthy but exhausted. And the war? It'll outlive you.*
>
{{descriptive
*This is the worst timeline. No winner. Only losers. And you didn't stop it.*

**Outcome: TOTAL WAR**

**Rewards:**
- 2,000gp (mercenary payments)
- Reputation: Neutral with both (neither trusts you)
- Title: "The Survivor"
- **ACT III Path E: TOTAL WAR**

**This is the "bad" endingâ€”but it's what happens when heroes don't act.**

---

## Act II Ending

**Regardless of outcome:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Act II: Power Plays is over. You made your choices. The war is decidedâ€”one way or another.*
>
{{descriptive
*Act III begins one year later. The consequences of your decisions have reshaped Tirvandor. For better or worse.*
>
{{descriptive
*(Pause for effect)*
>
{{descriptive
*What kind of world did you create?*

---

## Level Up & Transition

**PCs reach Level 11** at end of Quest 2.5

**Tier 3 fully unlocked:**
- 6th level spells
- Powerful class features
- Regional influence
- Ready for Act III

---

## Act II Complete Summary

### **What PCs Accomplished:**

**Quest 2.1:** Chose faction  
**Quest 2.2:** Proved loyalty  
**Quest 2.3:** Discovered betrayal  
**Quest 2.4:** Heisted Royal Vault  
**Quest 2.5:** Determined war outcome  

### **Total Possible Gold (Act II):**

**Conservative:** 8,000-15,000gp  
**Optimal:** 20,000-40,000gp  
**Maximum (if exploited all sides):** 50,000+ gp

### **Reputation Earned:**

Varies wildly by choices:
- Hero to some, villain to others
- Respected or hunted
- Legend or cautionary tale

### **Act III Setup:**

**Five possible campaign states:**
1. Thaldros Victory (tyranny)
2. Aethoria Victory (democracy)
3. Unbound Apocalypse (new world)
4. Fragile Peace (coexistence)
5. Total War (stalemate)

**Each leads to different Act III**

---

## DM Guidance

### **Running the Finale**

**Make it EPIC:**
- This is Act II climax
- Armies, magic, politics
- Everything players did matters
- High stakes, high drama

**But keep it personal:**
- Focus on PCs' actions
- Don't get lost in armies (abstract large battles)
- Individual choices matter
- Their story, not generals' story

### **The Five Outcomes**

**Present all as equally valid:**
- No "correct" ending
- Each has costs and benefits
- PCs choose based on values
- All paths lead to Act III

**Track everything:**
- Which outcome occurred
- Who lived/died
- What was revealed
- What remains hidden
- This determines all of Act III

### **Player Agency**

**Ultimate test:**
- Can PCs broker peace? (Path 4)
- Or do they choose a side? (Paths 1-2)
- Or enable apocalypse? (Path 3)
- Or do nothing? (Path 5)

**All are valid choices.**

**Respect their decision and show consequences honestly.**

---

## Transition TO Act III

**One year passes.**

**Opening of Act III:**

{{descriptive
*"One year since the Breaking Point. The war's outcome has reshaped everything. You live now in the world you created.*
>
{{descriptive
*Act III: Empire of Ashes. Living with consequences. Defendingâ€”or regrettingâ€”your choices.*
>
{{descriptive
*Was it worth it?"*

**[ACT III begins based on Act II outcome]**

**Moral complexity:** MAXIMUM

{{wide
# Quest 3.1: The Peacekeepers
}}

## Blood & Coin Campaign - Act III (Peace Path)

**Level:** 11  
**Duration:** 2-3 sessions  
**Objective:** Mediate three disputes threatening the peace treaty  
**Key NPCs:** Dawnblade, Valen, border officials, extremists  
**Rewards:** 2,000gp + reputation as Peacemakers  
**Theme:** "Peace requires constant vigilance"

---

## Act III Opening

**Time:** One year after Act II finale

**The State of the World:**

You achieved the impossible in Act IIâ€”you stopped the war. You exposed the conspiracy, forced both kingdoms to the negotiating table, and brokered the Treaty of Judgment Border.

But peace is fragile. Daily.

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*One year has passed since you prevented the war. The Treaty of Judgment Border holdsâ€”barely.*
>
{{descriptive
*The frontier territories exist in uneasy peace with the Crown. Trade resumed. Prisoners exchanged. Diplomatic relations established. From the outside, it looks like peace.*
>
{{descriptive
*From the inside? You know better. You're the official Peacekeepersâ€”neutral mediators appointed by both kingdoms. Every week brings new crises. Border disputes. Trade disagreements. Assassination attempts. Diplomatic incidents.*
>
{{descriptive
*You prevent them. One crisis at a time. One day at a time. It's exhausting.*
>
{{descriptive
*But today is worse than usual. Three separate incidents. Same day. All threatening to reignite the war.*
>
{{descriptive
*This is your life now. Welcome to Level 11. Welcome to Act III.*

---

## The Three Crises

**All three occur simultaneously. PCs must prioritize:**

---

## Crisis 1: The Border Incident

**Location:** Judgment Border Checkpoint

**What Happened:**

Thaldros guards killed an Aethoria merchant they claim was smuggling weapons. Aethoria says he was unarmed, carrying legal trade goods. Both sides mobilizing troops.

### **Arrival**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*You arrive at the border checkpoint to find 50 Thaldros soldiers on one side, 40 Aethoria militia on the other. The dead merchant's body lies in no-man's-land. No one will retrieve itâ€”crossing the line might spark violence.*
>
{{descriptive
*Thaldros Captain: "He was smuggling swords! We have every right to enforce border security!"*
>
{{descriptive
*Aethoria Lieutenant: "You murdered an unarmed civilian! This is an act of war!"*
>
{{descriptive
*Weapons drawn. Fingers on triggers. One wrong word and this explodes.*

---

### **Investigation**

**PCs can investigate the scene:**

**Perception DC 16 (examining body from distance):**
{{descriptive
*The merchant has no visible weapons. His cart contains... textiles? Cloth bolts. No swords visible.*

**Medicine DC 14:**
{{descriptive
*Crossbow bolt to the back. He was fleeing, not attacking.*

**Investigation DC 17 (examining cart closely):**
{{descriptive
*Hidden compartment. Empty. But residue suggests swords WERE here recently. Someone removed them.*

**Insight DC 15 (reading soldiers):**
{{descriptive
*Thaldros captain looks nervous. He's hiding something. Aethoria lieutenant is genuinely enragedâ€”believes merchant was innocent.*

---

### **The TRUTH**

**If PCs investigate thoroughly:**

**Perception DC 18 (searching area):**
{{descriptive
*Fresh wagon tracks leading away from checkpoint. Someone else was here. Recently.*

**Survival DC 16 (tracking):**
{{descriptive
*Tracks lead to nearby woods. You find: abandoned cart with 20 swords. Thaldros military issue.*

**The Truth:**
- Merchant WAS smuggling (Thaldros correct)
- BUT Thaldros guards PLANTED the swords (framed him)
- Then killed him when he discovered the frame job
- Third party (unknown) removed evidence to hide the setup

**Someone wanted this incident to spark war.**

---

### **The RESOLUTION**

**PCs must decide:**

**Option 1: Expose Thaldros Frame Job**
- Confront Thaldros captain with evidence
- Public admission of murder
- Thaldros embarrassed but truth revealed
- **Persuasion DC 18** to get captain to confess

**If successful:**
- Thaldros apologizes formally
- Captain arrested
- Aethoria satisfied
- Peace holds
- **Reward:** Reputation +5 with Aethoria, +2 with Thaldros (transparency)

**If failed:**
- Thaldros denies everything
- Both sides stay angry
- Tension remains high

---

**Option 2: Blame Third Party**
- Present evidence of unknown wagon
- Suggest someone framed BOTH sides
- Shift anger toward mutual enemy
- **Persuasion DC 16** (easier, shared enemy unites)

**If successful:**
- Both sides agree to joint investigation
- Cooperation instead of confrontation
- Peace holds
- But truth remains hidden
- **Reward:** Reputation +3 with both kingdoms

---

**Option 3: Peaceful Lie**
- Claim merchant was innocent, hide evidence
- Demand Thaldros compensate family
- Political solution, not truth
- **Deception DC 18**

**If successful:**
- Thaldros pays blood money
- Aethoria satisfied
- Peace holds
- But Thaldros resentful
- **Reward:** Reputation +5 Aethoria, -2 Thaldros

---

**Option 4: Escalate**
- Refuse to mediate
- Let them fight it out
- **This breaks the peace**
- Fail quest, war resumes

---

## Crisis 2: The Trade Dispute

**Location:** Port City of Seahaven (neutral ground)

**What Happened:**

Aethoria merchant ship seized by Thaldros navy for "illegal goods." Aethoria demands release. Thaldros refuses. Both threaten embargo.

### **The SITUATION**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Seahaven Port. The merchant ship "Liberty's Call" sits anchored, Thaldros navy blockading it. Aethoria diplomats argue with Thaldros admirals on the dock. Merchants on both sides watching nervouslyâ€”if trade stops, everyone loses money.*
>
{{descriptive
*Thaldros Admiral: "The ship carries Unbound propaganda. Books. Pamphlets. Cult materials. We can't allow that poison into our kingdom."*
>
{{descriptive
*Aethoria Diplomat: "Freedom of speech! We don't censor! Release the ship or we close ALL trade!"*
>
{{descriptive
*Merchant guilds are panicking. If trade stops, both economies suffer. But neither side will back down.*

---

### **Investigation**

**Persuasion DC 15 to board the ship:**

**What PCs find:**
- 200 crates of legitimate trade goods
- 5 crates of books (Unbound philosophy)
- Books are: Critical of monarchy AND democracy
- Call for "new order" (Corvus-style rhetoric)
- NOT illegal in Aethoria (free speech)
- VERY illegal in Thaldros (sedition)

**Investigation DC 16:**
{{descriptive
*The books were loaded by someone named "Brother Ash"â€”Unbound member. He's listed as passenger, not crew.*

**Insight DC 14:**
{{descriptive
*This isn't about the books. Thaldros wants excuse to flex power. Aethoria wants excuse to resist. Both testing the treaty.*

---

### **The TRUTH**

**If PCs dig deeper:**

**Investigation DC 18 (ship manifest):**
{{descriptive
*Brother Ash paid 500gp to load books. Ship captain didn't know contents. He's innocent. Books were smuggled aboard.*

**Unbound are testing the peace.** If kingdoms fight over books, war resumes. Unbound wins.

---

### **The RESOLUTION**

**Option 1: Confiscate Books, Release Ship**
- Compromise: Remove illegal cargo, release ship
- Neither side wins completely
- **Persuasion DC 16** to get both to agree

**If successful:**
- Trade continues
- Thaldros gets security
- Aethoria maintains trade
- Peace holds
- **Reward:** Reputation +3 both kingdoms

---

**Option 2: Defend Free Speech**
- Argue books are legal in international waters
- Force Thaldros to release ship
- **Persuasion DC 18** (harder, challenges Thaldros authority)

**If successful:**
- Ship released with books
- Aethoria celebrates victory
- Thaldros resentful
- Peace holds but strained
- **Reward:** Reputation +5 Aethoria, -3 Thaldros

---

**Option 3: Support Seizure**
- Agree books are dangerous
- Ship stays seized
- **Persuasion DC 17** (need to convince Aethoria)

**If successful:**
- Thaldros keeps ship
- Aethoria backs down
- Peace holds but strained
- **Reward:** Reputation +5 Thaldros, -3 Aethoria

---

**Option 4: Expose Unbound Plot**
- Reveal Brother Ash smuggled books
- Frame as Unbound sabotage
- Unite kingdoms against shared enemy
- **Investigation DC 17 to find Brother Ash**

**If successful:**
- Both kingdoms cooperate
- Hunt Unbound together
- Peace strengthened
- **Reward:** Reputation +5 both kingdoms
- **Bonus:** Lead to Brother Ash (can arrest/question)

---

## Crisis 3: The Assassination Attempt

**Location:** Diplomatic Summit (neutral ground)

**What Happened:**

Someone tried to assassinate Envoy Valen during peace summit. Aethoria blames Thaldros. Thaldros denies it. Summit collapsing.

### **The SCENE**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*You arrive at the summit building to chaos. Envoy Valen is aliveâ€”barely. Crossbow bolt missed his heart by inches. He's conscious, bleeding, furious.*
>
{{descriptive
*Valen: "Thaldros tried to kill me! So much for peace!"*
>
{{descriptive
*Commander Dawnblade: "We did NO such thing! This is a frame job!"*
>
{{descriptive
*Security found the assassin's positionâ€”rooftop across street. Bolt is Thaldros military issue. Valen's guards want blood. Dawnblade's honor guards are defensive. Violence is imminent unless you stop it.*

---

### **Investigation**

**Perception DC 15 (examining bolt):**
{{descriptive
*Thaldros military crossbow bolt. Standard issue. Available to thousands of soldiers.*

**Investigation DC 17 (examining rooftop):**
{{descriptive
*Sniper position well-chosen. Professional. But... something's off. The angle is wrong. Bolt should have killed Valen easily. This shooter either missed badly or missed on purpose.*

**Medicine DC 16 (examining Valen's wound):**
{{descriptive
*Bolt trajectory suggests deliberate near-miss. One inch right and Valen dies. This wasn't incompetenceâ€”it was precision missing.*

**Investigation DC 18 (rooftop evidence):**
{{descriptive
*Boot prints. Military boots. Size 10. Also: black fabric thread caught on roof tile. Not Thaldros colorsâ€”that's Unbound black.*

---

### **The TRUTH**

**The assassin was Unbound, not Thaldros.**

They used Thaldros equipment to frame them. Deliberately missed Valen (wanted to wound, not killâ€”dead martyr less useful than angry victim). Goal: Reignite war.

**If PCs find Brother Ash from Crisis 2:** He knows about assassin. Can be interrogated.

---

### **The RESOLUTION**

**Option 1: Blame Thaldros**
- Present bolt as evidence
- Demand Thaldros accountability
- **Persuasion DC 16** (Valen wants this)

**If successful:**
- Thaldros apologizes (even though innocent)
- Pays reparations
- Peace holds but resentment grows
- **Reward:** Reputation +5 Aethoria, -5 Thaldros
- **Long-term:** Thaldros eventually discovers truth, furious at injustice

---

**Option 2: Prove Frame Job**
- Present evidence of Unbound involvement
- Show deliberate near-miss
- **Investigation DC 18 to convince both sides**

**If successful:**
- Both kingdoms realize they're being manipulated
- Joint task force against Unbound
- Peace strengthened
- **Reward:** Reputation +5 both kingdoms
- **Bonus:** Hunt for Unbound begins (Quest 3.2 setup)

---

**Option 3: Cover-Up**
- Claim assassin died escaping
- No one to blame
- Move past incident
- **Deception DC 19** (very hard, Valen suspicious)

**If successful:**
- No blame assigned
- Summit continues
- Peace holds
- But mystery remains
- **Reward:** Reputation +2 both (neither fully satisfied)

---

**Option 4: Independent Investigation**
- Demand time to investigate properly
- Delay judgment
- **Persuasion DC 17** to get both sides to wait

**If successful:**
- 1 day to investigate
- Can find more evidence
- Better resolution possible
- But risky (tempers high)

---

## The Pattern

**If PCs investigate all three crises thoroughly:**

**Insight DC 17:**
{{descriptive
*These aren't coincidences. Same day. All designed to provoke war. Someone's coordinating this.*

**Investigation DC 18 (connecting evidence):**
{{descriptive
*Brother Ash connected to two incidents. Unbound black fabric at assassination. The hidden cart from border incident had Unbound symbols scratched inside.*

**The Revelation:**

**The Unbound are sabotaging the peace.**

Corvus (if alive) or Unbound remnants are deliberately creating incidents to restart war. Why? Chaos serves their goals.

**This sets up Quest 3.2: The Underground**

---

## Aftermath

**End of session:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*You handled three crises in one day. Three potential wars prevented. Three diplomatic victories (or compromises, or failuresâ€”depending on choices).*
>
{{descriptive
*But as you return to your quarters, exhausted, you realize: This is your life now. Every day. Every week. The peace doesn't maintain itself. It requires constant, thankless, exhausting work.*
>
{{descriptive
*And someone's actively trying to break it.*
>
{{descriptive
*(A messenger arrives with three more urgent dispatches)*
>
{{descriptive
*"More incidents. Northern border. Western trade route. Southern diplomatic mission. All need Peacekeeper intervention."*
>
{{descriptive
*Welcome to Act III. This is what you earned in Act II. The privilege of defending what you built.*

---

## Rewards

**Based on resolutions:**

**If All Three crises resolved successfully:**
- 2,000gp from grateful kingdoms
- Reputation: +8 with both (or uneven depending on choices)
- Title confirmed: "Official Peacekeepers"
- Rooms at diplomatic quarter (free lodging)

**If 2 of 3 resolved:**
- 1,200gp
- Reputation: +5 average
- Peace holds but strained

**If only 1 resolved:**
- 500gp
- Reputation: +2
- Peace very fragile
- Might not survive Act III

**If none resolved:**
- 0gp
- Peace breaks
- War resumes
- Failed Act III (bad ending)

---

## Level Up

**PCs remain Level 11** after this quest.

This quest establishes Act III pattern: constant crisis management.

---

## New Npcs For Compendium

**Add these:**

1. **Thaldros Border Captain Marcus Stone** (Knight, CR 3) - nervous, hiding guilt
2. **Frontier Lieutenant Sara Brightwind** (Veteran, CR 3) - righteous anger
3. **Thaldros Admiral Viktor Seaworth** (Knight, CR 5) - rigid, lawful
4. **Aethoria Diplomat Chen Aldermist** (Noble, CR 2) - idealist
5. **Brother Ash** (Unbound Agitator, Priest, CR 7) - if captured

---

## DM Guidance

### **Running Multiple Crises**

**Don't make PCs solve all simultaneously:**
- They prioritize (which matters most?)
- Delegate (can send allies to handle one)
- Accept imperfect solutions

**Time Pressure:**
- Each crisis has deadline
- Can't perfectly solve all
- Forces hard choices

### **The Investigation Layer**

**Reward thorough investigation:**
- Pattern emerges if they look
- Unbound connection is findable
- Sets up Act III villain

**But don't require it:**
- Can resolve crises without seeing pattern
- Just makes Quest 3.2 harder

### **Peace is Hard**

**This quest establishes theme:**
- Peace requires constant work
- Both sides need maintenance
- No victory, just daily survival
- This is the "good" ending they earned
- But "good" doesn't mean "easy"

---

## Transition to QUEST 3.2

**After resolving crises:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*You've bought peace another day. Maybe another week. But the incidents continue. And now you know: The Unbound are behind them.*
>
{{descriptive
*Corvus may be dead (or imprisoned, or in hiding). But his followers remain. Cells throughout both kingdoms. True believers who think war serves their goals.*
>
{{descriptive
*Quest 3.2: Hunt the Unbound. Root out the saboteurs. Before they succeed in breaking what you built.*

---

**Quest 3.1: The Peacekeepers - Complete**

**8,500 words**  
**Three interconnected crises**  
**Multiple resolution paths**  
**Sets up Act III structure**  
**Peace Path established**

**Next: Quest 3.2 (The Underground)**
