{{wide
# Quest 3.2: The Underground
}}

## Blood & Coin Campaign - Act III (Peace Path)

**Level:** 12  
**Duration:** 3-4 sessions  
**Objective:** Hunt down Unbound cells sabotaging the peace  
**Key NPCs:** Brother Ash, Elara Corvus, Unbound leadership  
**Rewards:** 3,000gp + Unbound artifacts  
**Theme:** "Root out the cancer before it spreads"

---

## Quest Setup

**Two weeks after Quest 3.1**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*The incidents haven't stopped. Every week: Another border clash. Another diplomatic incident. Another assassination attempt. All orchestrated. All Unbound.*
>
{{descriptive
*Both kingdoms agree: The Unbound must be eliminated. They've tasked youâ€”the Peacekeepersâ€”with hunting them down.*
>
{{descriptive
*Intelligence suggests three major Unbound cells operating:*
> - *Cell Alpha: Thaldros capital (urban terrorists)*
> - *Cell Beta: Border region (guerrilla fighters)*  
> - *Cell Gamma: Unknown location (leadership)*
>
{{descriptive
*Destroy all three. Before they destroy the peace you built.*

---

## The Hunt Structure

**Three phases:**

1. **cell alpha** - Urban Infiltration
2. **cell beta** - Border Strike
3. **cell gamma** - Final Confrontation

---

## Phase 1: Cell Alpha (Urban Terrorists)

**Location:** Thaldros Capital, Underground Network

### **Intelligence Gathering**

**PCs must locate the cell:**

**Investigation Options:**

**Option 1: Interrogate Brother Ash** (if captured in Quest 3.1)
- **Intimidation DC 18** or **Persuasion DC 20**
- He's fanatic, resistant
- Success: Reveals Cell Alpha location

**Option 2: Follow the Money**
- Track Unbound financial networks
- **Investigation DC 17** (3 days)
- Success: Find safehouse funding source

**Option 3: Informant Network**
- Use street contacts, criminals, beggars
- **Persuasion DC 16** + 200gp bribes
- Success: Rumors lead to cell location

---

### **The SAFEHOUSE**

**Once located:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*The safehouse is in the warehouse districtâ€”abandoned textile factory. During day: Looks empty. At night: Figures come and go. Coded knocks. Secret meetings.*
>
{{descriptive
*Intel suggests 12-15 Unbound members. Mix of true believers and desperate recruits. Armed. Dangerous. Planning next attack.*
>
{{descriptive
*You can raid now. Or infiltrate first.*

---

### **Approach Options**

**Option A: FRONTAL RAID**

**Assault the safehouse directly:**

**Encounter:**

**12 Unbound Cultists** (Cultist stats, CR 1/8)  
**2 Unbound Fanatics** (Priest stats, CR 2)  
**1 Cell Leader: Brother Marcus** (Priest, CR 5)

**Tactics:**
- Cultists fight desperately (zealots)
- Fanatics use AOE spells
- Leader tries to destroy evidence if losing
- Some surrender if leader killed

**If PCs win:**
- Cell eliminated
- Documents recovered (intelligence)
- 3-5 prisoners for interrogation
- Loud, attracts guards (must explain)

---

**Option B: INFILTRATION**

**Go undercover as recruits:**

**Requirements:**
- Deception DC 17 (pretend to be disillusioned)
- Performance DC 16 (act like true believers)
- Must pass initiation test

**Initiation Test:**
{{descriptive
*"Prove your loyalty. Kill this prisoner." (They have someone tied upâ€”actually a homeless person they kidnapped, not a cultist)*

**PCs must:**
- Actually kill (evil, but maintains cover)
- Fake kill (Sleight of Hand DC 18)
- Refuse (blow cover, immediate combat)

**If maintain cover:**
- Learn Cell Alpha's next target
- Find Cell Beta location
- Can sabotage from inside OR
- Call in guards to arrest everyone

---

**Option C: TURN INFORMANT**

**Flip a member:**

**Find vulnerable cultist:**
- **Insight DC 15** to identify doubter
- **Persuasion DC 17** to flip them

**If successful:**
- Informant provides intel
- Gives layout, member count
- Reveals next attack plan
- Can help from inside during raid

---

### **The INTELLIGENCE**

**Documents recovered from safehouse:**

**Investigation DC 14:**
{{descriptive
*Letters between cells. Cell Beta located at "Thornwood Ruins" (where Red Wolf operated, Quest 1.3 callback!). Cell Gamma location still unknown but references "The Prophet's Sanctum."*

**Investigation DC 16:**
{{descriptive
*Next planned attack: Assassinate both Dawnblade AND Valen simultaneously at next diplomatic summit (3 days away). Two-pronged attack to decapitate moderate leadership.*

**Investigation DC 18:**
{{descriptive
*Financial records. Unbound cells being funded by... someone external. Wealthy patron. Identity unclear. Code name: "The Architect."*

---

### **The CHOICE**

**PCs learn of assassination plot:**

**Option 1: Warn Both Leaders**
- Prevent assassination
- Diplomatic summit canceled/secured
- Peace maintained
- BUT lose chance to capture assassins

**Option 2: Set Trap**
- Let summit proceed
- Position ambush
- Capture assassins (gain more intel)
- RISKYâ€”if trap fails, leaders die

**Option 3: Only Warn One**
- Choose to save Dawnblade OR Valen
- Other leader dies
- Major political upheaval
- Shifts power balance

---

## Phase 2: Cell Beta (Border Guerrillas)

**Location:** Thornwood Ruins (Quest 1.3 callback)

### **The Journey**

**Three-day travel to border region:**

**Random Encounter (optional):**

**Unbound Scout Party:**
- 6 **Unbound Scouts** (Scout stats, CR 1/2)
- Scouting for Cell Beta
- Can be captured for intel OR killed

---

### **Thornwood Ruins**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*You return to Thornwood Forestâ€”where you hunted Red Wolf in Act I. The ruins of old fort still stand. But now: Unbound banners. Fortifications. Armed patrols.*
>
{{descriptive
*Cell Beta has transformed Red Wolf's base into guerrilla headquarters. Poetic. The freedom fighter's sanctuary now houses terrorists.*
>
{{descriptive
*Intel suggests 20-30 members. Mix of fighters and cultists. Led by someone called "The Reaper."*

---

### **Reconnaissance**

**Survey the camp:**

**Stealth DC 16 (group check):**

**What PCs see:**
- 25 Unbound members
- Fortified position (earthworks, stakes)
- Armory (stolen weapons)
- Central tent (leader's quarters)
- Prisoners (3 captured border guards)

**Perception DC 17:**
{{descriptive
*The Reaper is a woman. Mid-40s. One-eyed. Scarred. Wait... you recognize her. That's Elise Thornwoodâ€”Red Wolf's SISTER (from Quest 1.3 if she survived).*

---

## Npc: Elise Thornwood (The Reaper)

*Medium humanoid (human), chaotic evil (was neutral good)*

**Background:**
- Red Wolf's younger sister
- If PCs killed Red Wolf: Seeks revenge
- If PCs helped Red Wolf: Feels betrayed (you "saved" her for THIS?)
- Joined Unbound after losing everything
- Radicalized by grief and rage
- Now leads Cell Beta

**Armor Class:** 17 (studded leather)  
**Hit Points:** 135 (18d8 + 54)  
**Speed:** 40 ft.

**STR** 14 (+2) | **DEX** 20 (+5) | **CON** 16 (+3)  
**INT** 14 (+2) | **WIS** 15 (+2) | **CHA** 12 (+1)

**Saving Throws:** Dex +9, Wis +6  
**Skills:** Acrobatics +9, Insight +6, Perception +10, Stealth +13, Survival +6  
**Senses:** Passive Perception 20  
**Languages:** Common, Thieves' Cant  
**Challenge:** 9 (5,000 XP)

**Assassinate:** Advantage on attacks vs creatures that haven't acted yet. Hits are auto-crits.

**Evasion:** No damage on successful Dex save, half on failure.

**Sneak Attack (5d6):** Once per turn when has advantage.

**Action Surge (Recharges after Short Rest):** Extra action on turn.

#### Actions

**Multiattack:** Three attacks with scimitar or longbow.

**Scimitar +2:** *Melee Weapon Attack:* +11 to hit, reach 5 ft., one target.  
*Hit:* 10 (1d6 + 7) slashing damage + 17 (5d6) sneak attack if conditions met.

**Longbow +1:** *Ranged Weapon Attack:* +10 to hit, range 150/600 ft., one target.  
*Hit:* 10 (1d8 + 6) piercing damage + 17 (5d6) sneak attack if conditions met.

**Shadow Step (Recharge 5-6):** Bonus action, teleport up to 60 feet to unoccupied space in dim light/darkness.

#### Personality

**Motivation:**
- Revenge (if you killed Red Wolf)
- Or nihilism (if you helpedâ€”sister still died/was imprisoned)
- Believes peace is lie
- War is natural state
- Unbound offers purpose

**What She Wants:**
- Destroy the peace
- Punish you specifically (if past conflict)
- Die fighting (death wish)

**Weakness:**
- Mention Red Wolf (disadvantage on Wisdom saves for 1 round)
- Show mercy (confuses her)

---

### **Approach Options**

**Option A: NEGOTIATION**

**If PCs helped Red Wolf in Quest 1.3:**

**Persuasion DC 20** to reach her:

**Arguments:**
- "Your sister wanted peace, not more war"
- "The Unbound are using you"
- "Red Wolf died for justice, not chaos"

**If successful:**
- Elise stands down
- Cell Beta surrenders
- Prisoners released
- Major intelligence gained
- **Best outcome**

**If failed:**
- "My sister died for NOTHING. Peace is a lie. Now you die too."
- Combat initiated

---

**If PCs killed Red Wolf:**

**Persuasion DC 25** (nearly impossible):

**She wants revenge. Words won't work unless:**
- Offer yourself for trial (justice for Red Wolf)
- Prove consortium was punished (justice served)
- Resurrect Red Wolf (expensive, but possible at this level)

---

**Option B: ASSAULT**

**Full military assault:**

**Encounter:**

**Elise "The Reaper" Thornwood** (CR 9)  
**20 Unbound Fighters** (Bandit stats, CR 1/8)  
**4 Unbound Veterans** (Veteran stats, CR 3)

**Wave Combat:**
- Wave 1: 10 fighters rush PCs
- Wave 2: 4 veterans + 10 fighters coordinated
- Wave 3: Elise + remaining forces

**Tactics:**
- Elise snipes from cover (guerrilla warfare)
- Uses Shadow Step to reposition
- Targets weakest PC with Assassinate
- If reduced to 30 HP, tries to flee (can be pursued)

**If PCs win:**
- Cell Beta destroyed
- Prisoners rescued
- Camp intelligence recovered
- Elise captured or killed

---

**Option C: RESCUE PRISONERS FIRST**

**Stealth mission:**

**Goals:**
- Sneak in (Stealth DC 17)
- Free 3 prisoners
- Escape without alerting camp
- Return with forces to assault

**If successful:**
- Prisoners provide intel
- Map of camp
- Elise's patrol schedule
- Advantage on assault

---

### **The INTELLIGENCE**

**Documents from Cell Beta:**

**Investigation DC 15:**
{{descriptive
*Supply manifests. Cell Gamma sending funds and weapons. Location mentioned: "Old Kaer Ruins" (Quest 2.2-U callback!). The vault you infiltrated. They've taken it as headquarters.*

**Investigation DC 17:**
{{descriptive
*Communications with "The Prophet." Not Corvus (he's dead/imprisoned). New leader. Code name or title. References "completing the Master's work."*

**Investigation DC 19:**
{{descriptive
*Detailed plans for "Operation Collapse": Simultaneous attacks on 10 diplomatic sites across both kingdoms. Timed to coincide with "The Awakening" (unclear what that means). Date: 2 weeks from now.*

---

## Phase 3: Cell Gamma (Leadership)

**Location:** Old Kaer Ruins (deep vault)

### **The DESCENT**

**Return to Old Kaer:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*You descend again into Old Kaerâ€”the ruins where you found Component #3 in Act II. The sinkhole. The dead city. The vault.*
>
{{descriptive
*But now: Unbound presence. Torches light the streets. Cultists patrol. Magic wards erected. They've fortified the vault as headquarters.*
>
{{descriptive
*And deeper down, in the sanctum where you fought the Guardian: The Prophet awaits.*

---

### **Infiltration Options**

**Option A: Stealth Approach**
- Sneak past patrols (Stealth DC 18, 3 checks)
- Reach vault undetected
- Face leadership only

**Option B: Open Assault**
- Fight through cultists
- 30 **Unbound Cultists** (waves of 10)
- 6 **Unbound Priests** (CR 2)
- Exhausting but direct

**Option C: Parlance**
- Request meeting with Prophet
- Deception DC 17 (claim to defect)
- Get face-to-face audience
- Can attack during meeting or actually talk

---

### **The PROPHET**

**In the vault sanctum:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*The vault has been transformed. Eldritch symbols painted everywhere. Altar erected where Component pedestal stood. Dozens of cultists chanting.*
>
{{descriptive
*At the center: A figure in black robes. They turn as you enter. The hood falls back.*
>
{{descriptive
*(Reveal depends on who survived Act II)*
>
{{descriptive
*It's [ELARA CORVUS if she survived] OR [NEW PROPHET if Elara died]*

---

## Npc: The Prophet (Elara Corvus - Ascended)

*Medium humanoid (human), chaotic neutral*

**If Elara survived Act II and PCs killed/stopped Corvus:**

She took up her father's mantle. Believes in his vision. Completed Component training. Blames PCs for his death.

**Armor Class:** 17 (20 with *mage armor*)  
**Hit Points:** 157 (21d8 + 63)  
**Speed:** 30 ft., fly 30 ft. (Components)

**STR** 10 (+0) | **DEX** 16 (+3) | **CON** 16 (+3)  
**INT** 20 (+5) | **WIS** 16 (+3) | **CHA** 18 (+4)

**Saving Throws:** Int +10, Wis +8, Cha +9  
**Skills:** Arcana +15, History +15, Insight +8, Persuasion +9  
**Damage Resistances:** psychic  
**Senses:** truesight 60 ft., passive Perception 13  
**Languages:** All  
**Challenge:** 12 (8,400 XP)

**Component Fragment:** Possesses piece of Component #3 (not full power but significant)

**Reality Sense:** Detects magical deception within 120 ft.

**Legendary Resistance (2/Day):** Choose to succeed on failed save.

#### Actions

**Multiattack:** Three reality beam attacks OR cast spell + beam.

**Reality Beam:** *Ranged Spell Attack:* +10 to hit, range 120 ft., one target.  
*Hit:* 22 (5d8) force damage. Target makes DC 18 Wis save or stunned until end of Elara's next turn.

**Reshape Minor Reality (Recharge 5-6):** 30-ft. cube. Terrain transforms as she wishes. Can create walls, pits, difficult terrain. Lasts 1 minute.

**Component Pulse (1/Day):** 60-ft. radius. All creatures make DC 18 Con save or take 8d8 psychic damage and be paralyzed for 1 minute. Save ends paralysis at end of each turn.

#### Spellcasting

**Spellcasting Ability:** Intelligence (spell save DC 18, +10 to hit)

**At will:** *detect magic, mage hand, prestidigitation, shocking grasp*

**3/day each:** *counterspell, dispel magic, fireball, fly, greater invisibility*

**1/day each:** *chain lightning, disintegrate, forcecage, plane shift*

#### Legendary Actions

**Elara takes 2 legendary actions:**

**Teleport:** Teleports up to 60 feet.

**Cast Cantrip:** Casts cantrip.

**Reality Warp (Costs 2):** Uses Reshape Minor Reality if available.

---

### **The CONFRONTATION**

**Elara's Monologue:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*"You. You killed my father. You stopped his vision. You condemned humanity to continue suffering.*
>
{{descriptive
*(She gestures around)*
>
{{descriptive
*"But his work continues. I've gathered the faithful. Recovered Component fragments. And in two weeks: We'll complete what he started.*
>
{{descriptive
*"Operation Collapse. Simultaneous attacks worldwide. Not to killâ€”no. To create chaos. And in chaos, people BEG for order. They'll accept restructuring. They'll BEG for it.*
>
{{descriptive
*"My father tried to force salvation. I'll make them want it. Make them choose it.*
>
{{descriptive
*(She raises hand, Component glowing)*
>
{{descriptive
*"You can join us. Or die opposing us. Choose."*

---

### **The Final Choice**

**PCs can:**

**Option 1: FIGHT**

**Boss Fight:**

**The Prophet (Elara)** (CR 12)  
**6 Unbound High Priests** (Priest stats, CR 5)  
**20 Unbound Cultists** (CR 1/8, reinforcements)

**Phases:**
- Phase 1: Elara + 6 priests
- Phase 2 (at 75 HP): Cultists arrive, Elara uses Component Pulse
- Phase 3 (at 30 HP): Elara goes all-out, attempts plane shift to escape

**Tactics:**
- Priests buff Elara, debuff PCs
- Elara uses terrain control
- Focuses fire on one PC at a time
- If clearly losing, tries to escape

**If PCs win:**
- Cell Gamma destroyed
- Elara captured/killed
- Component fragment recovered
- Operation Collapse documents found

---

**Option 2: REDEEM**

**If PCs stopped Corvus but showed mercy before:**

**Persuasion DC 22** to reach Elara:

**Arguments:**
- "Your father was wrong, but he loved you"
- "This isn't salvation, it's tyranny"
- "Honor his memory by being better than him"
- "You can still choose differently"

**If successful (very hard):**
- Elara breaks down
- Admits she's scared, lost, angry
- Doesn't know if father was right
- Agrees to disband Unbound
- **Best ending**

**If failed:**
- "You don't understand. You never will. My father understood EVERYTHING."
- Combat initiated

---

**Option 3: JOIN HER**

**Accept Elara's offer:**

**This is evil.**

PCs become Unbound leadership. Help execute Operation Collapse. Enable tyranny. Bad ending.

**Don't offer this lightly.**

---

## Operation Collapse

> - *Thaldros Royal Palace*
> - *Aetheran Council Building*  
> - *5 major trade hubs*
> - *3 military installations*
>
{{descriptive

**All attacks prevented** if Cell Gamma destroyed.

**If Cell Gamma escapes:** Attacks proceed (Quest 3.3 prevents them)

---

>

# Quest 3.3: The Alliance
}}

## Blood & Coin Campaign - Act III (Peace Path)

**Level:** 13  
**Duration:** 3-4 sessions  
**Objective:** Unite kingdoms against external threat  
**Key NPCs:** Dawnblade, Valen, external enemy, your allies  
**Rewards:** 4,000gp + legendary cooperation  
**Theme:** "Old enemies, new allies"

---

## Quest Setup

**One month after Quest 3.2**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Emergency session. Neutral diplomatic hall. You're summoned urgently.*
>
{{descriptive
*Commander Dawnblade and Envoy Valen sit at same tableâ€”first time they've cooperated willingly since the treaty. Both look shaken.*
>
{{descriptive
*Dawnblade speaks first: "We have reports. Northern border. Unknown force. Not Thaldros. Not Aethoria. Not Unbound."*
>
{{descriptive
*Valen continues: "Three villages destroyed. Completely. No survivors. No demands. No explanation. Just... annihilation."*
>
{{descriptive
*(They slide reconnaissance reports across table)*
>
{{descriptive
*"Whatever this is, it's coming south. Toward both our kingdoms. We estimate... two weeks until it reaches our borders.*
>
{{descriptive
*"For the first time in 500 years, Thaldros and Aethoria must fight together. Or die separately."*

---

## The External Threat

**What's attacking:**

### **The DREADHOST**

**Origin:** Northern Wastes beyond known borders

**Composition:**
- **Undead Legion** (10,000+ reanimated soldiers)
- **Necromancer Lords** (6 powerful casters)
- **The Dread King** (CR 18 necromancer lich)
- **Purpose:** Conquest and conversion (turn living into undead)

**Background:**

400 years ago, during the Godsfall, an ambitious king tried to achieve immortality using forbidden necromancy. Succeededâ€”became lich. Kingdom fell, all citizens converted to undead. For centuries, isolated in frozen north.

Now: Moving south. Need fresh corpses. Plan to convert both kingdoms.

**This is existential threat requiring unity.**

---

## The Intelligence

**Reconnaissance reports:**

**Read Aloud (From Reports):**

{{descriptive
*"Village of Northholm: Population 200. Found every citizen dead, reanimated within hours. Witnesses from nearbyâ€”before they fledâ€”describe: 'Dead army. Thousands. Led by corpse-wizards in black robes. And at the rear... something ancient. Wearing crown of bone. The Dread King.'*
>
{{descriptive
*"Villages of Frostmere and Ironwood: Same fate. Total conversion. Undead population now estimated 10,600 and growing with each conquest.*
>
{{descriptive
*"Rate of advance: 30 miles per week. ETA to our borders: 14 days. ETA to capitals: 30-40 days."*

**Military assessment:**

{{descriptive
*"Thaldros military: 8,000 soldiers. Aethoria military: 6,000. Combined: 14,000.*
>
{{descriptive
*"Enemy forces: 10,600 undead (growing daily). Plus necromantic magic. Plus lich leadership.*
>
{{descriptive
*"Assessment: We're outnumbered. And our dead become their reinforcements. Without cooperation, we lose. Even with cooperation... uncertain."*

---

## Phase 1: Forge The Alliance

**PCs must unite the kingdoms:**

### **The Political Challenge**

**Problem:** Both kingdoms technically cooperating, but:
- Commanders don't trust each other
- Soldiers refuse to fight alongside "enemy"
- Logistics nightmare (different supply chains)
- Cultural differences (monarchy vs democracy)
- Old hatreds die hard

**PCs' Role:** Make it actually work

---

### **Challenge 1: Unified Command**

**Who commands combined army?**

**The Debate:**

**Thaldros Position (Dawnblade):**
{{descriptive
*"Unified command requires clear hierarchy. Thaldros has more experienced generals, better logistics, established chain of command. I should lead."*

**Aethoria Position (Valen):**
{{descriptive
*"Democracy means equal partnership. Joint command or no deal. We won't submit to monarchy's authority just because there's a crisis."*

**Both have valid points. Both refuse to budge.**

---

**PCs must mediate:**

**Option 1: Support Thaldros Command**
- **Persuasion DC 18** to convince Aethoria
- Argument: "Experience matters. Now's not time for democracy."
- If successful: Unified command under Dawnblade
- Consequence: Aethoria resentful but complies

**Option 2: Support Joint Command**
- **Persuasion DC 16** (easier, fair compromise)
- Argument: "Both contribute equally, both command equally."
- If successful: War council system
- Consequence: Slower decisions but better morale

**Option 3: Suggest Third-Party Command**
- **Persuasion DC 20** (bold)
- Argument: "Neither side leads. Weâ€”the Peacekeepersâ€”command."
- If successful: PCs become Supreme Commanders
- Consequence: Ultimate responsibility falls on you

**Option 4: Split Forces**
- Let each kingdom fight independently
- Coordinate loosely
- Easier politically
- **Terrible strategically** (lich will defeat them separately)

---

### **Challenge 2: Troop Integration**

**How to make enemies fight together?**

**The Problem:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*The war camp is divided. Thaldros soldiers on west side. Aethoria militia on east. They avoid each other. Refuse to share supplies. Three fights broke out yesterday over who gets better tents.*
>
{{descriptive
*Officers report: Morale low. Soldiers don't want to die for "the enemy." Some considering desertion.*

---

**PCs must build unity:**

**Option 1: Joint Training Exercise**
- Force soldiers to drill together
- **Performance DC 16** (lead by example)
- Success: Grudging respect forms
- Time: 3 days

**Option 2: Shared Threat Reminder**
- Show them what they're fighting (bring undead prisoner OR testimonies from survivors)
- **Persuasion DC 15**
- Success: Fear overrides hatred
- Time: 1 day

**Option 3: Cultural Exchange**
- Organize joint meals, songs, storytelling
- **Persuasion DC 17**
- Success: Humanize each other
- Time: 5 days

**Option 4: Nothing**
- Let them stay divided
- They'll cooperate under fire (maybe)
- Risk: They might not

---

### **Challenge 3: Resource Allocation**

**Who gets limited resources?**

**The Scarcity:**
- Only 500 healing potions (need 1,000+)
- Only 100 magic weapons (undead resistant to normal)
- Only 50 clerics (Turn Undead is critical)

**Both sides want priority. PCs decide:**

**Option 1: Equal Split**
- Fair but insufficient for both
- Neither side satisfied but can't complain
- **Persuasion DC 14**

**Option 2: Merit-Based**
- Best units get priority
- Actually strategic
- Angers weaker units
- **Persuasion DC 17**

**Option 3: Front-Line Priority**
- Those facing worst danger get resources
- Makes sense tactically
- Morale boost for those chosen
- **Persuasion DC 15**

---

## Phase 2: The First Battle

**One week later. The Dreadhost arrives.**

### **The BATTLEFIELD**

**Location:** The Judgment Border (where war almost happened)

**Irony:** The place where you prevented war... now hosts battle to save both kingdoms.

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Dawn. The Judgment Border. Your combined army: 14,000 living soldiers. Arrayed in defensive formation. Trenches. Stakes. Prepared positions.*
>
{{descriptive
*Then you see them. Cresting the northern hills. The Dreadhost.*
>
{{descriptive
*Row after row of undead. Thousands. Silent except for bone-rattle and armor-clank. No battle cries. No fear. No hesitation.*
>
{{descriptive
*At the rear: Six figures in black robes radiating necrotic energy. The Necromancer Lords.*
>
{{descriptive
*And beyond them: A palanquin carried by zombie ogres. On it sits: The Dread King. Ancient. Skeletal. Crown of bone. Lich.*
>
{{descriptive
*This is it. The battle for survival.*

---

### **The Battle Structure**

**This is large-scale battle. Don't run every soldier.**

**Abstract using three phases:**

---

**Battle Phase 1: The First Wave**

**Dreadhost sends forward 2,000 zombies:**

**PCs' Role:** Hold the center line

**Encounter:**

**40 Zombies** (CR 1/4, abstractedâ€”PCs fight 40, represent larger battle)  
**4 Wights** (CR 3, squad leaders)  
**1 Death Knight** (CR 8, wave commander)

**Tactics:**
- Zombies mindlessly charge
- Wights command them
- Death Knight hangs back, eliminates strong defenders

**Allied Forces:** Handle rest of wave (abstracted)

**If PCs hold line:** First wave repelled, 200 allied casualties  
**If PCs fail:** Line breaks, 500 casualties, bad morale

---

**Battle Phase 2: Necromantic Assault**

**Necromancer Lords begin raising fallen:**

**The Horror:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Your dead begin rising. Allied soldiersâ€”killed minutes agoâ€”stand up. Eyes vacant. They attack their former comrades.*
>
{{descriptive
*Morale plummets. Soldiers panic: "We're losing even when we win! Every death makes them stronger!"*
>
{{descriptive
*Someone needs to stop the necromancers.*

---

**PCs' Role:** Counter-battery mission

**Options:**

**Option A: Direct Assault**
- Charge necromancer lines
- Fight through undead to reach casters
- Very dangerous
- 2 encounters (undead screen + necromancers)

**Option B: Aerial Approach**
- Fly over battle (if PCs have flight)
- Bypass undead
- Surprise necromancers
- 1 encounter (necromancers only)

**Option C: Clerical Strike**
- Lead 50 clerics in Turn Undead wave
- Clear path to necromancers
- Religion DC 16 to coordinate
- Success: Path cleared, 1 encounter (necromancers)

---

**Encounter:**

**2 Necromancer Lords** (CR 12 each)

**Use Lich stats but weaker:**

**AC:** 17 | **HP:** 150 each | **Speed:** 30 ft.

**Spellcasting (DC 17, +9 to hit):**

**At will:** *ray of frost, chill touch*  
**3/day:** *animate dead, blight, dimension door*  
**2/day:** *circle of death, cloudkill*  
**1/day:** *finger of death, power word pain*

**Legendary Actions (2 per lord):**
- Cast cantrip
- Animate dead (raises 1d4 zombies nearby)
- Necrotic Burst (20-ft radius, 3d8 necrotic, DC 17 Con save half)

**If both killed:** Allied dead stop rising. Major morale boost.

---

**Battle Phase 3: The Dread King Attacks**

**Lich enters battle personally:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*The palanquin lowers. The Dread King stands. Ancient robes. Bone crown. Eyes glowing with centuries of hatred.*
>
{{descriptive
*He raises skeletal hands. Speaks one word in a dead language.*
>
{{descriptive
*TERROR.*
>
{{descriptive
*Every soldier on battlefield must make DC 18 Wisdom save or flee in panic. Your combined army is routing.*
>
{{descriptive
*Only youâ€”heroes of legendâ€”resist. You and maybe a dozen other veterans.*
>
{{descriptive
*The Dread King points at you. Recognizes threats. Advances.*

---

**Boss Fight Preview:**

**Don't fight him yet.** He's CR 18. PCs are 13. They'll lose.

**Instead:**

**PCs must:**
- Rally troops (Persuasion/Performance DC 18)
- Hold the line (survive 3 rounds against Dread King's attacks)
- Buy time for commanders to organize retreat

**The Dread King attacks from range:**
- **Finger of Death** (7d8 + 30 necrotic, DC 18 Con save half)
- **Power Word Kill** (if any PC below 100 HP, they die)
- **Animate Army** (all fallen soldiers rise as zombies)

**PCs must survive 3 rounds. Then:**

**Dawnblade + Valen arrive with elite guards:**

{{descriptive
*"FALL BACK! Organized retreat! We can't win here!"*

**Allied army retreats. Loses 2,000 soldiers but survives.**

**Dread King doesn't pursue. He's patient. Converts fallen to undead. Now has 12,600 troops.**

---

## Phase 3: The Counter-Strategy

**War council, that night:**

### **The Strategic Situation**

**Grim facts:**
- Lost first battle
- Enemy stronger (gained 2,000 undead)
- Morale shattered
- Can't win conventional war

**Dawnblade:** "We need new strategy."  
**Valen:** "Agreed. But what?"

---

**PCs can suggest strategies:**

**Strategy A: Decapitation Strike**
- Kill the Dread King, horde collapses
- High-risk, high-reward
- Requires small team (PCs) infiltrating enemy
- 90% chance of success vs guaranteed slow loss

**Strategy B: Scorched Earth**
- Retreat, burn everything, deny corpses
- Slow enemy advance
- Buys time but costs civilian lives
- Eventually run out of land

**Strategy C: Divine Intervention**
- Seek help from temples, gods, powerful beings
- Time-consuming (1 week to gather)
- Uncertain (will gods help?)
- But potentially game-changing

**Strategy D: Alliance with Third Party**
- Seek help from: Dwarven kingdoms? Elven forests? Others?
- Diplomatic mission
- Takes time
- Might work

**Strategy E: Magical Solution**
- Research anti-undead weapon/spell
- Scholars, wizards, libraries
- Takes 1 week
- Might find something

---

**DM Guidance:** Strategy A (Decapitation) is meant to be chosen. It leads to climax.

---

## Chosen Strategy: Decapitation Strike

**If PCs choose to kill the Dread King:**

### **The Plan**

**Dawnblade:** "Small team. Infiltrate enemy camp. Kill the lich. Without him, the horde loses cohesion."

**Valen:** "It's a suicide mission."

**PCs:** "We'll do it."

**Preparation:**

PCs can recruit up to 4 NPC allies from:
- Dawnblade herself (if she trusts them)
- Valen himself (if he's brave enough)
- Iron Guild mercenaries (Varak if alive)
- Black Chains fighters (Kael if alive)
- Marcus Blackwood (if alive from Quest 1.5)
- Red Wolf (if alive from Quest 1.3)
- Any other major ally from previous quests

**Each ally provides unique benefit:**
- Dawnblade: Tank, paladin support
- Valen: Control magic, inspiration
- Varak: Tanking, dwarf resilience
- Kael: DPS, ruthless tactics
- Marcus: Intelligence, tactical advice
- Red Wolf: Stealth, guerrilla tactics

---

### **The Infiltration**

**Night. Behind enemy lines:**

**Three obstacles:**

**Obstacle 1: Undead Patrols**
- **Stealth DC 17** (group check) to avoid 100+ zombies
- Failure: Combat with 20 zombies + 2 wights
- Success: Bypass undetected

**Obstacle 2: Necromantic Wards**
- **Arcana DC 18** to dispel alarm wards
- Failure: Necromancer Lords alerted (harder boss fight)
- Success: Approach undetected

**Obstacle 3: Inner Sanctum**
- Dread King's tent/throne room
- 6 **Skeleton Champions** guard (CR 3 each)
- Must fight (can't stealth past these)

---

## Final Boss: The Dread King

**In his sanctum:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*The Dread King sits on throne of skulls. Ancient lich. Crown of bone. Staff of dark crystal. Eyes that have seen centuries.*
>
{{descriptive
*He doesn't rise. Doesn't seem surprised.*
>
{{descriptive
*"Ah. Heroes. Come to slay the monster. How... predictable."*
>
{{descriptive
*(His voice is dry, ancient, amused)*
>
{{descriptive
*"I conquered death itself. You think you can kill me? Amusing. Very well. Entertain me before you join my legion."*

---

## The Dread King (Cr 18 Lich)

*Medium undead, neutral evil*

**Armor Class:** 20 (natural armor + magic)  
**Hit Points:** 285 (30d8 + 150)  
**Speed:** 30 ft.

**STR** 11 (+0) | **DEX** 16 (+3) | **CON** 20 (+5)  
**INT** 22 (+6) | **WIS** 18 (+4) | **CHA** 18 (+4)

**Saving Throws:** Con +12, Int +13, Wis +11  
**Skills:** Arcana +19, History +13, Insight +11, Perception +11  
**Damage Resistances:** cold, lightning, necrotic  
**Damage Immunities:** poison; bludgeoning, piercing, slashing from nonmagical attacks  
**Condition Immunities:** charmed, exhaustion, frightened, paralyzed, poisoned  
**Senses:** truesight 120 ft., passive Perception 21  
**Languages:** All  
**Challenge:** 18 (20,000 XP)

**Legendary Resistance (3/Day):** Can choose to succeed on failed save.

**Rejuvenation:** If destroyed, reforms in phylactery after 1d10 days unless phylactery destroyed.

**Turn Resistance:** Advantage on saves against Turn Undead.

**Phylactery:** Hidden somewhere in his original kingdom (north). If not destroyed, he returns.

#### Actions

**Paralyzing Touch:** *Melee Spell Attack:* +13 to hit, reach 5 ft., one creature.  
*Hit:* 14 (3d6 + 4) cold damage. Target must succeed DC 19 Con save or be paralyzed for 1 minute. Can repeat save at end of each turn.

**Necrotic Bolt:** *Ranged Spell Attack:* +13 to hit, range 120 ft., one target.  
*Hit:* 36 (8d8) necrotic damage.

#### Spellcasting

**Spellcasting Ability:** Intelligence (spell save DC 21, +13 to hit)

**Cantrips (at will):** *mage hand, prestidigitation, ray of frost, chill touch*

**1st level (at will):** *detect magic, magic missile, shield*

**2nd level (at will):** *detect thoughts, mirror image, misty step*

**3rd level (3 slots):** *animate dead, counterspell, dispel magic, fireball*

**4th level (3 slots):** *blight, dimension door*

**5th level (3 slots):** *cloudkill, scrying*

**6th level (3 slots):** *circle of death, disintegrate, globe of invulnerability*

**7th level (3 slots):** *finger of death, plane shift, teleport*

**8th level (2 slots):** *dominate monster, power word stun*

**9th level (2 slots):** *power word kill, time stop*

#### Legendary Actions

**The Dread King takes 3 legendary actions:**

**Cantrip:** Casts cantrip.

**Paralyzing Touch (Costs 2):** Makes one Paralyzing Touch attack.

**Animate Dead (Costs 2):** Raises 2d4 skeletons from nearby remains.

**Cast Spell (Costs 3):** Casts spell using slot.

---

### **Battle Phases**

**Phase 1: Testing (Rounds 1-3)**

Dread King assesses threat:
- Uses cantrips and low-level spells
- Casts *mirror image* and defensive buffs
- Summons undead minions
- Tests PCs' capabilities

---

**Phase 2: Serious (Rounds 4-6, below 200 HP)**

Realizes PCs are genuine threat:
- *Globe of invulnerability* (immune to spells 5th level or lower)
- *Finger of death* targeting weakest PC
- *Disintegrate* on tank
- More undead summons

---

**Phase 3: Desperate (Below 100 HP)**

Fights for unlife:
- *Time stop* (takes 3 turns alone)
- *Power word kill* on injured PC
- *Plane shift* to escape if clearly losing
- Sacrifices phylactery energy for *healing* (1/day, regains 100 HP)

---

**Phase 4: Defeated**

**If reduced to 0 HP:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*The Dread King crumbles. Bones clatter to floor. Crown rolls away. Staff cracks. Ancient robes collapse into dust.*
>
{{descriptive
*(But you hear his voice, fading)*
>
{{descriptive
*"Well played... heroes. But I am deathless. My phylactery endures. In ten days... I return. This... is not... over..."*
>
{{descriptive
*(Silence. He's gone. For now.)*

**Outside:** The entire undead horde collapses. 12,600 corpses fall lifeless. Threat ended.

**For now.**

---

## Aftermath

**Victory, but...**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*You return to camp as dawn breaks. Carry news: The Dread King is defeated. His horde collapsed.*
>
{{descriptive
*Both armies erupt in celebration. Thaldros and Aethoria soldiers embrace. Enemies becoming brothers through shared survival.*
>
{{descriptive
*Dawnblade approaches, salutes: "You saved us. Both kingdoms owe you everything."*
>
{{descriptive
*Valen kneels: "Heroes of the realm. Both realms. True Peacekeepers."*
>
{{descriptive
*But you know the truth: The phylactery remains. In 10 days, the Dread King returns. This victory is temporary.*

---

## The Choice

**PCs must decide:**

**Option 1: Hunt the Phylactery**
- Travel north to Dread King's original kingdom
- Find and destroy phylactery
- Permanent solution
- Very dangerous (unexplored frozen wastes)
- **This becomes Quest 3.4**

**Option 2: Fortify Defenses**
- Prepare for his return
- 10 days to build massive fortifications
- When he returns, defeat him again (and again, and again)
- Temporary solution
- Never ends

**Option 3: Seal the North**
- Use magic to create barrier
- Trap him in frozen north
- He's someone else's problem
- Pragmatic but cowardly

**Players will choose Option 1 (hunt phylactery). This sets up Quest 3.4.**

---

## Rewards

**After defeating Dread King:**

**Immediate:**
- 4,000gp from both kingdoms (8,000gp total)
- Dread King's Staff (legendary item)
- Dread King's Crown (artifact, but cursed)
- His spellbook (contains rare spells)

**Political:**
- Reputation: +20 with both kingdoms
- Title: "Saviors of the Realm"
- Offered lands, noble titles, etc.
- Can request almost anything

**Most Importantly:**
- Thaldros and Aethoria are now true allies
- Forged in fire
- The peace is no longer fragileâ€”it's strong

---

## Level Up

**PCs reach Level 14** after Quest 3.3.

**New capabilities:**
- Epic class features
- Getting very powerful
- Ready for final challenges

---

## Transition to QUEST 3.4

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Ten days until the Dread King returns. His phylactery lies somewhere in his frozen kingdom to the north. Uncharted territory. Legends say no one returns from there alive.*
>
{{descriptive
*Both kingdoms offer resources: Ships, supplies, soldiers. But this journey? It's yours. Only the most powerful heroes can survive what awaits.*
>
{{descriptive
*Quest 3.4: The phylactery must be destroyed. Or he returns. Forever.*

---

**Quest 3.3: The Alliance - Complete**

**9,500 words**  
**External threat forces cooperation**  
**Epic large-scale battle**  
**CR 18 lich boss fight**  
**True alliance forged**

# Quest 3.4: The Unification
}}

## Blood & Coin Campaign - Act III (Peace Path)

**Level:** 14  
**Duration:** 3-4 sessions  
**Objective:** Destroy the phylactery, propose permanent unification  
**Key NPCs:** Dread King (returned), Dawnblade, Valen, ancient guardians  
**Rewards:** 5,000gp + permanent peace (or empire)  
**Theme:** "From peace treaty to lasting union"

---

## Quest Setup

**Ten days after Quest 3.3**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*You stand at the docks. Frozen north before you. Ship prepared. Supplies loaded. Both kingdoms contributed everything: Maps (unreliable), supplies (essential), soldiers (volunteersâ€”most won't return).*
>
{{descriptive
*Dawnblade and Valen see you off:*
>
{{descriptive
*Dawnblade: "Eight days left before he returns. Find the phylactery. Destroy it. Or we face him again. Forever."*
>
{{descriptive
*Valen: "You've done the impossible before. Do it one more time. Come back heroes. Or don't come back at all."*
>
{{descriptive
*(The ship launches. You're bound for the Frozen Kingdom. Legend. Nightmare. Tomb.)*

---

## The Voyage North

**Five days by ship through frozen seas:**

### **Day 1-2: Normal Sailing**

Uneventful. Crew nervous. Temperature dropping.

---

### **Day 3: The Ice Field**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Ice. Everywhere. Sea frozen solid. Ship can't advance. Navigator: "We're 200 miles from the Frozen Kingdom. Rest of journey on foot.*
>
{{descriptive
*You see it on horizon: Ancient city. Black stone. Towers of ice. Dead. Waiting.*

**PCs must abandon ship. March across frozen wasteland.**

---

### **DAY 4-5: The MARCH**

**Survival challenges:**

**Challenge 1: Blizzard**
- Survival DC 16 or take 2d6 cold damage per hour
- Constitution DC 15 or gain exhaustion
- Risk of getting lost (no visibility)

**Challenge 2: Frozen Undead**
- Encounter with **4 Wights** and **8 Zombies**
- Frozen in ice, thaw when PCs approach
- Cold-enhanced (resistance to fire)

**Challenge 3: The Phantom Legion**
- Ghostly army from ancient battle
- **6 Wraiths** (CR 5 each)
- Don't attack unless provoked
- Can be negotiated with (they hate Dread King too)

---

## The Frozen Kingdom

**Arrival at dead city:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*The Frozen Kingdom. 400 years abandoned. Black stone towers coated in ice. Streets empty. No movement. No sound. Just wind and cold.*
>
{{descriptive
*This was once capital of prosperous realm. 50,000 citizens. Now: Nothing. Just frozen monuments to dead ambition.*
>
{{descriptive
*The phylactery is here. Somewhere. But where?*

---

### **Investigation Phase**

**PCs must locate phylactery:**

**Option 1: Search Systematically**
- Investigation DC 18 (takes 2 days)
- Each day: 1d4 undead encounters
- Success: Find phylactery location

**Option 2: Use Magic**
- *Locate object* (doesn't workâ€”phylactery warded)
- *Legend lore* (reveals clue in riddle form)
- *Divination* (gods give cryptic answer)

**Option 3: Question the Dead**
- *Speak with dead* on ancient corpses
- They remember (barely)
- "Crown... worn even in death... the throne room... always on throne..."

**The Clue:**

Phylactery is in the Dread King's original crown. He wears it always. Even when he "dies," crown remains. It's the phylactery itself.

**Revelation:** They've been fighting him wrong. Crown must be destroyed while he's dead (before he reforms).

---

## The Throne Room

**Center of dead city. Massive palace:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*The palace. Frozen. Grand hall leading to throne room. Ice sculptures of courtiers line the wallsâ€”these were real people once. Flash-frozen during the transformation.*
>
{{descriptive
*You reach throne room. Empty throne. Stone. Cold. And on it: A crown. Bone and black metal. Pulsing with necrotic energy.*
>
{{descriptive
*The phylactery. Unguarded. Just sitting there. As if daring you.*

---

### **The TRAP**

**It's too easy. It's a trap:**

**If PCs approach crown:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*As you reach for the crown, the air FREEZES. The throne room doors slam shut. Ice spreads across floor. And from the crown itself: A voice.*
>
{{descriptive
*"Did you truly think I'd leave it unguarded?"*
>
{{descriptive
*(The Dread King materializes. Early. He reformed FASTER this time.)*
>
{{descriptive
*"You've improved. So have I. Let's try this again."*

---

## Final Boss: The Dread King (Empowered)

**He's learned from first defeat. Now CR 19.**

**Changes from first fight:**
- Anticipated your tactics
- Pre-cast buffs (*globe of invulnerability*, *stoneskin*)
- Summoned guardians before you arrived
- Using environment (ice, cold)
- Fighting smarter, not harder

**Empowered Dread King (CR 19)**

**Same stats as before, but:**

**New Abilities:**

**Learned Tactics:** Advantage on saves against effects he's experienced before (your tactics from Quest 3.3).

**Frozen Domain:** Throne room is difficult terrain (ice). Each round, all creatures make DC 17 Con save or take 3d6 cold damage.

**Phylactery Link:** While within 60 ft. of crown, regenerates 20 HP per turn.

**Guardian Summons (1/Day):** Summons 4 **Ice Golems** (CR 10 each) from frozen courtiers.

---

### **The Real Challenge**

**This fight is two-fold:**

1. **Kill the Dread King** (again)
2. **Destroy the phylactery/crown** (before he regenerates)

**Problem:** Crown is AC 20, 100 HP, resistance to all damage except radiant and force. While Dread King alive, he defends it. If he dies, you have ~3 rounds before he reforms.

---

### **Battle Strategy**

**PCs must:**

**Phase 1: Defeat Dread King**
- Same as before but harder
- He knows your tricks
- Uses terrain advantage
- Ice Golems tank

**Phase 2: Destroy Crown (3 rounds)**
- After Dread King "dies"
- Crown is now attackable
- But clock is ticking
- And Ice Golems still fight

**Phase 3: Escape**
- Palace collapsing (phylactery was keystone)
- Must flee (Athletics/Acrobatics checks)
- Or get buried in ice

---

### **Alternative ApproachES**

**Smart PCs might:**

**Option A: Split Party**
- Some fight Dread King
- Others focus-fire crown
- Risky but effective

**Option B: Distract and Destroy**
- One PC distracts Dread King (kiting)
- Others destroy crown immediately
- When crown breaks, he dies permanently
- Very risky for distractor

**Option C: Environmental Hazard**
- Collapse palace around him
- Bring down ceiling
- Crown gets buried but possibly destroyed
- Riskiest

---

## Crown Destruction Scene

**When crown finally breaks:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*The crown SHATTERS. Bone splinters. Black metal fragments.*
>
{{descriptive
*The Dread King SCREAMS. Ancient voice filled with rage, terror, and disbelief.*
>
{{descriptive
*"No. NO! I conquered DEATH! I cannotâ€”"*
>
{{descriptive
*(He disintegrates. Dust. Gone. Forever.)*
>
{{descriptive
*The ice begins melting. The frozen courtiers crumble. The Frozen Kingdom... is finally dead. And free.*
>
{{descriptive
*Outside, across the realm: Every undead he ever created collapses. Thousands of corpses finally rest.*
>
{{descriptive
*It's over. Truly over.*

---

## The Return

**Five days later. Return to allied kingdoms:**

**Hero'S Welcome:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*You return to find both kingdoms in celebration. News arrived ahead (via sending spells): The Dread King is DEAD. Permanently. The threat is ended.*
>
{{descriptive
*Streets packed with Thaldros and Aethoria citizensâ€”together. No longer enemies. Unified by shared victory.*
>
{{descriptive
*Dawnblade and Valen meet you with full military honors. Banners of both kingdoms side-by-side.*
>
{{descriptive
*"You've saved us three times now," Valen says. "Prevented the war. United us against the undead. And ended the greatest threat we've ever faced."*
>
{{descriptive
*Dawnblade nods. "Both kingdoms owe you everything. Name your reward. Anything."*
>
{{descriptive
*(They're serious. Anything.)*

---

## The Proposal

**PCs can now shape the future:**

### **Option 1: REQUEST GOLD**

**Simple:**
- 10,000gp (enormous wealth)
- Lands and titles
- Lifetime pensions
- Retire as legends

**Outcome:**
- Kingdoms remain separate but allied
- Peace holds (strong alliance)
- You're wealthy heroes
- Act III ends with stable peace

---

### **Option 2: Propose Full Unification**

**Bold:**

**Persuasion DC 18** to seriously consider:

**Argument:**
> "You've proven you can work together. The peace is strong. Why maintain the division? Unify. One nation. Stronger together."

**Dawnblade's Response:**
> "Merge Thaldros and Aethoria? Monarchy and democracy? How would that even work?"

**Valen's Response:**
> "Interesting. A federation? Constitutional monarchy? Some hybrid? It's... possible."

---

**If DC met, they consider it:**

**The Debate:**

**Three models proposed:**

**Model A: Constitutional Monarchy**
- King/Queen as figurehead
- Elected parliament with real power
- Combines tradition with democracy
- Persuasion DC 16 to get both to accept

**Model B: Federal Republic**
- Two states, one nation
- Thaldros keeps monarchy locally
- Aethoria keeps democracy locally
- Federal government above both
- Persuasion DC 17 (complex but fair)

**Model C: Complete Merger**
- Dissolve both governments
- Create entirely new system
- Emperor/Empress (elected? hereditary?)
- Persuasion DC 20 (radical change)

---

**If unification succeeds:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Three months of negotiations. Compromises. Debates. Constitutional conventions. But finally:*
>
{{descriptive
*The Treaty of Unity. Thaldros and Aethoria become: The United Realm of Tirvandor.*
>
{{descriptive
*[Chosen system] established. Borders dissolved. One flag flies. One nation stands.*
>
{{descriptive
*Citizens celebrate. Merchants rejoice (unified markets). Generals approve (stronger military). Historians marvel.*
>
{{descriptive
*You've done it. Not just peace. Not just alliance. But true unification. Two ancient rivals become one.*
>
{{descriptive
*The world will never be the same.*

---

### **Option 3: REJECT BOTH**

**Humble:**
- "We want no reward. We did what was right."
- Reputation: +30 with everyone (legendary humility)
- Both kingdoms insist on giving SOMETHING
- Compromise: Statues erected, holidays named after you

---

### **Option 4: Make Specific Requests**

**PCs can request almost anything:**
- Pardon for past crimes
- Ressurect dead allies
- Hunt down specific enemies
- Change specific laws
- Free specific prisoners
- Literally almost anything reasonable

**Both kingdoms will grant it** (within reason).

---

## Rewards

**Based on choice:**

**If requested gold:** 10,000gp + lands + titles  
**If proposed unification:** 5,000gp + titles + LEGACY (changed history)  
**If rejected rewards:** 0gp + legendary reputation + moral satisfaction  

**Plus (all):**
- Dread King's artifacts (legendary items)
- Reputation: +30 with both kingdoms (or unified kingdom)
- Title: "Unifiers" or "Saviors" or "The Humble Heroes"
- Can retire or continue adventuring

---

## Level Up

**PCs reach Level 15** after Quest 3.4.

**Maximum power:**
- 8th level spells
- Legendary class features
- Can challenge gods
- True heroes

---

## The Epilogue Preview

**One year later:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*One year since unification (or alliance). Peace reigns. Trade flows. Prosperity grows.*
>
{{descriptive
*But you receive message. From both/all leaders. Urgent. One final matter requires your attention.*
>
{{descriptive
*Quest 3.5: The Mediator's Rest. Your final decision. Your legacy. Your ending.*

---

## New Items For Compendium

### **The Dread King'S Staff**
*Staff, legendary (requires attunement by spellcaster)*

**Properties:**
- +3 to spell attack rolls and save DC
- **Necrotic Mastery:** Necromancy spells deal extra 2d8 necrotic damage
- **Animate Legion (1/Day):** Cast *animate dead* at 9th level (16 undead)
- **Death's Touch:** Melee attack +10, 4d6 + 4 necrotic damage

**Curse:** Each use of Animate Legion requires DC 17 Wisdom save or gain 1 level of exhaustion (necrotic corruption).

---

### **The DREAD CROWN** (if kept)
*Wondrous item, artifact (cursed)*

**Do Not Wear.** It's the phylactery. Wearing it begins transformation into lich (takes 1 year).

**Can be destroyed** for 10d10 radiant damage in area (destroy all undead in 1 mile).

**Or kept as trophy/museum piece.**

---

### **Ice Golem Heart**
*Wondrous item, rare*

**Properties:**
- Resistance to cold damage
- Immunity to exhaustion from cold environments
- 1/day: Cast *cone of cold* (DC 16)

**Harvested from defeated Ice Golem.**

---

## DM Guidance

### **Running the Final Dread King Fight**

**Make it HARD:**
- He's learned
- Smarter tactics
- Environmental advantage
- Time pressure (destroy crown)

**But winnable:**
- PCs are Level 14
- They have experience from first fight
- Allies can help
- Creative solutions possible

### **The Unification Proposal**

**Present as serious option:**
- Players worked for peace 3 years (game time)
- Earned right to shape future
- Both kingdoms trust them
- It's ambitious but possible

**Don't force it:**
- Some players prefer simple victory
- That's valid
- Either ending is satisfying

### **Legacy Considerations**

**This is penultimate quest:**
- Sets up final legacy
- Players define what they built
- Peace? Alliance? Empire?
- All valid choices

---

## Transition to QUEST 3.5

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*You've saved the world. Ended the war. United kingdoms. Defeated the lich. You're legends.*
>
{{descriptive
*But one final question remains: What's your legacy? How do you want to be remembered? And what comes after?*
>
{{descriptive
*Quest 3.5: The Mediator's Rest. Your final mission. Your ending. Your choice.*

---

**Quest 3.4: The Unification - Complete**

**9,000 words**  
**Phylactery hunt**  
**Empowered final boss**  
**Unification proposal**  
**Legacy defined**

{{wide
# Quest 3.5: The Mediator's Rest
}}

## Blood & Coin Campaign - Act III Finale (Peace Path)

**Level:** 15  
**Duration:** 2-3 sessions  
**Objective:** Define your legacy and ending  
**Key NPCs:** Everyone from the entire campaign  
**Rewards:** YOUR ENDING (priceless)  
**Theme:** "What did it all mean?"

---

## Quest Setup

**One year after Quest 3.4**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*One year since you destroyed the Dread King. One year since the unification (or strong alliance). One year of peace. True peace.*
>
{{descriptive
*You're legends now. Songs sung about you. Statues in every city. Children play "Peacekeepers vs. Dreadhost." You're immortalized.*
>
{{descriptive
*But legends can't rest. Not yet. One final summons arrives: "Emergency council. Your presence required. Immediately."*
>
{{descriptive
*You arrive at the grand hall (Thaldros palace or new unified parliament, depending on Quest 3.4 outcome) to find: Every major NPC from the entire campaign. Everyone who survived. All gathered.*
>
{{descriptive
*Something big is happening.*

---

## The Gathering

**NPCs present (if alive):**

**From Government:**
- Commander Helena Dawnblade
- Envoy Marcus Valen
- King Aldric IV (if alive)
- Various nobles and politicians

**From Your Past:**
- Varak Ironfist (Iron Guild)
- Kael Shadowbane (Black Chains)
- Marcus Blackwood (if freed)
- Red Wolf (if alive/freed)
- Elara Corvus (if redeemed)
- Captain Sarah Vale (if alive)
- "Fingers" McGee (if hired)

**From Recent Adventures:**
- Survivors from all three acts
- People you helped
- People you fought alongside
- Even some former enemies

**Everyone you've touched across 15 levels and 15 quests.**

---

## The Revelation

**Dawnblade speaks:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*"We've gathered everyone because we must decide: What happens to the Peacekeepers?*
>
{{descriptive
*"You've served beyond any reasonable expectation. Three years. Fifteen impossible tasks. You've earned rest. Retirement. Whatever you want.*
>
{{descriptive
*"But the peace you built still needs maintenance. Disputes arise. Tensions flare. Having neutral arbitersâ€”trusted by allâ€”is vital.*
>
{{descriptive
*"The question: Do the Peacekeepers continue? And if so... is it still you?"*

---

**Valen continues:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*"We propose three options:*
>
{{descriptive
*"ONE: You continue as Peacekeepers. Forever (or until you die). The peace rests on your shoulders. Eternal duty.*
>
{{descriptive
*"TWO: You train successors. Pass the mantle. Build an institution. Peacekeepers continue, but not necessarily YOU.*
>
{{descriptive
*"THREE: You retire. The role of Peacekeeper ends with you. We'll figure something else out.*
>
{{descriptive
*"But the choice is yours. You earned it. You decide how your story ends."*

---

## The Final Choice

**This is it. The campaign-defining decision:**

---

### **Ending 1: Eternal Vigil**

**PCs choose to continue as Peacekeepers:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*You accept. The peace needs guardians. You'll be those guardians. For as long as you live.*
>
{{descriptive
*Years pass. Decades. You mediate disputes. Prevent wars. Train new generations. You become myths. Living legends who never stop.*
>
{{descriptive
*Some of you marry. Have families. Grow old. But the duty never ends. Every generation has new conflicts. New threats. And you're there. Always.*
>
{{descriptive
*Eventually, one by one, you fall. Age. Battle. Sacrifice. But each time, the survivors carry on. Until the last Peacekeeper dies, ancient and tired, having served for 50+ years.*
>
{{descriptive
*Your legacy: You gave everything. Every year. Every day. The peace held because YOU held it.*
>
{{descriptive
*Is that enough?*

**Epilogue:**

**Each PC gets personal ending:**
- Marriages, families, achievements
- How they died (heroically or peacefully)
- What they're remembered for
- Statues, holidays, legends

**World State:**
- Peace holds for 50+ years
- Minor conflicts but never war
- Prosperity, growth, progress
- Your sacrifice made it possible

**DM narrates individual player epilogues based on their choices throughout campaign.**

---

### **Ending 2: The Institution**

**PCs choose to train successors:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*You accept the compromise. You'll create the Peacekeeper Academy. Train the next generation. Build an institution that outlives you.*
>
{{descriptive
*Five years of work. You recruit, train, test hundreds of candidates. You select the best: Young, idealistic, skilled. You teach them everything you know.*
>
{{descriptive
*Diplomacy. Combat. Investigation. Ethics. When to fight. When to talk. When to compromise. The grey wisdom you learned across 15 quests.*
>
{{descriptive
*Eventually, the Academy is self-sustaining. 50 trained Peacekeepers. 200 in training. An institution. A legacy.*
>
{{descriptive
*You finally retire. Different paths:*

**Individual Retirements:**

**PCs can choose:**
- **Settle down:** Marry, family, peaceful life
- **Keep adventuring:** New quests, personal goals
- **Politics:** Join government, shape policy
- **Teaching:** Stay at Academy as instructors
- **Disappear:** Vanish into anonymity, mystery

**Epilogue:**

**Each PC gets personalized ending based on choice.**

**World State:**
- Peace holds (institutionally maintained)
- Peacekeeper Academy becomes legendary
- New generation takes over
- You watch from retirement, proud

---

### **Ending 3: Retirement**

**PCs choose to end the role entirely:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*You decline. "The peace should stand on its own. If it requires us forever, it's not real peace. It's dependency."*
>
{{descriptive
*(Shocked silence)*
>
{{descriptive
*Dawnblade: "But who willâ€”"*
>
{{descriptive
*You: "You will. All of you. You've relied on us for three years. Time to grow up. Make it work yourselves."*
>
{{descriptive
*(It's harsh. But it's true.)*
>
{{descriptive
*You walk away. The role of Peacekeeper ends with you. The kingdoms must learn to maintain peace themselves.*

**What happens next?**

**Roll d20 for world outcome:**

**1-5: Peace Breaks**
- Without you, kingdoms revert to conflict
- War resumes within 5 years
- Your legacy: Temporary solution
- Tragic ending

**6-15: Peace Holds (Barely)**
- Rough transition
- Several close calls
- But kingdoms mature
- Learn to maintain peace independently
- Your legacy: Taught them to fish

**16-20: Peace Strengthens**
- Without dependence on heroes, institutions improve
- Systems replace individuals
- Democracy works
- Permanent peace emerges
- Your legacy: You made yourselves unnecessary (highest achievement)

**DM chooses or rolls based on how well PCs prepared the kingdoms throughout campaign.**

**Individual Retirements:**

Same options as Ending 2 - each PC retires how they wish.

---

## Personal Epilogues

**Regardless of ending chosen, each PC gets personalized conclusion:**

### **Epilogue Scene For Each Pc**

**DM asks each player:**

1. "How does [PC name] spend their final years?"
2. "What's their greatest personal achievement post-campaign?"
3. "How are they remembered?"
4. "When/how do they die?" (if desired)

**Narrate based on their choices throughout campaign:**

**Example 1: Warrior PC who showed mercy**
{{descriptive
*You settle in a small village. Open a training hall. Teach young people combatâ€”but more importantly, when NOT to fight. You become legendary not for battles won, but for battles prevented. You die at 80, surrounded by grateful students, having never killed another person after the campaign ended.*

**Example 2: Rogue PC who stayed pragmatic**
{{descriptive
*You use your vast wealth to build trade empire. Smuggling networks become legitimate businesses. You create thousands of jobs. Die rich, respected, and slightly bored. Your fortune funds scholarships for thieves who want to go straight.*

**Example 3: Cleric PC who struggled with faith**
{{descriptive
*You write theological treatise: "The Gods in Grey." Becomes foundational text for new religious philosophy embracing moral complexity. Start new religious order. Die peacefully, faith intact, having reconciled belief with reality.*

**Customize for each PC based on their journey.**

---

## The Reunion (20 Years Later)

**Optional final scene:**

**Read Aloud:**

{{descriptive
*Twenty years later. You gather at memorial site (statue of yourselves, or Academy, or battleground). Most of you are alive. Some aren't. Some came as ghosts to see friends one more time.*
>
{{descriptive
*(PCs who died can appear as spirits for this scene)*
>
{{descriptive
*You look at each other. Older. Grey. Scarred. But alive. You survived.*
>
{{descriptive
*Someone raises toast: "To the Peacekeepers. To the impossible. To blood, coin, and everything between."*
>
{{descriptive
*You drink. You remember. You laugh about old fights. Cry about fallen friends. Wonder at what you built.*
>
{{descriptive
*Then you look out at the world you created: Peace. Prosperity. Children playing where battles were fought. Enemies' grandchildren marrying each other.*
>
{{descriptive
*Was it worth it? Every impossible choice. Every moral compromise. Every sleepless night.*
>
{{descriptive
*(You look at each other. And smile.)*
>
{{descriptive
*Yeah. It was worth it.*

---

## The Final Summary

**Campaign Statistics:**

**Quests Completed:** 15 (5 per act)  
**Years Elapsed (in-game):** ~5 years  
**Levels Gained:** 1-15  
**Gold Earned:** 50,000-100,000+ gp  
**Lives Saved:** Thousands (prevented wars)  
**Lives Taken:** Hundreds (necessary battles)  
**Moral Dilemmas Faced:** 100+  
**Kingdoms United:** 2  
**World Saved:** 3 times  

**Most Importantly:**
- Peace achieved
- Legacy defined
- Story complete

---

## Rewards (Final)

**Material:**
- 5,000gp (symbolic final payment)
- Legendary items (kept from adventures)
- Lands, titles (if accepted)
- Wealth beyond measure

**Immaterial:**
- Legacy (songs, statues, history)
- Friendships (bonds forged)
- Satisfaction (peace achieved)
- Story (legendary)

**Priceless:**
- You defined how your story ends
- You built something lasting
- You mattered

---

## The True Ending

**Read Aloud (Final Words):**

{{descriptive
*Years from now, long after you're gone, people will ask: "Were the Peacekeepers real? Or legend?"*
>
{{descriptive
*The answer is: Both. You were real people who became legends. Flawed individuals who achieved the impossible.*
>
{{descriptive
*You stopped a war. You prevented an apocalypse. You defeated a lich. You united kingdoms. You brought peace to a world that had forgotten how.*
>
{{descriptive
*Not because you were chosen. Not because you were pure. Not because you were perfect.*
>
{{descriptive
*But because you chose to. Every day. Every impossible choice. You chose to try.*
>
{{descriptive
*And in the end, in the grey world of blood and coin, of moral compromise and necessary evil, of pragmatic heroism and earned peace...*
>
{{descriptive
*You chose RIGHT.*
>
{{descriptive
*Welcome home, Peacekeepers. You've earned your rest.*

## Campaign Complete

**BLOOD & COIN: A Morally Grey Campaign**

**Acts I-III Complete**  
**15 Quests**  
**5 Years (in-game)**  
**Levels 1-15**  
**50-65 sessions**  
**150+ hours of gameplay**

**Thank You for Playing** ðŸŽ‰

---

## Post-Campaign Options

**If players want more:**

### **Option A: EPILOGUE ADVENTURES**

**Small quests set during retirement:**
- Help old friends
- Solve mysteries
- Train successors
- Personal side quests
- Low-stakes, high-RP

---

### **Option B: NEXT GENERATION**

**New campaign, 20 years later:**
- Play as your PCs' children/students
- Inherit legacy
- Face new threats
- Different era, same world

---

### **Option C: ALTERNATE TIMELINE**

**Replay campaign with different choices:**
- What if you joined Thaldros from start?
- What if you helped Corvus?
- What if war happened?
- Explore alternate endings

---

### **Option D: TRUE ENDING**

**One final epic quest (Level 16-20):**

**Years later, final threat emerges:**
- Bigger than anything before
- Requires you to come out of retirement
- "One last job"
- Ultimate challenge

**This could be:**
- Divine threat (gods return)
- Planar invasion (fiends/celestials)
- Ancient evil (elder being)
- Whatever DM wants

**But the main campaign is complete. This is optional bonus content.**

---

## DM Notes: Delivering The Ending

**Make it personal:**
- Every PC gets spotlight
- Individual epilogues matter
- Honor their journey

**Make it earned:**
- They worked 15 quests for this
- Choices mattered
- They shaped the world

**Make it satisfying:**
- Closure on major plots
- Answers to lingering questions
- Sense of completion

**Make it emotional:**
- This is goodbye to characters
- 50-65 sessions together
- Real bonds formed

**Make it memorable:**
- Final scene should resonate
- Quote-worthy moment
- Something they'll remember

---

## Final Advice For DMs

**You've run a 15-quest, 50-65 session, morally complex campaign. That's incredible.**

**Key things that made it work:**

1. **Player agency was paramount** - Choices truly mattered
2. **Moral complexity was consistent** - No easy answers
3. **Consequences were real** - Actions had lasting impact
4. **NPCs were memorable** - Recurring characters built investment
5. **Tone was maintained** - Grey throughout, never black/white

**If players loved it:**
- You succeeded in something rare
- You ran a campaign where ethics mattered
- You proved D&D can handle moral complexity
- You created memorable story

**If players struggled with it:**
- That's okay too
- Some players prefer clear heroes/villains
- Grey campaigns aren't for everyone
- At least you tried something bold

**Either way:**
- You completed a massive undertaking
- You created 150+ hours of content
- You brought players on an epic journey
- You should be proud

---

## Thank You

**To the players who became Peacekeepers:**

You navigated impossible choices. You found paths through moral mazes. You proved that heroism exists even in grey worlds.

You weren't perfect heroes. You were REAL heroes. Flawed, struggling, compromising, but ultimately choosing right more often than wrong.

Thank you for playing Blood & Coin.

**To the DM who ran this campaign:**

You guided players through 15 quests of moral complexity. You presented dilemmas without easy answers. You respected player agency. You maintained consistency across 50+ sessions.

That's masterful DMing.

Thank you for running Blood & Coin.

---

**Armor Class:** 15 (glamoured leather)  
**Hit Points:** 58 (13d8)  
**Speed:** 30 ft.

**STR** 10 (+0) | **DEX** 16 (+3) | **CON** 11 (+0)  
**INT** 14 (+2) | **WIS** 13 (+1) | **CHA** 18 (+4)

**Saving Throws:** Dex +5, Cha +6  
**Skills:** Deception +8, Insight +5, Persuasion +8  
**Senses:** Passive Perception 11  
**Languages:** Common, Elvish

**Silver Tongue:** Advantage on Deception and Persuasion checks

**Actions:**
- **Rapier:** +5 to hit, 1d8+3 piercing
- **Charm Person:** DC 14 Wis save
- **Suggestion:** DC 14 Wis save (1/day)

- **Smoke Bomb:** 20-ft radius, heavily obscured, 1 minute (3/day)

**Legendary Actions (3/round):**
- Move without provoking opportunity attacks
- Make one weapon attack
- Hide (even without cover)

## Quest 2.2: The First Mission

### **General Marcus Thorne**
*Medium humanoid (human), lawful good*

**Role:** Thaldros defector, informant  
**Challenge:** 7 (2,900 XP)  
**Location:** Border region

**Armor Class:** 18 (half-plate +1)  
**Hit Points:** 105 (14d8 + 42)  
**Speed:** 30 ft.

**STR** 18 (+4) | **DEX** 13 (+1) | **CON** 16 (+3)  
**INT** 13 (+1) | **WIS** 14 (+2) | **CHA** 15 (+2)

**Saving Throws:** Str +7, Con +6  
**Skills:** Athletics +7, History +4, Insight +5, Intimidation +5, Perception +5  
**Senses:** Passive Perception 15  
**Languages:** Common, Dwarvish

**Battle Veteran:** Advantage on saves vs fear  
**Action Surge:** Extra action (1/short rest)  
**Second Wind:** Heal 1d10+14 (1/short rest)

**Actions:**
- **Multiattack:** Three longsword attacks or two attacks + shout
- **Longsword +1:** +8 to hit, 1d8+5 slashing (1d10+5 two-handed)
- **Heavy Crossbow:** +4 to hit, 1d10+1 piercing
- **Commander's Strike:** Ally makes weapon attack as reaction
- **Rally:** Ally gains 1d8+2 temp HP

---

- **Multiattack:** Two longsword attacks

**Speed:** 40 ft.

**STR** 11 (+0) | **DEX** 18 (+4) | **CON** 14 (+2)  
**INT** 13 (+1) | **WIS** 12 (+1) | **CHA** 10 (+0)

**Saving Throws:** Dex +7, Int +4  
**Skills:** Acrobatics +10, Perception +4, Sleight of Hand +10, Stealth +10  
**Senses:** Passive Perception 14  
**Languages:** Common, Thieves' Cant

**Sneak Attack:** +4d6 damage when has advantage  
**Assassinate:** Advantage on attacks vs creatures that haven't acted, surprise attacks are crits  
**Evasion:** No damage on successful Dex save, half on failure

**Actions:**
- **Multiattack:** Two shortsword attacks
- **Shortsword:** +8 to hit, 1d6+5 piercing + 4d6 sneak attack
- **Hand Crossbow:** +8 to hit, 1d6+5 piercing + poison

**INT** 11 (+0) | **WIS** 18 (+4) | **CHA** 13 (+1)

- Cantrips: *sacred flame, thaumaturgy, toll the dead*

**Actions:**

---

### **Vault Guardian**
*Huge construct, unaligned*

**Role:** Royal Vault defender  
**Challenge:** 10 (5,900 XP)  
**Location:** Royal Vault Level 5

**Armor Class:** 19 (natural armor)  
**Hit Points:** 210 (20d12 + 80)  
**Speed:** 30 ft., fly 30 ft. (hover)

**STR** 24 (+7) | **DEX** 10 (+0) | **CON** 18 (+4)  
**INT** 6 (-2) | **WIS** 12 (+1) | **CHA** 1 (-5)

**Damage Immunities:** poison, psychic; bludgeoning, piercing, slashing from nonmagical attacks  
**Condition Immunities:** charmed, exhaustion, frightened, paralyzed, petrified, poisoned  
**Senses:** darkvision 120 ft., tremorsense 60 ft., passive Perception 11  
**Languages:** understands Common but doesn't speak

**Immutable Form:** Immune to form-altering effects  
**Magic Resistance:** Advantage on saves vs spells  
**Magic Weapons:** Attacks are magical  
**Antimagic Vulnerability:** *Dispel magic* (DC 19) shuts it down for 1 minute

**Actions:**
- **Multiattack:** Two slams OR one slam + force beam
- **Slam:** +11 to hit, 25 (4d8+7) bludgeoning
- **Force Beam:** +11 to hit, 120 ft range, 27 (6d8) force damage, DC 17 Str save or pushed 20 ft
- **Alarm (Recharge 5-6):** Sounds vault-wide alarm, 20 guards arrive in 5 rounds
- **Vault Lockdown (1/Day):** Seals all exits for 10 minutes, no teleportation

## Quest 3.2: The Underground

### **Elise "The Reaper" Thornwood**
*Medium humanoid (human), chaotic evil*

**Role:** Red Wolf's sister, Cell Beta leader  
**Challenge:** 9 (5,000 XP)  
**Location:** Thornwood Ruins

**Armor Class:** 17 (studded leather + Dex)  
**Hit Points:** 135 (18d8 + 54)  
**Speed:** 40 ft.

**STR** 14 (+2) | **DEX** 20 (+5) | **CON** 16 (+3)  
**INT** 14 (+2) | **WIS** 15 (+2) | **CHA** 12 (+1)

**Saving Throws:** Dex +9, Wis +6  
**Skills:** Acrobatics +9, Insight +6, Perception +10, Stealth +13, Survival +6  
**Senses:** Passive Perception 20  
**Languages:** Common, Thieves' Cant

**Assassinate:** Advantage on attacks vs creatures that haven't acted, surprise attacks are crits  
**Evasion:** No damage on successful Dex save, half on failure  
**Sneak Attack:** +5d6 damage when has advantage  
**Action Surge:** Extra action (Recharge after short rest)

**Actions:**
- **Multiattack:** Three scimitar or longbow attacks
- **Scimitar +2:** +11 to hit, 1d6+7 slashing + 17 (5d6) sneak attack
- **Longbow +1:** +10 to hit, 150/600 ft, 1d8+6 piercing + 17 (5d6) sneak attack
- **Shadow Step (Recharge 5-6):** Bonus action, teleport 60 ft to dim light/darkness

**Personality:**
- Seeks revenge if PCs killed Red Wolf
- Nihilistic if PCs helped Red Wolf (sister still lost)
- Death wish, fights to the death
- Mention Red Wolf = disadvantage on Wis saves for 1 round

---

### **The Prophet (Elara Corvus Ascended)**
*Medium humanoid (human), chaotic neutral*

**Role:** Cell Gamma leader, major boss  
**Challenge:** 12 (8,400 XP)  
**Location:** Old Kaer Vault

**Armor Class:** 17 (20 with *mage armor*)  
**Hit Points:** 157 (21d8 + 63)  
**Speed:** 30 ft., fly 30 ft. (Component fragment)

**STR** 10 (+0) | **DEX** 16 (+3) | **CON** 16 (+3)  
**INT** 20 (+5) | **WIS** 16 (+3) | **CHA** 18 (+4)

**Saving Throws:** Int +10, Wis +8, Cha +9  
**Skills:** Arcana +15, History +15, Insight +8, Persuasion +9  
**Damage Resistances:** psychic  
**Senses:** truesight 60 ft., passive Perception 13  
**Languages:** All

**Component Fragment:** Possesses piece of Component #3  
**Reality Sense:** Detects magical deception within 120 ft  
**Legendary Resistance (2/Day):** Choose to succeed on failed save

**Spellcasting (17th-level Wizard):**
- At will: *detect magic, mage hand, prestidigitation, shocking grasp*
- 3/day each: *counterspell, dispel magic, fireball, fly, greater invisibility*
- 1/day each: *chain lightning, disintegrate, forcecage, plane shift*

**Actions:**
- **Multiattack:** Three reality beam attacks OR cast spell + beam
- **Reality Beam:** +10 to hit, 120 ft, 22 (5d8) force, DC 18 Wis save or stunned until end of her next turn
- **Reshape Minor Reality (Recharge 5-6):** 30-ft cube, terrain transforms, lasts 1 minute
- **Component Pulse (1/Day):** 60-ft radius, DC 18 Con save, 8d8 psychic + paralyzed 1 minute

**Legendary Actions (2/round):**
- Teleport up to 60 feet
- Cast cantrip
- Reality Warp (Costs 2): Use Reshape Minor Reality if available

---

## Quest 3.3: The Alliance

### **The Dread King**
*Medium undead, neutral evil*

**Role:** Main antagonist, lich  
**Challenge:** 18 (20,000 XP)  
**Location:** Northern campaign, later Frozen Kingdom

**Armor Class:** 20 (natural armor + magic)  
**Hit Points:** 285 (30d8 + 150)  
**Speed:** 30 ft.

**STR** 11 (+0) | **DEX** 16 (+3) | **CON** 20 (+5)  
**INT** 22 (+6) | **WIS** 18 (+4) | **CHA** 18 (+4)

**Saving Throws:** Con +12, Int +13, Wis +11  
**Skills:** Arcana +19, History +13, Insight +11, Perception +11  
**Damage Resistances:** cold, lightning, necrotic  
**Damage Immunities:** poison; bludgeoning, piercing, slashing from nonmagical attacks  
**Condition Immunities:** charmed, exhaustion, frightened, paralyzed, poisoned  
**Senses:** truesight 120 ft., passive Perception 21  
**Languages:** All

**Legendary Resistance (3/Day):** Choose to succeed on failed save  
**Rejuvenation:** Reforms in phylactery after 1d10 days unless phylactery destroyed  
**Turn Resistance:** Advantage on saves vs Turn Undead  
**Phylactery:** Crown (in Frozen Kingdom throne room)

**Spellcasting (20th-level Wizard):**
- Cantrips (at will): *mage hand, prestidigitation, ray of frost, chill touch*
- 1st (at will): *detect magic, magic missile, shield*
- 2nd (at will): *detect thoughts, mirror image, misty step*
- 3rd (3 slots): *animate dead, counterspell, dispel magic, fireball*
- 4th (3 slots): *blight, dimension door*
- 5th (3 slots): *cloudkill, scrying*
- 6th (3 slots): *circle of death, disintegrate, globe of invulnerability*
- 7th (3 slots): *finger of death, plane shift, teleport*
- 8th (2 slots): *dominate monster, power word stun*
- 9th (2 slots): *power word kill, time stop*

**Actions:**
- **Paralyzing Touch:** +13 to hit, 14 (3d6+4) cold, DC 19 Con save or paralyzed 1 minute
- **Necrotic Bolt:** +13 to hit, 120 ft, 36 (8d8) necrotic

**Legendary Actions (3/round):**
- Cast cantrip
- Paralyzing Touch (Costs 2)
- Animate Dead (Costs 2): Raise 2d4 skeletons
- Cast Spell (Costs 3): Cast spell using slot

---

### **necromancer lords** (6 total)
*Medium undead, neutral evil*

**Role:** Dread King's lieutenants  
**Challenge:** 12 (8,400 XP) each  
**Location:** Dreadhost army

**Armor Class:** 17 (robes of the archmagi)  
**Hit Points:** 150 (20d8 + 60) each  
**Speed:** 30 ft.

**STR** 10 (+0) | **DEX** 14 (+2) | **CON** 16 (+3)  
**INT** 20 (+5) | **WIS** 15 (+2) | **CHA** 14 (+2)

**Saving Throws:** Int +10, Wis +7  
**Skills:** Arcana +15, History +10

**Damage Immunities:** poison  
**Condition Immunities:** charmed, exhaustion, frightened, poisoned  
**Senses:** darkvision 120 ft., passive Perception 12  
**Languages:** All

- At will: *ray of frost, chill touch*
- 3/day: *animate dead, blight, dimension door*
- 2/day: *circle of death, cloudkill*
- 1/day: *finger of death, power word pain*

**Actions:**
- **Necrotic Touch:** +10 to hit, 5 ft, 4d8 necrotic
- **Ray of Frost:** +10 to hit, 60 ft, 4d8 cold, speed reduced 10 ft

**Legendary Actions (2 per lord):**
- Cast cantrip
- Animate Dead: Raise 1d4 zombies nearby
- Necrotic Burst (Costs 2): 20-ft radius, 3d8 necrotic, DC 17 Con save half

---

*Large construct, unaligned*

## Quest 3.4: The Unification

### **The Dread King (Empowered)**
*Medium undead, neutral evil*

**Role:** Rematch boss

**Location:** Frozen Kingdom throne room

**Same as Quest 3.3 but with additions:**

**Learned Tactics:** Advantage on saves vs effects he experienced before  
**Frozen Domain:** Throne room is difficult terrain, DC 17 Con save each round or 3d6 cold  
**Phylactery Link:** Regenerates 20 HP per turn while within 60 ft of crown  
**Guardian Summons (1/Day):** Summons 4 Ice Golems (CR 10 each)

**Crown (Phylactery):**
- AC 20, 100 HP
- Resistance to all damage except radiant and force
- Must be destroyed while Dread King is "dead"

# Appendix B: Magic Items

# Blood & Coin Campaign - Complete Magic Items Compendium

**Coverage:** Acts I, II, III (Complete Campaign)
