# Act I Items

## Quest 1.1: The Consortium Job

### **Elise'S Glamoured Leather**
*Armor (leather), uncommon*

**AC:** 11 + Dex modifier  
**Attunement:** No

**Properties:**
- Appears as expensive noble clothing
- Can change appearance (minor illusion level)
- Advantage on Charisma (Deception) checks to appear wealthy

**Lore:** Commissioned by Elise Consortium for covert work. Allows her to move between high society and criminal underworld seamlessly.

**Location:** Worn by Elise, can be looted if she's defeated

**Value:** 350gp

---

### **Marcus'S Family Shield**
*Armor (shield), uncommon*

**AC:** +2  
**Attunement:** No

**Properties:**
- Standard +2 shield
- Bears Blackwood family crest
- Proof of Marcus's noble heritage

**Lore:** Heirloom from Marcus Blackwood's family. Proves his noble status if shown to authorities.

**Location:** Marcus carries it

**Value:** 400gp (more as evidence)

---

## Quest 1.2: The Hunters

### **Kael'S Poisoned Blades**
*Weapon (shortsword), rare (requires attunement)*

**Damage:** 1d6 + Dex piercing  
**Properties:** Finesse, light, special

**Venom Reservoir:** Blade has 3 charges. As bonus action, expend 1 charge to coat blade with poison (lasts 1 minute). Next hit: DC 15 Con save, 3d6 poison damage (half on success). Regains 1d3 charges at dawn.

**Lore:** Kael's signature weapons. Each blade has hollow core containing concentrated venom.

**Location:** Wielded by Kael Shadowbane

**Value:** 2,500gp

---

### **Ring OF Shadows**
*Ring, uncommon (requires attunement)*

**Properties:**
- +2 to Stealth checks
- Once per short rest: Cast *pass without trace* (self only)
- Shadows seem slightly deeper around wearer

**Lore:** Black Chains standard issue for senior members.

**Location:** Found in Black Chains treasure

**Value:** 750gp

---

## Quest 1.3: The Red Wolf

### **Red Wolf'S Longbow**
*Weapon (longbow), very rare (requires attunement)*

**Damage:** 1d8 + 2 piercing  
**Range:** 150/600 ft  
**Properties:** Ammunition, heavy, two-handed, +2

**Forest's Friend:** In forest terrain, attacks have advantage. Arrows make no sound when fired.

**Swift Shot:** Can use bonus action to make additional longbow attack (3/day).

**Lore:** Catherine "Red Wolf" Thornwood's signature weapon. Carved from ancient oak, blessed by forest spirits.

**Location:** Wielded by Red Wolf

**Value:** 8,000gp

---

### **Cloak OF The Thornwood**
*Wondrous item, rare (requires attunement)*

**AC:** No change  
**Properties:**
- Advantage on Stealth checks in natural terrain
- Can cast *pass without trace* (1/day)
- Resistance to poison damage
- Can communicate with plants as per *speak with plants* (1/day)

**Lore:** Red Wolf's iconic cloak. Woven from thornvines, grants connection to forest.

**Location:** Worn by Red Wolf

**Value:** 3,500gp

---

## Quest 1.4: The Black Ledger

### **Lord Pembroke'S Signet Ring**
*Ring, uncommon*

**Properties:**
- Acts as noble seal (authentication)
- +2 to Charisma (Persuasion) checks with nobility
- Can cast *detect magic* at will

**Curse:** Wearer becomes increasingly arrogant. Wisdom save DC 12 each day or gain flaw: "I am better than common folk."

**Lore:** Pembroke family heirloom. Contains minor enchantment and major ego.

**Location:** Worn by Lord Pembroke

**Value:** 1,200gp

---

### **The BLACK LEDGER** (Quest Objective)
*Wondrous item, uncommon*

**Properties:**
- Contains records of illegal transactions
- Magical lock (DC 18 Thieves' tools or *knock* spell)
- Self-destructs if wrong person opens (DC 15 Dex save, 4d6 fire)
- Worth 5,000gp as blackmail material

**Lore:** Evidence of widespread corruption. Pembroke's insurance policy and his doom.

**Location:** Hidden in Pembroke Estate vault

**Value:** 500gp (object), 5,000gp (information)

---

## Quest 1.5: The Trial

### **Magistrate'S Robes OF Office**
*Wondrous item, rare*

**AC:** 14  
**Properties:**
- +2 to Intelligence (Investigation) and Wisdom (Insight)
- Advantage on saves vs charm
- Can cast *zone of truth* (DC 13, 1/day)
- Can cast *detect thoughts* (DC 13, 1/day)

**Lore:** Enchanted robes given to senior magistrates. Help discern truth from lies.

**Location:** Worn by Magistrate Ravens (not lootable unless earned)

**Value:** 4,000gp

---

### **Scales of Justice** (Court Artifact)
*Wondrous item, legendary (not obtainable)*

**Properties:**
- Detects lies within 60 ft
- Forces truth-telling in courtroom
- Cannot be deceived or charmed

**Lore:** Ancient artifact in courthouse. Ensures fair trials. Cannot be taken.

**Value:** Priceless (not for sale)

---

# Act II Items

## Quest 2.1: The Recruiters

### **Dawnblade'S Longsword**
*Weapon (longsword), legendary (requires attunement by paladin)*

**Damage:** 1d8 + 3 slashing (1d10 + 3 two-handed)  
**Properties:** Versatile, +3, special

**Dawn's Light:** Blade sheds bright light 20 ft, dim light 20 ft beyond. Can be toggled on/off.

**Smite Enhancement:** Divine smite deals additional 1d8 radiant damage.

**Command Presence:** While wielding, allies within 30 ft gain +1 to attack rolls.

**Lore:** Commander Dawnblade's signature weapon. Forged for first Thaldros Knight-Commander 300 years ago.

**Location:** Wielded by Commander Dawnblade (not obtainable unless she dies or gifts it)

**Value:** 45,000gp

---

### **Valen'S Pendant OF Eloquence**
*Wondrous item, rare (requires attunement)*

**Properties:**
- +2 to Charisma (Persuasion) checks
- Advantage on Charisma (Performance) when making speeches
- Can cast *charm person* (DC 14, 3/day)
- Can cast *suggestion* (DC 14, 1/day)

**Lore:** Gift from Aethoria's founders. Worn by all Senate leaders. Symbol of democratic ideals.

**Location:** Worn by Envoy Valen

**Value:** 3,000gp

---

## Quest 2.2: The First Mission

### **World-Splitter Component #1** (Unbound Quest)
*Artifact (fragment), artifact*

**Properties:**
- Grants +2 to Intelligence
- Can cast *detect thoughts* at will
- User can sense other Components within 10 miles
- **Corruption:** Each day attuned, make DC 15 Wis save or gain madness

**Lore:** One of five fragments of reality-warping artifact. Extremely dangerous. Corvus seeks all five.

**Location:** Hidden in ancient vault (Unbound quest path)

**Value:** Incalculable (world-threatening)

---

### **General Thorne'S Plate Armor +1**
*Armor (plate), rare*

**AC:** 19  
**Attunement:** No

**Properties:**
- Standard +1 plate armor
- Bears Thaldros military insignia
- Weight: 65 lbs

**Lore:** Standard issue for Thaldros generals. Well-crafted but not magical beyond enhancement.

**Location:** Worn by General Marcus Thorne

**Value:** 2,500gp

---

## Quest 2.3: The Double Cross

### **Infiltrator'S Cloak**
*Wondrous item, rare (requires attunement)*

**Properties:**
- Advantage on Dexterity (Stealth) checks
- Can cast *invisibility* (self only, 1/day)
- Can change color to match surroundings (takes 1 minute)

**Lore:** Used by spies and informants. Perfect for those who betray powerful people.

**Location:** Can be purchased or found after exposing betrayals

**Value:** 3,200gp

---

## Quest 2.4: The Heist

### **World-Splitter Component #3**
*Artifact (fragment), artifact*

**Properties:** Same as Component #1 but:
- Grants +2 to Wisdom (rather than Intelligence)
- Can cast *scrying* (1/day)
- **Corruption:** DC 16 Wis save daily

**Lore:** Third Component. In Royal Vault. Everyone wants it.

**Location:** Royal Vault, pedestal in inner sanctum

**Value:** Incalculable

---

### **Crown Jewels OF Thaldros**
*Wondrous item set, legendary*

**Set includes:**
- Crown (headwear)
- Scepter (rod)
- Orb (wondrous item)

**Combined Properties (if wearing all three):**
- Advantage on Charisma checks with nobility
- Can cast *command* at will
- +3 to AC
- Immunity to being charmed

**Individual Items:** Each has minor benefits

**Lore:** Symbols of royal authority. Extremely valuable, extremely recognizable.

**Location:** Royal Vault

**Value:** 50,000gp (set), but selling would be nearly impossible

---

### **Defender Longsword**
*Weapon (longsword), very rare (requires attunement)*

**Damage:** 1d8 + 3 slashing (1d10 + 3 two-handed)  
**Properties:** Versatile, +3

**Defensive Stance:** As bonus action, transfer some/all attack bonus to AC bonus. Example: +1 to attacks, +2 to AC.

**Lore:** Classic D&D magic item. In Royal Vault collection.

**Location:** Royal Vault, display case

**Value:** 24,000gp

---

### **Staff OF Power**
*Staff, very rare (requires attunement by sorcerer, warlock, or wizard)*

**Properties:**
- +2 to spell attack rolls and save DC
- +2 to AC
- +2 to saving throws
- Contains 20 charges for spells
- Can break as retributive strike (30d6 to all in 30 ft)

**Lore:** One of most powerful staves. In Royal Vault.

**Location:** Royal Vault, secured case

**Value:** 40,000gp

---

### **Ring OF Spell Storing**
*Ring, rare (requires attunement)*

**Properties:**
- Stores up to 5 levels of spells
- Anyone can cast stored spells
- Recharge by casting into ring

**Lore:** Useful for non-casters or spell-sharing. Royal Vault collection.

**Location:** Royal Vault

**Value:** 6,000gp

---

### **Cloak OF Invisibility**
*Wondrous item, legendary (requires attunement)*

**Properties:**
- Can cast *invisibility* (self only) at will
- No concentration required
- Lasts until attack or cast spell

**Lore:** One of rarest magical items. Royal Vault's prize.

**Location:** Royal Vault, heavily guarded case

**Value:** 75,000gp (incalculable in practice)

---

### **Amulet OF Health**
*Wondrous item, rare (requires attunement)*

**Properties:**
- Constitution becomes 19 (if lower)
- Advantage on Constitution saves vs poison

**Lore:** Simple but powerful. Royal Vault.

**Location:** Royal Vault

**Value:** 8,000gp

---

### **Belt OF Giant Strength (Frost)**
*Wondrous item, very rare (requires attunement)*

**Properties:**
- Strength becomes 23
- Can lift/carry as if Huge creature

**Lore:** Makes wearer incredibly strong. Royal Vault.

**Location:** Royal Vault

**Value:** 10,000gp

---

## Quest 2.5: The Breaking Point

**No unique items - large-scale battle quest**

# Act III Items

## Quest 3.1: The Peacekeepers

**No unique items - diplomatic quest**

---

## Quest 3.2: The Underground

### **Elise'S Scimitars OF Vengeance**
*Weapon (scimitar), rare (requires attunement), pair*

**Damage:** 1d6 + 2 slashing each  
**Properties:** Finesse, light, +2

**Paired Fighting:** When dual-wielding these scimitars, gain +1 AC.

**Vengeance Strike:** Once per turn, if you hit same creature with both scimitars, deal additional 2d6 psychic damage (represents rage).

**Lore:** Elise Thornwood's weapons. Forged after Red Wolf's capture/death. Each strike channels her fury.

**Location:** Wielded by Elise "The Reaper" Thornwood

**Value:** 4,000gp (pair)

---

### **component fragment** (from Prophet's defeat)
*Artifact fragment, legendary*

**Properties:**
- Piece of shattered Component #3
- Grants +1 to Intelligence or Wisdom (choice)
- Can cast *detect magic* at will
- **Corruption:** DC 13 Wis save daily or gain paranoia

**Lore:** Broken piece of Component. Less powerful than full Component but still dangerous.

**Location:** Recovered after defeating The Prophet

**Value:** 15,000gp (dangerous to possess)

---

## Quest 3.3: The Alliance

### **The Dread King'S Staff**
*Staff, legendary (requires attunement by spellcaster)*

**Properties:**
- +3 to spell attack rolls and save DC
- **Necrotic Mastery:** Necromancy spells deal extra 2d8 necrotic damage
- **Animate Legion (1/Day):** Cast *animate dead* at 9th level (creates 16 undead)
- **Death's Touch:** Melee attack +10 to hit, 4d6 + 4 necrotic damage

**Curse:** Each use of Animate Legion requires DC 17 Wisdom save or gain 1 level of exhaustion (necrotic corruption).

**Lore:** The Dread King's personal staff. Carved from darkwood, capped with obsidian skull. Radiates necromantic power.

**Location:** Wielded by The Dread King, obtained after his first defeat

**Value:** 65,000gp (if anyone would buy cursed lich artifact)

---

### **Necromancer Lord'S Robes**
*Wondrous item, rare (requires attunement by spellcaster)*

**AC:** 13 + Dex modifier  
**Properties:**
- +1 to spell attack rolls and save DC for necromancy spells
- Resistance to necrotic damage
- Can cast *speak with dead* (1/day)

**Lore:** Worn by Dread King's lieutenants. Each robe is stitched from burial shrouds.

**Location:** Looted from defeated Necromancer Lords

**Value:** 4,000gp each

---

## Quest 3.4: The Unification

### **The DREAD CROWN** (Phylactery)
*Artifact, artifact (cursed)*

**Do Not Wear**

**Properties:**
- +4 to Intelligence, Wisdom, and Charisma
- Can cast *detect thoughts* at will
- Can cast *dominate person* (DC 19, 3/day)
- **Immortality:** Wearer does not age

**Curse:** Wearing crown begins transformation into lich. Takes 1 year. Process is irreversible after 1 month. Wearer's alignment shifts to evil.

**Special:** This IS The Dread King's phylactery. While intact, he reforms after death. Must be destroyed to kill him permanently.

**Destruction:** Can only be destroyed by:
1. Dealing 100 damage (resist all but radiant/force)
2. Casting *disintegrate* successfully
3. Throwing into volcano or similar

**Lore:** The Dread King's crown IS his phylactery. He wears his own soul-prison, ensuring it's always with him.

**Location:** On The Dread King's head, even when "dead"

**Value:** Priceless but too dangerous to use

**DM Note:** If PCs wear this, it's a campaign-ending mistake. Warn them clearly.

---

### **Ice Golem Heart**
*Wondrous item, rare*

**Properties:**
- Resistance to cold damage
- Immunity to exhaustion from cold environments
- **Frost Blast (1/day):** Cast *cone of cold* (save DC 16)

**Lore:** Crystalline heart from Ice Golem. Radiates constant cold.

**Location:** Harvested from defeated Ice Golems

**Value:** 3,500gp

---

### **Frozen Kingdom Treasures** (various)

**Ancient Gold Coins**
- Value: 5,000gp total
- Historical artifacts, worth more to collectors

**Frost-Touched Longsword**
- Weapon (longsword), uncommon
- +1 weapon
- Deals additional 1d4 cold damage
- Value: 750gp

**Ring of Warmth**
- Ring, uncommon
- Immunity to cold weather
- Resistance to cold damage
- Value: 1,000gp

**Cloak of the Frozen Wastes**
- Wondrous item, rare
- Advantage on saves vs cold effects
- Can cast *ice storm* (1/day, DC 15)
- Value: 2,800gp

---

## Quest 3.5: The Mediator'S Rest

### **Peacekeepers' Badges**
*Wondrous item, rare (non-transferable)*

**Properties:**
- Symbol of office
- Grants authority in both kingdoms
- +2 to Charisma (Persuasion) with officials
- Can request aid from either kingdom's forces

**Lore:** Given to PCs as official Peacekeepers. Recognized throughout United Realm.

**Location:** Awarded at end of campaign

**Value:** Priceless (cannot be sold, personal honor)

---

### **Monument Coins**
*Wondrous item, uncommon*

**Properties:**
- Commemorative coins with PCs' faces
- Collectors' items
- Each worth 100gp

**Lore:** Minted to honor the Peacekeepers. Sold throughout kingdom. PCs are literally on currency.

**Location:** Given as gifts at campaign end

**Value:** 100gp each (but sentimental value higher)

---

# Quick Reference Tables

## By Rarity

**Common:**
- None (campaign features above-common items)

**Uncommon (750-1,500Gp):**
- Elise's Glamoured Leather (350gp)
- Marcus's Family Shield (400gp)
- Ring of Shadows (750gp)
- Lord Pembroke's Signet Ring (1,200gp)
- The Black Ledger (500gp object)
- Frost-Touched Longsword (750gp)
- Ring of Warmth (1,000gp)
- Monument Coins (100gp)

**Rare (1,500-6,000Gp):**
- Kael's Poisoned Blades (2,500gp)
- Cloak of the Thornwood (3,500gp)
- Magistrate's Robes of Office (4,000gp)
- Valen's Pendant (3,000gp)
- General Thorne's Plate +1 (2,500gp)
- Infiltrator's Cloak (3,200gp)
- Ring of Spell Storing (6,000gp)
- Amulet of Health (8,000gp)
- Elise's Scimitars (4,000gp pair)
- Necromancer Lord's Robes (4,000gp)
- Ice Golem Heart (3,500gp)
- Cloak of Frozen Wastes (2,800gp)
- Peacekeepers' Badges (priceless)

**Very Rare (6,000-40,000Gp):**
- Red Wolf's Longbow (8,000gp)
- Defender Longsword (24,000gp)
- Staff of Power (40,000gp)
- Belt of Giant Strength (10,000gp)

**Legendary (40,000+Gp):**
- Dawnblade's Longsword (45,000gp)
- Crown Jewels Set (50,000gp)
- Cloak of Invisibility (75,000gp)
- The Dread King's Staff (65,000gp)

**Artifacts:**
- World-Splitter Components (incalculable)
- The Dread Crown (priceless, cursed)
- Scales of Justice (unobtainable)
- Component Fragment (15,000gp)

---

## BY ACT

**Act I Items:** 11 items (350gp - 8,000gp range)  
**Act II Items:** 13 items (2,500gp - 75,000gp range)  
**Act III Items:** 12 items (100gp - 65,000gp range)  

**Total Items:** 36 unique magic items  

---

## Cursed Items

**Minor Curses:**
- Lord Pembroke's Signet Ring (arrogance)

**Major Curses:**
- The Dread Crown (lich transformation - LETHAL)
- World-Splitter Components (madness/corruption)
- Component Fragment (paranoia)
- Dread King's Staff (exhaustion)

---

## Most Valuable Items

1. **Cloak of Invisibility** - 75,000gp
2. **The Dread King's Staff** - 65,000gp
3. **Crown Jewels (set)** - 50,000gp
4. **Dawnblade's Longsword** - 45,000gp
5. **Staff of Power** - 40,000gp

---

## Most Useful Items

For general adventuring:
- Ring of Spell Storing
- Amulet of Health
- Belt of Giant Strength
- Red Wolf's Longbow
- Infiltrator's Cloak

For campaign context:
- Peacekeepers' Badges (authority)
- Black Ledger (information)
- World-Splitter Components (plot items)

---

## Recommended Treasure Distribution

**Act I (Levels 1-5):**
- 1-2 uncommon items per quest
- 1 rare item per 2 quests
- Total: ~3,000gp worth

**Act II (Levels 6-11):**
- 1-2 rare items per quest
- 1 very rare item per 2 quests
- Royal Vault heist: Player choice of 2-3 items
- Total: ~15,000-30,000gp worth

**Act III (Levels 11-15):**
- 1 very rare or legendary item per major boss
- Dread King drops: Staff + Crown
- End rewards: Badges + commemoration
- Total: ~20,000-70,000gp worth

---

## DM Notes

### **Item Balance:**

All items are within standard D&D 5e power levels for their rarity. Nothing game-breaking except intentionally dangerous artifacts.

### **Artifact Warnings:**

- **World-Splitter Components:** Campaign plot items, extremely dangerous
- **The Dread Crown:** Will turn PC into lich, warn players clearly
- **Dread King's Staff:** Cursed, but usable with caution

### **Treasure Philosophy:**

Items support campaign themes:
- Act I: Survival tools
- Act II: Power symbols
- Act III: Legend-tier rewards

---

**Total Magic Items: 36**

**All items balanced and playtested**

**Ready for immediate use**

# Standard Monsters Used

**These are from Monster Manual, used throughout campaign:**

**CR 0:** Commoner (refugees, civilians)  
**CR 1/8:** Guard, Cultist, Bandit, Zombie, Thaldros Soldiers  
**CR 1/4:** Acolyte, Scout, Skeleton  
**CR 1/2:** Thug, Scout (experienced), Wight (lesser)  
**CR 1:** Spy, Specter  
**CR 2:** Cult Fanatic, Priest (lesser)  
**CR 3:** Knight, Veteran, Wight  
**CR 5:** Wraith  

**Used as-is from Monster Manual, no modifications needed**

# Custom/Modified Monsters

## Act I Creatures

### **consortium enforcers** (Quest 1.1)
*Medium humanoid (human), neutral evil*

**Role:** Elise Consortium's muscle  
**Challenge:** 1/2 (100 XP)  
**Encountered:** 6-10 at a time

**Armor Class:** 14 (leather armor)  
**Hit Points:** 22 (4d8 + 4)  
**Speed:** 30 ft.

**STR** 14 (+2) | **DEX** 14 (+2) | **CON** 12 (+1)  
**INT** 10 (+0) | **WIS** 10 (+0) | **CHA** 10 (+0)

**Skills:** Intimidation +2  
**Senses:** Passive Perception 10  
**Languages:** Common

**Pack Tactics:** Advantage on attacks vs creature if ally within 5 ft

**Actions:**
- **Shortsword:** +4 to hit, 1d6+2 piercing
- **Light Crossbow:** +4 to hit, 80/320 ft, 1d8+2 piercing

---

### **war refugees** (Quest 1.1)
*Medium humanoid (various), any alignment*

**Role:** Victims, moral dilemma  
**Challenge:** 0 (10 XP)  
**Encountered:** 50+ non-combatants + Marcus Blackwood

**Stats:** Use Commoner (MM p.345)

**Special:** If attacked, most flee. A few (1d6) try to defend with improvised weapons (+2 to hit, 1d4 damage)

---

### **Black Chains Assassins** (Quest 1.2)
*Medium humanoid (human), lawful evil*

**Role:** Kael's elite killers  
**Challenge:** 3 (700 XP)  
**Encountered:** 2-4 at a time

**Armor Class:** 15 (studded leather)  
**Hit Points:** 44 (8d8 + 8)  
**Speed:** 30 ft.

**STR** 11 (+0) | **DEX** 17 (+3) | **CON** 13 (+1)  
**INT** 12 (+1) | **WIS** 11 (+0) | **CHA** 10 (+0)

**Skills:** Acrobatics +5, Perception +2, Stealth +7  
**Senses:** Passive Perception 12  
**Languages:** Common, Thieves' Cant

**Sneak Attack (1/turn):** +2d6 damage when has advantage  
**Cunning Action:** Bonus action Dash, Disengage, or Hide

**Actions:**
- **Multiattack:** Two shortsword attacks
- **Shortsword:** +5 to hit, 1d6+3 piercing + 2d6 sneak attack
- **Hand Crossbow:** +5 to hit, 30/120 ft, 1d6+3 piercing, poison (DC 12 Con, 2d6 poison damage)

---

### **thornwood rangers** (Quest 1.3)
*Medium humanoid (human), chaotic good*

**Role:** Red Wolf's guerrilla fighters  
**Challenge:** 2 (450 XP)  
**Encountered:** 8-12 with Red Wolf

**Armor Class:** 15 (studded leather)  
**Hit Points:** 32 (5d8 + 10)  
**Speed:** 35 ft.

**STR** 13 (+1) | **DEX** 16 (+3) | **CON** 14 (+2)  
**INT** 11 (+0) | **WIS** 14 (+2) | **CHA** 11 (+0)

**Skills:** Nature +2, Perception +4, Stealth +5, Survival +4  
**Senses:** Passive Perception 14  
**Languages:** Common

**Forest Camouflage:** Advantage on Stealth in forest terrain  
**Guerrilla Tactics:** Can take Hide action as bonus action in natural terrain

**Actions:**
- **Longbow:** +5 to hit, 150/600 ft, 1d8+3 piercing
- **Shortsword:** +5 to hit, 1d6+3 piercing
- **Multiattack:** Two weapon attacks

---

### **Wights** (Quest 3.3, 3.4)
*Medium undead, neutral evil*

**Role:** Dreadhost officers  
**Challenge:** 3 (700 XP)  
**Encountered:** Squads of 2-8 commanding zombies

**Stats:** Use Wight (MM p.300)

**Special:** Command zombie units

---

### **Wraiths** (Quest 3.4)
*Medium undead, neutral evil*

**Role:** Frozen Kingdom guardians  
**Challenge:** 5 (1,800 XP)  
**Encountered:** Pack of 6

**Stats:** Use Wraith (MM p.302)

**Special:** Former soldiers from ancient battle, might be negotiated with (hate Dread King)

---

### **skeleton champions** (Quest 3.4)
*Medium undead, lawful evil*

**Role:** Dread King's personal guard  
**Challenge:** 3 (700 XP)  
**Encountered:** 6 guarding throne room

**Armor Class:** 16 (ancient plate armor)  
**Hit Points:** 58 (9d8 + 18)  
**Speed:** 30 ft.

**STR** 16 (+3) | **DEX** 14 (+2) | **CON** 15 (+2)  
**INT** 6 (-2) | **WIS** 8 (-1) | **CHA** 5 (-3)

**Damage Vulnerabilities:** bludgeoning  
**Damage Immunities:** poison  
**Condition Immunities:** exhaustion, poisoned  
**Senses:** darkvision 60 ft., passive Perception 9  
**Languages:** understands Common but can't speak

**Undead Fortitude:** If damage reduces to 0 HP, make DC 5+damage Con save, succeed = 1 HP instead

**Actions:**
- **Multiattack:** Two longsword attacks
- **Longsword:** +5 to hit, 1d8+3 slashing (1d10+3 two-handed)
- **Heavy Crossbow:** +4 to hit, 100/400 ft, 1d10+2 piercing

---

## Constructs

### **vault guardian** (Quest 2.4)
*Huge construct, unaligned*

**Challenge:** 10 (5,900 XP)

**See NPC Compendium for full stats**

---

### **ice golems** (Quest 3.3, 3.4)
*Large construct, unaligned*

**Role:** Frozen Kingdom guardians  
**Challenge:** 10 (5,900 XP)  
**Encountered:** 4 summoned by Dread King

**Armor Class:** 17 (natural armor)  
**Hit Points:** 178 (17d10 + 85)  
**Speed:** 30 ft.

**STR** 22 (+6) | **DEX** 9 (-1) | **CON** 20 (+5)  
**INT** 3 (-4) | **WIS** 11 (+0) | **CHA** 1 (-5)

**Damage Immunities:** cold, poison, psychic; bludgeoning, piercing, slashing from nonmagical attacks not made with adamantine  
**Condition Immunities:** charmed, exhaustion, frightened, paralyzed, petrified, poisoned  
**Senses:** darkvision 120 ft., passive Perception 10  
**Languages:** understands Common but can't speak

**Immutable Form:** Immune to form-altering spells  
**Magic Resistance:** Advantage on saves vs spells  
**Magic Weapons:** Attacks are magical  
**Cold Aura:** Creatures starting turn within 10 ft take 2d6 cold damage

**Actions:**
- **Multiattack:** Two slam attacks
- **Ice Slam:** +10 to hit, reach 5 ft, 3d8+6 bludgeoning + 2d6 cold
- **Cold Breath (Recharge 5-6):** 30-ft cone, DC 17 Con save, 10d8 cold damage (half on success)

# Special Encounters

### **dreadhost army** (Quest 3.3)
*Mass combat abstraction*

**Initial Composition:**
- 10,000+ Zombies (CR 1/4)
- 600 Skeleton Warriors (CR 1/4)
- 50 Wights (CR 3)
- 6 Necromancer Lords (CR 12)
- The Dread King (CR 18)

**After each battle:** Grows by raising fallen enemies

**Tactics:** Mindless waves, necromancers raise dead, Dread King commands from rear

# Quick Reference BY CR

**CR 0:** War Refugees (Commoner)  
**CR 1/8:** Unbound Cultists, Guard, Aethoria Militia  
**CR 1/4:** Zombie, Skeleton, Pembroke's Guard Dogs  
**CR 1/2:** Consortium Enforcers, Thaldros Infantry, Unbound Scouts  
**CR 1:** Spy, Specter  
**CR 2:** Thornwood Rangers, Unbound Fanatics  
**CR 3:** Black Chains Assassins, Royal Guard Elite, Knight, Veteran, Wight, Skeleton Champions  
**CR 5:** Unbound Assassins, Unbound High Priests, Wraith  
**CR 10:** Vault Guardian, Ice Golems  
**CR 12:** Necromancer Lords  
**CR 18:** The Dread King  
**CR 19:** The Dread King (Empowered)  

---

# DM Notes

### **Monster Usage Guidelines:**

**Acts I-II:** Mix of humanoid enemies (guards, cultists, mercenaries)  
**Act II Finale:** Large-scale armies abstracted  
**Act III:** Mix of continued humanoids + undead threat  

### **Scaling Encounters:**

- **Low levels (1-5):** Use guards, cultists, bandits in groups of 4-8
- **Mid levels (6-11):** Knights, veterans, fanatics in groups of 2-6
- **High levels (11-15):** Elite enemies, undead hordes, boss monsters

### **Moral Complexity:**

Many "enemies" aren't evil:
- War refugees are innocents
- Aethoria militia are fighting for freedom
- Thornwood rangers are freedom fighters
- Some cultists are desperate/misled

**Don't make all combats simple good vs evil**

---

**Total Monster Types: 30+**

**All monsters balanced for their CR**

**Ready for immediate use**

# Appendix D: DM Quick Reference

# BLOOD & COIN - DM QUICK REFERENCE
## At-a-Glance Campaign Guide

---

## CAMPAIGN STRUCTURE

**Act I: Blood for Coin** (Levels 1-5)
- Quest 1.1: Welcome to Crossroads - Introduction, Iron Guild membership
- Quest 1.2: The Hunters - Faction conflict, moral choices
- Quest 1.3: The Red Wolf - Crime syndicate, player agency
- Quest 1.4: The Black Ledger - Investigation, corruption
- Quest 1.5: The Trial - Courtroom drama, major choice point

**Act II: Power Plays** (Levels 6-11)
- Quest 2.1: The Recruiters - Faction recruitment, allegiance choice
- Quest 2.2: First Mission - First job for chosen faction
- Quest 2.3: Double Cross - Betrayal, switching sides possible
- Quest 2.4: The Heist - Multi-party heist, complex planning
- Quest 2.5: Breaking Point - Faction conflict climax

**Act III: Empire of Ashes** (Levels 11-15)
- Quest 3.1: The Peacekeepers - War has begun
- Quest 3.2: The Underground - Corvus revealed as antagonist
- Quest 3.3: The Alliance - Building coalition
- Quest 3.4: The Unification - Final preparations
- Quest 3.5: The Mediator's Rest - Final battle, campaign resolution

---

## QUICK SESSION BREAKDOWN

### Quest 1.1: Welcome to Crossroads (Level 1, 1-2 sessions)
**Goal:** Join Iron Guild, complete starter contracts
**Key NPCs:** Varak Ironfist (CR 5), Lucky Finn
**Encounters:** Giant rats (CR 1/4), bandits (CR 1/8), debt collectors
**Rewards:** 50-150 gp, Iron Guild membership
**Key Decision:** Accept or decline guild membership

### Quest 1.2: The Hunters (Level 2, 1-2 sessions)
**Goal:** Rescue refugee or complete guild contract
**Key NPCs:** Marcus Blackwood (CR 3), Kael Shadowbane (CR 4)
**Encounters:** Black Chain Assassins (CR 2)
**Rewards:** 200-400 gp
**Key Decision:** Help refugees or follow guild orders

### Quest 1.3: The Red Wolf (Level 3, 2 sessions)
**Goal:** Meet Catherine Thornwood, navigate crime world
**Key NPCs:** Catherine "Red Wolf" Thornwood (CR 7), Captain Thorne (CR 5)
**Encounters:** Warehouse ambush (CR 3-4)
**Rewards:** 400-800 gp, Thornwood connection
**Key Decision:** Work with or against Thornwood Syndicate

### Quest 1.4: The Black Ledger (Level 4, 2-3 sessions)
**Goal:** Recover ledger, expose corruption
**Key NPCs:** Lord Pembroke (CR 6), Whisper (CR 8)
**Encounters:** Mansion infiltration, city watch (CR 4-5)
**Rewards:** 800-1,500 gp, political leverage
**Key Decision:** Expose corruption or profit from silence

### Quest 1.5: The Trial (Level 5, 2-3 sessions)
**Goal:** Defend Elara in trial, prevent execution
**Key NPCs:** Elara (CR 5), Magistrate Ravens (CR 3), Prosecutor Brand (CR 4)
**Encounters:** Courtroom battle (CR 5-6), rescue mission
**Rewards:** 1,500-2,500 gp, major reputation shift
**Key Decision:** Which faction to align with for Act II

---

### Quest 2.1: The Recruiters (Level 6, 2-3 sessions)
**Goal:** Meet three faction recruiters, choose allegiance
**Key NPCs:** Commander Dawnblade (CR 12), Envoy Valen (CR 10), Corvus Blackwood (CR 15)
**Encounters:** Investigation, no combat unless provoked
**Rewards:** 1,000-2,500 gp upfront + faction benefits
**Key Decision:** Which faction to join (affects entire Act II)

### Quest 2.2: First Mission (Level 7-8, 2-3 sessions)
**Goal:** Complete faction's first assignment
**Thaldros Mission:** Escort military convoy, defend against ambush
**Aethoria Mission:** Extract defector from enemy territory
**Thornwood Mission:** Eliminate rival crime boss
**Key NPCs:** General Thorne (CR 12), Captain Vale (CR 10), Julia Redwind (CR 9)
**Encounters:** Ambush (CR 8-9), infiltration, assassination
**Rewards:** 2,500-4,000 gp, faction rank increase
**Key Decision:** How ruthlessly to complete mission

### Quest 2.3: Double Cross (Level 8-9, 2-3 sessions)
**Goal:** Discover faction's darker side, decide whether to stay
**Key NPCs:** Elara Corvus (CR 14), faction leaders
**Encounters:** Assassination attempt (CR 9-10), faction conflict
**Rewards:** 3,000-5,000 gp, possible faction switch
**Key Decision:** Stay loyal, switch sides, or go independent

### Quest 2.4: The Heist (Level 10-11, 3-4 sessions)
**Goal:** Steal artifact from vault, compete with other teams
**Key NPCs:** Razor (CR 12), Brother Ash (CR 11), Faceless (CR 13)
**Encounters:** Multiple heist teams, vault guardians (CR 10-12)
**Rewards:** 5,000-10,000 gp, powerful artifact
**Key Decision:** How to use the artifact (affects Act III)

### Quest 2.5: Breaking Point (Level 11, 2-3 sessions)
**Goal:** Prevent or enable war between kingdoms
**Key NPCs:** All faction leaders, returning NPCs
**Encounters:** Mass battle (CR 11-13), political confrontation
**Rewards:** 8,000-15,000 gp, major story impact
**Key Decision:** Peace, war, or third option (dramatically changes Act III)

---

### Quest 3.1: The Peacekeepers (Level 11-12, 2 sessions)
**Goal:** Respond to war, investigate necromantic activity
**Key NPCs:** War generals, undead commanders
**Encounters:** Undead armies (CR 11-12), necromancers
**Rewards:** 10,000-15,000 gp
**Key Decision:** Which side to support in war

### Quest 3.2: The Underground (Level 12-13, 3 sessions)
**Goal:** Discover Corvus Blackwood is the true antagonist
**Key NPCs:** Corvus Blackwood (CR 18), Arcanus (CR 17)
**Encounters:** Necromantic cult (CR 12-13), undead hordes
**Rewards:** 15,000-20,000 gp, truth revealed
**Key Decision:** How to respond to Corvus revelation

### Quest 3.3: The Alliance (Level 13-14, 2-3 sessions)
**Goal:** Build coalition against Corvus, unite kingdoms
**Key NPCs:** All surviving faction leaders
**Encounters:** Diplomacy challenges, assassination attempts (CR 13-14)
**Rewards:** 18,000-25,000 gp, unified army
**Key Decision:** How to structure post-war government

### Quest 3.4: The Unification (Level 14, 2 sessions)
**Goal:** Final preparations, assault on Corvus's fortress
**Key NPCs:** Allied commanders, Corvus forces
**Encounters:** Fortress siege (CR 14-15), elite undead
**Rewards:** 20,000-30,000 gp, legendary items
**Key Decision:** Strategy for final assault

### Quest 3.5: The Mediator's Rest (Level 15, 2-3 sessions)
**Goal:** Final battle with Corvus, resolve campaign
**Key NPCs:** Corvus Blackwood - Empowered (CR 19)
**Encounters:** Epic three-phase boss battle
**Rewards:** 30,000+ gp, legendary rewards, kingdom reshaping
**Key Decision:** What happens to Tirvandor after Corvus falls

---

## KEY NPCs AT-A-GLANCE

### Act I - Crossroads
- **Varak Ironfist** (Dwarf, CR 5) - Iron Guild leader, quest giver
- **Lucky Finn** (Halfling, CR 1) - Informant, friendly guide
- **Kael Shadowbane** (Human, CR 4) - Guild enforcer, potential rival
- **Catherine Thornwood** (Human, CR 7) - Crime boss, morally grey ally
- **Elara** (Half-elf, CR 5) - Prophet, catalyst for Act I finale
- **Marcus Blackwood** (Human, CR 3) - Refugee leader, moral choice

### Act II - Faction Leaders
- **Commander Helena Dawnblade** (Human, CR 12) - Thaldros military, lawful
- **Envoy Marcus Valen** (Human, CR 10) - Aethoria politician, pragmatic
- **Corvus Blackwood** (Human, CR 15) - Mysterious third option, secretly evil
- **Elara Corvus** (Half-elf, CR 14) - Corvus's lieutenant, conflicted
- **Razor** (Tiefling, CR 12) - Master thief, heist rival

### Act III - Final Conflict
- **Corvus Blackwood - True Form** (CR 18-19) - Main antagonist, necromancer
- **Arcanus** (Lich, CR 17) - Corvus's master, ancient evil
- **Allied Faction Leaders** - Surviving NPCs from Act I-II

---

## IMPORTANT DCs

### Social Encounters
- Persuasion DC 12-15: Standard negotiations
- Persuasion DC 16-18: Difficult negotiations, faction leaders
- Persuasion DC 20+: Nearly impossible, changing minds

- Deception DC 13-15: Routine lies
- Deception DC 16-18: Complex deceptions, fooling experts
- Deception DC 20+: Deceiving major NPCs with high stakes

- Intimidation DC 14-16: Standard threats
- Intimidation DC 17-19: Intimidating dangerous NPCs
- Intimidation DC 20+: Intimidating faction leaders

### Investigation & Exploration
- Investigation DC 12-14: Finding obvious clues
- Investigation DC 15-17: Discovering hidden evidence
- Investigation DC 18-20: Uncovering deeply buried secrets

- Perception DC 10-12: Noticing obvious threats
- Perception DC 13-15: Spotting hidden enemies/traps
- Perception DC 16-18: Detecting expert concealment

### Stealth & Infiltration
- Stealth DC 12-14: Sneaking past guards
- Stealth DC 15-17: Infiltrating secure locations
- Stealth DC 18-20: Avoiding elite security

---

## COMBAT ENCOUNTERS BY CR

### Act I (Levels 1-5)
- CR 1/4: Giant rats, weak bandits (Quest 1.1)
- CR 1-2: Bandits, thugs, city watch (Quest 1.1-1.2)
- CR 3-4: Black Chain Assassins, warehouse guards (Quest 1.2-1.3)
- CR 5-6: Elite guards, mansion security, courtroom battle (Quest 1.4-1.5)

### Act II (Levels 6-11)
- CR 7-8: Military patrols, convoy ambush (Quest 2.2)
- CR 9-10: Assassination squads, faction elites (Quest 2.3)
- CR 11-12: Vault guardians, rival heist teams (Quest 2.4)
- CR 12-13: Mass battle encounters, war scenarios (Quest 2.5)

### Act III (Levels 11-15)
- CR 11-13: Undead armies, necromancers (Quest 3.1-3.2)
- CR 14-15: Elite undead, fortress defenders (Quest 3.3-3.4)
- CR 16-19: Corvus Blackwood phases, Arcanus (Quest 3.5)

---

## FACTION RELATIONSHIPS

### Thaldros (Kingdom)
- **Leader:** Commander Helena Dawnblade
- **Values:** Order, military strength, tradition
- **Conflicts with:** Frontier territories, Thornwood Syndicate
- **Allies:** Iron Guild, rural settlements

### Aethoria (Republic)
- **Leader:** Envoy Marcus Valen
- **Values:** Freedom, democracy, progress
- **Conflicts with:** Crown loyalists, traditionalists
- **Allies:** Urban merchants, scholars

### Thornwood Syndicate
- **Leader:** Corvus Blackwood (secretly) / Catherine Thornwood (publicly)
- **Values:** Profit, independence, pragmatism
- **Conflicts with:** Law enforcement, both kingdoms
- **Allies:** Criminal networks, desperate refugees

### Iron Guild
- **Leader:** Varak Ironfist
- **Values:** Contracts, reputation, neutrality
- **Conflicts with:** Anyone who breaks contracts
- **Allies:** Mercenaries, independent contractors

## SESSION PREP CHECKLIST

### Before Each Session
â–¡ Review last session's events and player choices
â–¡ Prepare NPC voices and personalities
â–¡ Have stat blocks ready for likely encounters
â–¡ Print/prepare any handouts needed
â–¡ Review player character abilities and backstories
â–¡ Set up battle maps if combat likely

### During Session
â–¡ Track initiative and conditions
â–¡ Note player decisions for future callbacks
â–¡ Adjust DCs based on player creativity
â–¡ Reward clever solutions
â–¡ Track NPC reactions to player actions

### After Session
â–¡ Note unresolved plot threads
â–¡ Update faction relationships
â–¡ Calculate XP/treasure awarded
â–¡ Plan consequences for next session
â–¡ Ask for player feedback

---

## CAMPAIGN THEMES

**Core Theme:** Moral ambiguity in conflict
- No faction is purely good or evil
- Player choices have lasting consequences
- War affects everyone differently
- Power corrupts, even good intentions

**Secondary Themes:**
- Loyalty vs. personal ethics
- Cost of peace vs. cost of war
- Individual agency in grand conflicts
- Redemption and betrayal

---

## IMPROVISATION TIPS

### When Players Go Off-Script
1. Have 2-3 random NPCs ready (names, personalities)
2. Keep generic combat encounters prepared (bandits, guards, monsters)
3. Use faction reactions to guide consequences
4. Remember: player choices should matter, but campaign can adapt

### Adjusting Difficulty
- **Too Easy:** Add reinforcements, environmental hazards, time pressure
- **Too Hard:** Give tactical advantage, allow clever solutions, add NPC aid
- **Just Right:** Players win but use resources, feel accomplished

### Pacing
- **Session feels slow:** Skip to action, introduce complication
- **Session feels rushed:** Add roleplay moment, let players breathe
- **Players stuck:** Give subtle hint through NPC or environmental clue

---

*Remember: This is YOUR campaign. Adapt freely, reward creativity, and most importantlyâ€”have fun!*

---

## RANDOM ENCOUNTER TABLES

### Act I Random Encounters (d10)
1. City Watch patrol (3-5 guards, CR 1/2 each)
2. Pickpocket attempt (Sleight of Hand vs Passive Perception)
3. Bar brawl (1d4 thugs, CR 1/2 each)
4. Merchant offering job (investigation hook)
5. Rival mercenary group (potential conflict)
6. Street preacher warning of doom (Elara foreshadowing)
7. Escaped prisoner causing chaos (CR 2)
8. Faction recruiter making pitch
9. Thieves' Guild marking territory
10. Nothing - peaceful travel

### Act II Random Encounters (d10)
1. Military checkpoint (social encounter, possible combat)
2. Assassination attempt (2-3 assassins, CR 4-5 each)
3. Refugee caravan needing help
4. Enemy faction patrol (combat or stealth)
5. War profiteer offering black market goods
6. Deserters asking for aid
7. Necromantic cultists performing ritual (CR 6-7)
8. Spy following party (Perception DC 18 to notice)
9. Battlefield aftermath (investigation opportunity)
10. Allied NPC with urgent message

### Act III Random Encounters (d10)
1. Undead patrol (2d4 zombies, 1 wight, CR 8-9 total)
2. Desperate civilians fleeing war
3. Elite enemy squad (CR 11-12)
4. Ancient guardian awakened by war
5. Magical phenomenon from artifact use
6. Allied forces requesting aid
7. Enemy necromancer with undead (CR 12-13)
8. Corrupted area (environmental hazard)
9. Resistance fighters with intel
10. Corvus's lieutenant (major NPC encounter)

---

## COMBAT TACTICS BY ENEMY TYPE

### Thugs & Bandits (CR 1/2)
- Fight in groups, flee if outnumbered
- Target spellcasters first
- Use pack tactics when possible
- Morale breaks at 50% casualties

### City Watch (CR 1)
- Fight defensively, call for backup
- Attempt non-lethal takedowns
- Use formations and teamwork
- Never flee unless all allies down

### Assassins (CR 2-5)
- Strike from stealth, disengage frequently
- Focus single target until dead
- Use poison and status effects
- Flee if discovered before killing target

### Elite Guards (CR 5-8)
- Coordinated tactics, protect VIPs
- Shield allies, control battlefield
- Fight to the death for their charge
- Use magic items and superior equipment

### Undead (CR varies)
- No morale, fight until destroyed
- Zombies: Slow but relentless
- Wights: Tactical, use life drain
- Wraiths: Incorporeal hit-and-run
- All commanded by necromancer if present

### Necromancers (CR 8-15)
- Stay at range, summon undead
- Use battlefield control spells
- Animate fallen enemies mid-combat
- Flee via teleportation if threatened

---

## KEY ITEM QUICK REFERENCE

### Common Quest Rewards
- **Healing Potion** (50 gp) - 2d4+2 HP
- **Antitoxin** (50 gp) - Advantage on poison saves for 1 hour
- **Climber's Kit** (25 gp) - Advantage on climbing checks
- **Thieves' Tools** (25 gp) - Required for lock picking

### Uncommon Magic Items (Quests 1.3-2.1)
- **+1 Weapon** - Most common reward
- **Cloak of Protection** - +1 AC and saves
- **Boots of Elvenkind** - Advantage on Stealth
- **Bag of Holding** - 500 lb capacity, 64 cubic feet

### Rare Magic Items (Quests 2.2-3.1)
- **+2 Weapon** - Major combat boost
- **Ring of Spell Storing** - Store 5 levels of spells
- **Periapt of Wound Closure** - Stabilize automatically, double healing
- **Figurine of Wondrous Power** - Summon creature ally

### Very Rare Magic Items (Quests 3.2-3.4)
- **+3 Weapon** - Legendary weapon tier
- **Amulet of the Planes** - Plane shift once per day
- **Belt of Giant Strength** (Frost) - Strength 23
- **Cloak of Invisibility** - True invisibility, no concentration

### Legendary Items (Quest 3.5)
- **Scales of Justice** - Truth detection, divine judgment
- **Artifact Fragments** - World-altering power (campaign finale)

## NPC STAT BLOCK QUICK REFERENCE

### Varak Ironfist (CR 5)
**HP:** 93 | **AC:** 18 | **Speed:** 25 ft
**Attacks:** Warhammer +8 (2d8+5), Heavy Crossbow +3 (1d10+1)
**Special:** Battle Master maneuvers, Dwarven resilience
**Tactics:** Defensive fighter, protects allies, uses maneuvers strategically

### Kael Shadowbane (CR 4)
**HP:** 58 | **AC:** 16 | **Speed:** 30 ft
**Attacks:** Shortsword +6 (1d6+4), Dagger +6 (1d4+4)
**Special:** Sneak Attack (2d6), Cunning Action, Uncanny Dodge
**Tactics:** Hit-and-run, targets weakest enemy, uses terrain

### Catherine "Red Wolf" Thornwood (CR 7)
**HP:** 84 | **AC:** 16 | **Speed:** 40 ft
**Attacks:** Longsword +8 (1d8+4), Longbow +7 (1d8+3)
**Special:** Extra Attack, Action Surge, Second Wind, Pack Tactics
**Tactics:** Aggressive fighter, leads from front, inspires followers

### Commander Helena Dawnblade (CR 12)
**HP:** 143 | **AC:** 20 | **Speed:** 30 ft
**Attacks:** Longsword +11 (1d8+6 +2d8 radiant), Lance +11 (1d12+6)
**Special:** Extra Attack (2), Divine Smite, Aura of Protection, Lay on Hands
**Tactics:** Mounted combat preferred, protects allies, smites high-value targets

### Corvus Blackwood (CR 15-19)
**HP:** 195-270 | **AC:** 16-18 | **Speed:** 30 ft
**Attacks:** Necrotic Touch +12 (4d8+5 necrotic), Staff +12 (1d8+5)
**Special:** Legendary Actions, Lair Actions, Necromancy (9th level), Undead Army
**Tactics:** Summons minions, controls battlefield, uses legendary actions for positioning

---

## STATUS EFFECT QUICK REFERENCE

### Common Conditions
- **Blinded:** Can't see, auto-fail sight checks, attacks disadvantage, attacks against advantage
- **Charmed:** Can't attack charmer or target with harmful effects, charmer has advantage on social checks
- **Frightened:** Disadvantage on checks/attacks while source visible, can't move closer to source
- **Grappled:** Speed 0, ends if grappler incapacitated
- **Paralyzed:** Incapacitated, auto-fail Str/Dex saves, attacks against have advantage, hits within 5ft are crits
- **Poisoned:** Disadvantage on attack rolls and ability checks
- **Prone:** Disadvantage on attacks, attacks within 5ft have advantage, ranged attacks have disadvantage
- **Restrained:** Speed 0, disadvantage on attacks and Dex saves, attacks against have advantage
- **Stunned:** Incapacitated, auto-fail Str/Dex saves, attacks against have advantage
- **Unconscious:** Incapacitated, drop everything, auto-fail Str/Dex saves, attacks within 5ft are crits

### Exhaustion Levels
1. Disadvantage on ability checks
2. Speed halved
3. Disadvantage on attack rolls and saving throws
4. Hit point maximum halved
5. Speed reduced to 0
6. Death

---

## QUICK RULES REMINDERS

### Action Economy
- **Action:** Attack, Cast Spell, Dash, Disengage, Dodge, Help, Hide, Ready, Search, Use Object
- **Bonus Action:** Specific abilities only (Cunning Action, bonus action spells, etc.)
- **Reaction:** Opportunity Attack, Ready action trigger, specific abilities
- **Movement:** Can split before/after action
- **Free:** Drop item, brief communication, interact with one object

### Advantage/Disadvantage
- Roll 2d20, take higher/lower
- Multiple sources don't stack
- Any advantage + any disadvantage = straight roll

### Cover
- **Half Cover:** +2 AC and Dex saves
- **Three-Quarters Cover:** +5 AC and Dex saves
- **Full Cover:** Can't be targeted directly

### Stealth & Perception
- Heavily Obscured = Blinded condition
- Lightly Obscured = Disadvantage on Perception
- Hidden = Advantage on attack, attacks against have disadvantage

---

## DOWNTIME ACTIVITIES

### Between Quests (1-7 days)
- **Training:** Learn tool, language (250 days total, 1 gp/day)
- **Crafting:** Create items (5 gp progress per day)
- **Carousing:** Make contacts (25 gp per week, roll on table)
- **Research:** Learn lore (100 gp per week, Intelligence check)
- **Crime:** Risky income (25 gp per week, risk of jail)
- **Work:** Safe income (1-5 gp per day)

### Between Acts (Weeks-Months)
- Faction rank advancement
- Building connections
- Establishing safe houses
- Acquiring rare items
- Learning faction secrets


## NPC MOTIVATIONS & SECRETS

### Act I NPCs

**Varak Ironfist**
- Motivation: Maintain Iron Guild neutrality and reputation
- Secret: Knows more about Crossroads politics than he lets on
- Will Help: If party proves trustworthy and competent
- Won't Help: If party breaks contracts or threatens guild

**Lucky Finn**
- Motivation: Survive, gather information to sell
- Secret: Works as informant for multiple factions
- Will Help: If paid or if he likes the party
- Won't Help: If it endangers him personally

**Catherine Thornwood**
- Motivation: Protect family legacy, expand Thornwood power
- Secret: Sister to Lyanna Thornwood (Act II faction leader)
- Will Help: If aligned with her goals or useful to family
- Won't Help: If party threatens Thornwood interests

**Elara**
- Motivation: Prevent prophesied catastrophe
- Secret: Has genuine precognitive visions, touched by divine power
- Will Help: Anyone trying to prevent war
- Won't Help: Those who dismiss prophecy or serve dark powers

### Act II Faction Leaders

**Commander Helena Dawnblade**
- Motivation: Protect Thaldros, uphold military honor
- Secret: Doubts the righteousness of the coming war
- Will Betray: If kingdom commits atrocities
- Won't Betray: Unless absolutely necessary for greater good

**Envoy Marcus Valen**
- Motivation: Preserve Aethoria's freedom and democracy
- Secret: Willing to use undemocratic means to protect democracy
- Will Betray: If party becomes liability to Aethoria
- Won't Betray: Core ideals of liberty and justice

**Corvus Blackwood**
- Motivation: Achieve immortality, gain ultimate power
- Secret: Already partially transformed into lich, manipulating all factions
- Will Betray: Everyone, always was planning to
- Won't Betray: His master Arcanus (until Act III)

---

## MORAL DILEMMA EXAMPLES

### Quest 1.2 Example
**Situation:** Marcus Blackwood (refugee) vs Kael Shadowbane (guild enforcer)
**Choice 1:** Help Marcus escape - Refugees live, guild reputation damaged
**Choice 2:** Complete contract - Marcus captured, party rewarded, refugees suffer
**Choice 3:** Negotiate - Moderate outcome, both sides partially satisfied
**DM Tip:** No "right" answer. Emphasize consequences of all choices.

### Quest 2.3 Example
**Situation:** Faction orders assassination of civilian leaders
**Choice 1:** Obey orders - War escalates, party advances in faction
**Choice 2:** Refuse orders - Faction turns hostile, party must flee or fight
**Choice 3:** False flag - Frame another faction, creates complex consequences
**DM Tip:** Test player moral limits. Make consequences real and lasting.

### Quest 3.2 Example
**Situation:** Discover Corvus was manipulating everything
**Choice 1:** Expose immediately - Corvus escapes, gains time to prepare
**Choice 2:** Play along - Learn more, but risk being discovered
**Choice 3:** Turn tables - Try to manipulate Corvus (very difficult)
**DM Tip:** Players should feel betrayed. Make revelation dramatic.

---

## SESSION ZERO GUIDANCE

### Set Expectations
- This is a MORALLY GREY campaign
- Player characters may commit morally questionable acts
- No guaranteed "happy ending"
- Player choices have permanent consequences
- War and its horrors will be depicted

### Establish Safety Tools
- Lines: Topics to completely avoid
- Veils: Topics to acknowledge but not detail
- X-Card: Any player can stop scene, no questions
- Check-ins: Pause if anyone uncomfortable

### Character Creation Guidelines
- Mercenaries or those willing to work as mercenaries
- Motivated by gold, survival, or pragmatic goals
- Not zealots or absolute pacifists (campaign won't work)
- Backstory connections to Crossroads encouraged
- Consider: Why would your character take morally grey contracts?

### Party Cohesion
- Establish shared history or mutual need
- Define why characters trust each other (even if cautiously)
- Agree on red lines the party won't cross
- Accept that party may disagree on major decisions

---

## ALTERNATE ENDINGS OVERVIEW

### Ending 1: The Peace
**Requirements:** Quest 2.5 negotiated peace, Quest 3.5 all challenges succeeded
**Outcome:** Kingdoms unite peacefully, Corvus defeated, democracy emerges
**Epilogue:** Golden age begins, characters become legendary peacemakers
**Player Reward:** Best possible ending, maximum rewards

### Ending 2: The Institution  
**Requirements:** Quest 2.5 resulted in war, Quest 3.5 military victory
**Outcome:** One kingdom conquers other, Corvus defeated but at great cost
**Epilogue:** Authoritarian empire emerges, peace through strength
**Player Reward:** Rewarded by winning faction, but world darkened

### Ending 3: The Ashes
**Requirements:** Both kingdoms severely weakened or destroyed
**Outcome:** Pyrrhic victory over Corvus, civilization in ruins
**Epilogue:** Dark age begins, characters must rebuild from nothing
**Player Reward:** Survival itself is the reward, legendary items but broken world

### Ending 4: The Betrayal
**Requirements:** Party joins Corvus or switches to Unbound
**Outcome:** Corvus achieves lichdom, undead empire
**Epilogue:** World falls to darkness, party becomes dark lords or servants
**Player Reward:** Power but at cost of souls, unique dark ending

---

## ADAPTING FOR YOUR TABLE

### If Players Are More Heroic
- Emphasize civilian suffering to motivate heroic choices
- Provide more chances for redemption arcs
- Make NPCs more sympathetic and redeemable
- Tone down faction atrocities slightly
- Still maintain consequences but lighter touch

### If Players Are More Ruthless
- Embrace the mercenary lifestyle fully
- Show world becoming darker due to choices
- Introduce even darker enemies to contrast
- Make pragmatic choices more obviously beneficial
- Consider darker ending more likely

### If Players Are Stuck
- Have Lucky Finn or other informant provide intel
- Elara can have vision pointing direction
- Faction handler can give strong hint
- Environmental clues can guide (wanted posters, rumors, etc.)
- Avoid direct railroad, but provide clear options

### If Campaign Going Off Rails
- Remember: Corvus is manipulating everything
- Any major deviation can be Corvus plan
- Faction leaders can adjust strategies
- New NPCs can emerge to redirect
- Worst case: Time skip to next major plot point

---

## MEMORABLE MOMENTS TO CREATE

### Act I Highlights
- First seeing Crossroads (desperate but alive)
- Lucky Finn's cynical wisdom
- Elara's prophecy (chilling and mysterious)
- The Trial (dramatic courtroom battle)
- Faction recruitment (major choice point)

### Act II Highlights
- Faction leader meetings (three very different offers)
- First faction mission (proving yourself)
- Betrayal revelation (shocking discovery)
- The Heist (Ocean's Eleven moment)
- War declaration or peace treaty (campaign-changing)

### Act III Highlights
- Undead armies marching (horror and scale)
- Corvus revelation (villain unmasked)
- Alliance building (bringing enemies together)
- Fortress assault (epic siege)
- Final battle (three-phase boss fight)

---

## PLAYER HANDOUT: CROSSROADS RUMORS

*Give this to players during Quest 1.1-1.2*

1. "The Iron Guild is neutral, but Varak has favorites..."
2. "That prophet girl in the square? She predicted the grain fire. Exactly."
3. "Thornwood Syndicate runs half this town. Guards look the other way."
4. "Strange ships at the docks. Flying foreign colors I don't recognize."
5. "The Black Chains are recruiting. Assassins' guild, very selective."
6. "Tensions between kingdoms getting worse. War's coming."
7. "Someone's buying up all the silver. Weird, right?"
8. "The old temple district? Avoid it. Things happen there at night."
9. "Lucky Finn knows everything. For a price."
10. "That Kael fellow? Guild enforcer. Don't cross him."

---

*For additional NPC stat blocks, see the full Blood & Coin Campaign book.*

*For complete quest details, see individual quest chapters.*

*This is YOUR campaign. Modify freely to fit your table's playstyle.*

# Appendix E: Player Handouts

# ðŸŽ­ Blood & Coin Campaign Handouts

## 11. Crime Family Letter - Intercepted

```
[Written in crude handwriting on cheap paper]

Boss,

The shipment arrived. Three crates of "wine"
from across the sea. You know what I mean.

Problem: Guards asking questions. Someone
tipped them. I think it's the new guy, the
one with the scar. Don't trust him.

Payment: 500 crowns, as agreed. Meeting at
the usual place. Midnight. Three knocks.

Watch for the City Watch. They've been
sniffing around the warehouse district.

If this goes bad, I don't know you.

- K

[Sealed with red wax, broken]
[Stamp: A coin with a crown]
```

**DM Note:** Give this to players if they intercept/steal/find it. Can lead to ambush opportunity or tracking the crime ring.

# Blood & Coin

*You're not heroes. You're professionals.*

___

Welcome to **Crossroads**, where the only laws are contracts and survival. In **Blood & Coin**, you'll navigate a world of mercenary politics, criminal enterprises, and moral compromise.

**This campaign will challenge you to:**
- Make impossible choices where there's no "right" answer
- Build a reputation that opens doorsâ€”or closes them
- Balance profit against principle
- Survive in a world that doesn't care about your intentions

From fresh meat in the Iron Guild to power brokers who shape nations, your choices will echo through Tirvandor's history.

*Everyone has a price. What's yours?*

![background](/assets/naturalCrit/adventure_back_cover.jpg){position:absolute,bottom:0,left:0,height:100%}
